22static void leabra_converter_init() {
23 DumpFileCvt* cvt = new DumpFileCvt("Leabra", "LeabraUnit");
24 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("_MGroup", "_Group"));
25 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("Project", "V3LeabraProject"));
26 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("V3LeabraProject_Group", "Project_Group")); // fix prev
27 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("V3LeabraProjection", "LeabraPrjn")); // new prjn type!
28 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("LeabraPrjn_Group", "Projection_Group"));
29 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("Network", "LeabraNetwork"));
30 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("LeabraNetwork_Group", "Network_Group")); // fix prev
31 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("LeabraWiz", "LeabraWizard"));
32 // obsolete types get replaced with taBase..
33 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("WinView_Group", "taBase_Group"));
34 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("ProjViewState_List", "taBase_List"));
35 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("NetView", "taNBase"));
36 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("DataTable", "taNBase"));
37 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("EnviroView", "taNBase"));
38 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("Xform", "taBase"));
39 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("ImageEnv", "ScriptEnv"));
40 cvt->repl_strs.Add(NameVar("unique/w=", "unique"));
41 taMisc::file_converters.Add(cvt);
42}

44void leabra_module_init() {

46 leabra_converter_init(); // configure converter
47}

66
67float WtScaleSpec::SLayActScale(float savg, float lay_sz, float n_cons) {
68 int slay_act_n = (int)(savg * lay_sz + .5f); // sending layer actual # active
69 slay_act_n = MAX(slay_act_n, 1)(((slay_act_n) > (1)) ? (slay_act_n) : (1));
70 float rval = 1.0f;
71 if(n_cons == lay_sz) {
72 rval = 1.0f / (float)slay_act_n;
73 }
74 else {
75 int r_max_act_n = MIN((int)n_cons, slay_act_n)((((int)n_cons) < (slay_act_n)) ? ((int)n_cons) : (slay_act_n
)); // max number we could get
76 int r_avg_act_n = (int)(savg * n_cons + .5f);// recv average actual # active if uniform
77 r_avg_act_n = MAX(r_avg_act_n, 1)(((r_avg_act_n) > (1)) ? (r_avg_act_n) : (1));
78 int r_exp_act_n = r_avg_act_n + sem_extra;
79 r_exp_act_n = MIN(r_exp_act_n, r_max_act_n)(((r_exp_act_n) < (r_max_act_n)) ? (r_exp_act_n) : (r_max_act_n
));
80 rval = 1.0f / (float)r_exp_act_n;
81 }
82 return rval;
83}

119void XCalLearnSpec::Initialize() {
120 thr_l_mix = 0.01f;
121 s_mix = 0.9f;
122 d_rev = 0.10f;
123 d_thr = 0.0001f;
124 m_mix = 1.0f - s_mix;
125 thr_m_mix = 1.0f - thr_l_mix;
126 d_rev_ratio = -(1.0f - d_rev) / d_rev;
127}
128
129void XCalLearnSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
130 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
131 m_mix = 1.0f - s_mix;
132 thr_m_mix = 1.0f - thr_l_mix;
133 d_rev_ratio = (1.0f - d_rev) / d_rev;
134 if(d_rev > 0.0f)
135 d_rev_ratio = -(1.0f - d_rev) / d_rev;
136 else
137 d_rev_ratio = -1.0f;
138 if(owner) owner->UpdateAfterEdit(); // update our conspec so it can recompute lookup function!
139}

152void AdaptRelNetinSpec::Defaults_init() {
153 trg_fm_input = .85f;
154 trg_fm_output = .15f;
155 trg_lateral = 0.0f;
156 trg_sum = 1.0f;
157 tol_lg = 0.05f;
158 tol_sm = 0.2f;
159 rel_lrate = .2f;
160}
161
162void AdaptRelNetinSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
163 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
164 trg_sum = trg_fm_input + trg_fm_output + trg_lateral;
165 TestWarning(fabsf(trg_sum - 1.0f) > .01, "UAE", "target values do not sum to 1");
166}
167
168bool AdaptRelNetinSpec::CheckInTolerance(float trg, float val) {
169 float tol;
170 if(trg > .25f)
171 tol = tol_lg * trg;
172 else
173 tol = tol_sm * trg;
174 if(fabsf(trg - val) <= tol) return true;
175 return false;
176}

179void LeabraConSpec::Initialize() {
180 min_obj_type = &TA_LeabraCon;
181 learn_rule = LEABRA_CHL;
182 inhib = false;
183
184 learn = true;
185
186 wt_sig_fun.x_range.min = 0.0f;
187 wt_sig_fun.x_range.max = 1.0f;
188 wt_sig_fun.res = 1.0e-5f; // 1e-6 = 1.9Mb & 33% slower!, but 4x more accurate; 1e-5 = .19Mb
189 wt_sig_fun.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
190
191 wt_sig_fun_inv.x_range.min = 0.0f;
192 wt_sig_fun_inv.x_range.max = 1.0f;
193 wt_sig_fun_inv.res = 1.0e-5f; // 1e-6 = 1.9Mb & 33% slower!, but 4x more accurate; 1e-5 = .19Mb
194 wt_sig_fun_inv.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
195
196 wt_sig_fun_lst.off = -1.0f; wt_sig_fun_lst.gain = -1.0f; // trigger an update
197 wt_sig_fun_res = -1.0f;
198
199 lrs_value = EPOCH;
200 lrate_sched.interpolate = false;
201
202 Defaults_init();
203}

217void LeabraConSpec::InitLinks() {
218 inherited::InitLinks();
219 InitLinks_taAuto(&TA_LeabraConSpec);
220 children.SetBaseType(&TA_LeabraConSpec);
221 children.el_typ = GetTypeDef(); // but make the default to be me!
222 CreateWtSigFun();
223 if(taMisc::is_loading || taMisc::is_duplicating) return;
224 LeabraNetwork* mynet = GET_MY_OWNER(LeabraNetwork)(LeabraNetwork *) GetOwner(&TA_LeabraNetwork);
225 if(mynet) {
226 SetLearnRule(mynet); // get current learning rule.
227 }
228}
229
230void LeabraConSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
231 if(HasBaseFlag(BF_MISC2)) return; // flag used for marking UAE
232 SetBaseFlag(BF_MISC2); // now in it, mark..
233
234 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
235 lrate_sched.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
236 lmix.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
237 xcal.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui(); // this calls owner
238 rel_net_adapt.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
239 CreateWtSigFun();
240 LeabraNetwork* mynet = GET_MY_OWNER(LeabraNetwork)(LeabraNetwork *) GetOwner(&TA_LeabraNetwork);
241 if(mynet) {
242 SetLearnRule(mynet); // get current learning rule, just in case..
243 if(wt_sig.dwt_norm && !mynet->dwt_norm_enabled) {
244 mynet->dwt_norm_enabled = true; // don't have a way of turning this off..
245 }
246 }
247
248 ClearBaseFlag(BF_MISC2); // done..
249}
250
251bool LeabraConSpec::CheckConfig_RecvCons(RecvCons* cg, bool quiet) {
252 bool rval = true;
253 if(learn_rule == CTLEABRA_CAL) {
254 if(cg->prjn) {
255 if(cg->prjn->CheckError(!cg->prjn->con_type->InheritsFrom(&TA_LeabraSRAvgCon), quiet, rval,
256 "does not have con_type = LeabraSRAvgCon -- required for CTLEABRA_CAL learning to hold the sravg connection-level values -- I just fixed this for you in this projection, but must do Build to get it to take effect")) {
257 cg->prjn->con_type = &TA_LeabraSRAvgCon;
258 }
259 }
260 }
261 return rval;
262}
263
264void LeabraConSpec::Compute_NetinScale(LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp, LeabraLayer* from) {
265 float savg = from->kwta.pct;
266 float from_sz = (float)from->units.leaves;
267 float n_cons = (float)recv_gp->size;
268 if(wt_scale.old) {
269 if(savg_cor.norm_con_n) // this is default
270 recv_gp->scale_eff = wt_scale.NetScale() / (n_cons * savg);
271 else
272 recv_gp->scale_eff = wt_scale.NetScale() / (from_sz * savg);
273 }
274 else { // new way!
275 recv_gp->scale_eff = wt_scale.FullScale(savg, from_sz, n_cons);
276 }
277}
278
279
280void LeabraConSpec::SetLearnRule(LeabraNetwork* net) {
281 if((int)net->learn_rule == (int)learn_rule) return;
282 learn_rule = (LeabraConSpec::LearnRule)net->learn_rule;
283 // todo: could set come conflicting params..
284 if(learn_rule != LEABRA_CHL) {
285 if(wt_sig.off == 1.25f)
286 wt_sig.off = 1.0f; // this is key
287 if(GetTypeDef() == &TA_LeabraConSpec) { // only for generic conspecs -- not derived ones!
288 if(lrate == 0.01f)
289 lrate = 0.02f; // also important
290 }
291 wt_sig.dwt_norm = true; // definitely default for xcal
292 }
293 else {
294 if(wt_sig.off == 1.0f)
295 wt_sig.off = 1.25f;
296 if(GetTypeDef() == &TA_LeabraConSpec) { // only for generic conspecs -- not derived ones!
297 if(lrate == 0.02f)
298 lrate = 0.01f; // also important
299 }
300 }
301 UpdateAfterEdit(); // pick up flags
302}
303
304void LeabraConSpec::SetCurLrate(LeabraNetwork* net, int epoch) {
305 cur_lrate = lrate; // as a backup..
306 if(lrs_value == NO_LRS) return;
307
308 if(lrs_value == EXT_REW_AVG) {
309 LeabraLayer* er_lay = LeabraLayerSpec::FindLayerFmSpecNet(net, &TA_ExtRewLayerSpec);
310 if(er_lay != NULL__null) {
311 LeabraUnit* un = (LeabraUnit*)er_lay->units.Leaf(0);
312 float avg_rew = un->act_avg;
313 int ar_pct = (int)(100.0f * avg_rew);
314 cur_lrate = lrate * lrate_sched.GetVal(ar_pct);
315 return;
316 }
317 else {
318 TestWarning(true, "SetCurLrate", "appropriate ExtRew layer not found for EXT_REW_AVG, reverting to EPOCH!");
319 SetUnique("lrs_value", true);
320 lrs_value = EPOCH;
321 UpdateAfterEdit();
322 }
323 }
324 if(lrs_value == EXT_REW_STAT) {
325 int arval = 0;
326 if(net->epoch < 1) {
327 arval = lrate_sched.last_ctr;
328 }
329 else {
330 arval = (int)(100.0f * net->avg_ext_rew);
331 }
332 cur_lrate = lrate * lrate_sched.GetVal(arval);
333 }
334
335 // this is no longer relevant
336// if(lrs_value == SE_STAT) {
337// int seval = 0;
338// if(net->epoch < 1) {
339// seval = lrate_sched.last_ctr;
340// }
341// else {
342// seval = (int);
343// }
344// cur_lrate = lrate * lrate_sched.GetVal(seval);
345// }
346
347 if(lrs_value == EPOCH) {
348 cur_lrate = lrate * lrate_sched.GetVal(epoch);
349 }
350}
351
352void LeabraConSpec::LogLrateSched(int epcs_per_step, float n_steps) {
353 float log_ns[3] = {1, .5f, .2f};
354
355 lrate_sched.SetSize((int)n_steps);
356 for(int i=0;i<n_steps;i++) {
357 lrate_sched[i]->start_ctr = i * epcs_per_step;
358 lrate_sched[i]->start_val = log_ns[i%3] * powf(10.0f,-(i/3));
359 }
360 UpdateAfterEdit(); // needed to update the sub guys
361}
362
363void LeabraConSpec::CreateWtSigFun() {
364 if((wt_sig_fun_lst.gain == wt_sig.gain) && (wt_sig_fun_lst.off == wt_sig.off)
365 && (wt_sig_fun_res == wt_sig_fun.res))
366 return;
367 wt_sig_fun.AllocForRange();
368 int i;
369 for(i=0; i<wt_sig_fun.size; i++) {
370 float w = wt_sig_fun.Xval(i);
371 wt_sig_fun[i] = wt_sig.SigFmLinWt(w);
372 }
373 wt_sig_fun_inv.AllocForRange();
374 for(i=0; i<wt_sig_fun_inv.size; i++) {
375 float w = wt_sig_fun_inv.Xval(i);
376 wt_sig_fun_inv[i] = wt_sig.LinFmSigWt(w);
377 }
378 // prevent needless recomputation of this lookup table..
379 wt_sig_fun_lst.gain = wt_sig.gain; wt_sig_fun_lst.off = wt_sig.off;
380 wt_sig_fun_res = wt_sig_fun.res;
381}
382
383void LeabraConSpec::GraphWtSigFun(DataTable* graph_data) {
384 taProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(taProject)(taProject *) GetOwner(&TA_taProject);
385 if(!graph_data) {
386 graph_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(name + "_WtSigFun", true);
387 }
388 graph_data->StructUpdate(true);
389 graph_data->ResetData();
390 int idx;
391 DataCol* lnwt = graph_data->FindMakeColName("Wt", idx, VT_FLOAT);
392 DataCol* sigwt = graph_data->FindMakeColName("SigWt", idx, VT_FLOAT);
393 DataCol* invwt = graph_data->FindMakeColName("InvWt", idx, VT_FLOAT);
394 lnwt->SetUserData("MIN", 0.0f);
395 lnwt->SetUserData("MAX", 1.0f);
396 sigwt->SetUserData("MIN", 0.0f);
397 sigwt->SetUserData("MAX", 1.0f);
398 invwt->SetUserData("MIN", 0.0f);
399 invwt->SetUserData("MAX", 1.0f);
400
401 float x;
402 for(x = 0.0f; x <= 1.0f; x += .01f) {
403 float sig = wt_sig.SigFmLinWt(x);
404 float inv = wt_sig.LinFmSigWt(x);
405 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
406 lnwt->SetValAsFloat(x, -1);
407 sigwt->SetValAsFloat(sig, -1);
408 invwt->SetValAsFloat(inv, -1);
409 }
410 graph_data->StructUpdate(false);
411 graph_data->FindMakeGraphView();
412}
413
414void LeabraConSpec::GraphXCaldWtFun(DataTable* graph_data, float thr_p) {
415 taProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(taProject)(taProject *) GetOwner(&TA_taProject);
416 if(!graph_data) {
417 graph_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(name + "_XCalFun", true);
418 }
419 graph_data->StructUpdate(true);
420 graph_data->ResetData();
421 int idx;
422 DataCol* sravg = graph_data->FindMakeColName("SRAvg", idx, VT_FLOAT);
423 DataCol* dwt = graph_data->FindMakeColName("dWt", idx, VT_FLOAT);
424 sravg->SetUserData("MIN", 0.0f);
425 sravg->SetUserData("MAX", 1.0f);
426 dwt->SetUserData("MIN", -1.0f);
427 dwt->SetUserData("MAX", 1.0f);
428
429 float x;
430 for(x = 0.0f; x <= 1.0f; x += .01f) {
431 float dw = xcal.dWtFun(x, thr_p);
432 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
433 sravg->SetValAsFloat(x, -1);
434 dwt->SetValAsFloat(dw, -1);
435 }
436 graph_data->StructUpdate(false);
437 graph_data->FindMakeGraphView();
438}

440void LeabraConSpec::GraphXCalSoftBoundFun(DataTable* graph_data) {
441 taProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(taProject)(taProject *) GetOwner(&TA_taProject);
442 if(!graph_data) {
443 graph_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(name + "_XCalSoftBoundFun", true);
444 }
445 graph_data->StructUpdate(true);
446 graph_data->ResetData();
447 int idx;
448 DataCol* wt = graph_data->FindMakeColName("Wt", idx, VT_FLOAT);
449 DataCol* dwt = graph_data->FindMakeColName("dWt", idx, VT_FLOAT);
450 wt->SetUserData("MIN", 0.0f);
451 wt->SetUserData("MAX", 1.0f);
452 dwt->SetUserData("MIN", 0.0f);
453 dwt->SetUserData("MAX", 0.5f);
454
455 float x;
456 for(x = 0.0f; x <= 1.0f; x += .01f) {
457 float dw = xcal.SymSbFun(x);
458 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
459 wt->SetValAsFloat(x, -1);
460 dwt->SetValAsFloat(dw, -1);
461 }
462 graph_data->StructUpdate(false);
463 graph_data->FindMakeGraphView();
464}

466void LeabraConSpec::WtScaleCvt(float savg, int lay_sz, int n_cons,
467 bool norm_con_n) {
468 int slay_act_n = (int)(savg * lay_sz + .5f); // sending layer actual # active
469 slay_act_n = MAX(slay_act_n, 1)(((slay_act_n) > (1)) ? (slay_act_n) : (1));
470 int r_avg_act_n = (int)(savg * n_cons + .5f);// recv average actual # active if uniform
471 r_avg_act_n = MAX(r_avg_act_n, 1)(((r_avg_act_n) > (1)) ? (r_avg_act_n) : (1));
472 float old_val;
473 if(norm_con_n)
474 old_val = 1.0f / (float)(savg * n_cons);
475 else
476 old_val = 1.0f / (float)slay_act_n;
477 float new_val = wt_scale.SLayActScale(savg, lay_sz, n_cons);
478 float new_old_rat = new_val / old_val;
479 float old_new_rat = old_val / new_val;
480 taMisc::Info("old_scale:", StringtaString(old_val), "new_scale:", StringtaString(new_val),
481 "new / old:", StringtaString(new_old_rat), "old / new:", StringtaString(old_new_rat),
482 StringtaString("cur wt_scale.abs: ") + StringtaString(wt_scale.abs) + StringtaString(" new abs to remain same: ") +
483 StringtaString(old_new_rat * wt_scale.abs));
484 // new = new_abs.* new_sc
485 // old = old_abs * old_sc
486 // new_abs * new_sc = old_abs * old_sc
487 // new_abs = old_abs * (old_sc / new_sc)
488}

541bool LeabraBiasSpec::CheckObjectType_impl(taBase* obj) {
542 // don't allow anything to point to a biasspec except the unitspec!

556
557void ActFunSpec::Defaults_init() {
558 gelin = true;
559 vm_mod_max = 0.95f;
560 old_gelin = false;
561 if(taMisc::is_loading) {
562 taVersion v511(5, 1, 1);
563 if(taMisc::loading_version < v511) { // default prior to 511 is non-gelin
564 gelin = false;
565 }
566 else {
567 taVersion v531(5, 3, 1);
568 if(taMisc::loading_version < v531) { // default prior to 531 is old-gelin
569 old_gelin = true;
570 }
571 }
572 }
573 if(gelin) {
574 thr = .5f;
575 gain = 100.0f;
576 nvar = .005f;
577 }
578 else {
579 thr = .25f;
580 gain = 600.0f;
581 nvar = .005f;
582 }
583 avg_dt = .005f;
584 avg_init = 0.15f;
585}

587void ActFunSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
588 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
589 if(owner) owner->UpdateAfterEdit(); // update our unitspec so it can recompute lookup function!
590}
591
592void SpikeFunSpec::Initialize() {
593 g_gain = 9.0f;
594 rise = 0.0f;
595 decay = 5.0f;
596 window = 3;
597 eq_gain = 8.0f;
598 eq_dt = 0.02f;
599 // vm_dt of .1 should also be used; vm_noise var .002???
600
601 gg_decay = g_gain / decay;
602 gg_decay_sq = g_gain / (decay * decay);
603 gg_decay_rise = g_gain / (decay - rise);
604
605 oneo_decay = 1.0f / decay;
606 if(rise > 0.0f)
607 oneo_rise = 1.0f / rise;
608 else
609 oneo_rise = 1.0f;
610}
611
612void SpikeFunSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
613 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
614 if(window <= 0) window = 1;
615 if(decay > 0.0f) {
616 gg_decay = g_gain / decay;
617 gg_decay_sq = g_gain / (decay * decay);
618 if(decay != rise)
619 gg_decay_rise = g_gain / (decay - rise);
620
621 oneo_decay = 1.0f / decay;
622 if(rise > 0.0f)
623 oneo_rise = 1.0f / rise;
624 else
625 oneo_rise = 1.0f;
626 }
627}

638 clamp_type = REGULAR;
639}

641void SpikeMiscSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
642 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
643 vm_dend_time = 1.0f / vm_dend_dt;
644}

679 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();

681 if(asymp_act < .00001f) asymp_act = .00001f;
682 if(asymp_act > 1.0f) asymp_act = 1.0f;
683 depl = rec * (1.0f - asymp_act) / (asymp_act * .95f);
684 depl = MAX(depl, 0.0f)(((depl) > (0.0f)) ? (depl) : (0.0f));

815void LeabraUnitSpec::Initialize() {

824 noise.var = .001f;
825
826 noise_conv.x_range.min = -.05f;
827 noise_conv.x_range.max = .05f;
828 noise_conv.res = .001f;
829 noise_conv.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
830
831 if(act.gelin) {
832 nxx1_fun.x_range.min = -.1f;
833 nxx1_fun.x_range.max = 1.0f;
834 nxx1_fun.res = .001f;
835 nxx1_fun.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
836 }
837 else {
838 nxx1_fun.x_range.min = -.03f;
839 nxx1_fun.x_range.max = .20f;
840 nxx1_fun.res = .001f;
841 nxx1_fun.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
842 }
843
844 Defaults_init();
845
846 CreateNXX1Fun();
847}

897void LeabraUnitSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
898 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
899
900 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
901 dt.midpoint = true; // must use midpoint for spiking
902 }
903
904 clamp_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
905 vm_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
906 depress.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
907 noise_sched.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
908 spike.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
909 spike_misc.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
910 adapt.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
911 dt.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
912 act_avg.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
913 noise_adapt.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
914 CreateNXX1Fun();
915 e_rev_sub_thr.e = e_rev.e - act.thr;
916 e_rev_sub_thr.l = e_rev.l - act.thr;
917 e_rev_sub_thr.i = e_rev.i - act.thr;
918 e_rev_sub_thr.h = e_rev.h - act.thr;
919 e_rev_sub_thr.a = e_rev.a - act.thr;
920 // thr_sub_e_rev_i = g_bar.i * (act.thr - e_rev.i);
921 thr_sub_e_rev_i = (act.thr - e_rev.i);
922 thr_sub_e_rev_e = (act.thr - e_rev.e);
923}

925void LeabraUnitSpec::CheckThisConfig_impl(bool quiet, bool& rval) {
926 inherited::CheckThisConfig_impl(quiet, rval);
927 if(CheckError(da_mod.on && act.i_thr != ActFunSpec::NO_AH, quiet, rval,
928 "da_mod is on but act.i_thr != NO_AH -- this is generally required for da modulation to work properly as it operates through the a & h currents, and including them in i_thr computation leads to less clean modulation effects -- I set this for you in spec:", name)) {
929 SetUnique("act", true);
930 act.i_thr = ActFunSpec::NO_AH; // key for dopamine effects
931 }
932 LeabraNetwork* net = GET_MY_OWNER(LeabraNetwork)(LeabraNetwork *) GetOwner(&TA_LeabraNetwork);
933 // if(net) {
934 // }
935}
936
937bool LeabraUnitSpec::CheckConfig_Unit(Unit* un, bool quiet) {
938 if(!inherited::CheckConfig_Unit(un, quiet)) return false;
939
940 // Network* net = GET_MY_OWNER(Network);
941 bool rval = true;
942
943 return rval;
944}
945
946void LeabraUnitSpec::CreateNXX1Fun() {
947 // first create the gaussian noise convolver
948 if(act.gelin) {
949 nxx1_fun.x_range.max = 1.0f;
950 nxx1_fun.res = .001f; // needs same fine res to get the noise transitions
951 nxx1_fun.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
952 }
953 else {
954 nxx1_fun.x_range.max = .20f;
955 nxx1_fun.res = .001f;
956 nxx1_fun.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
957 }
958 float ns_rng = 3.0f * act.nvar; // range factor based on noise level -- 3 sd
959 ns_rng = MAX(ns_rng, nxx1_fun.res)(((ns_rng) > (nxx1_fun.res)) ? (ns_rng) : (nxx1_fun.res));
960 nxx1_fun.x_range.min = -ns_rng;
961
962 noise_conv.x_range.min = -ns_rng;
963 noise_conv.x_range.max = ns_rng;
964 noise_conv.res = nxx1_fun.res;
965 noise_conv.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
966
967 noise_conv.AllocForRange();
968 int i;
969 float eff_nvar = MAX(act.nvar, 1.0e-6f)(((act.nvar) > (1.0e-6f)) ? (act.nvar) : (1.0e-6f)); // just too lazy to do proper conditional for 0..
970 float var = eff_nvar * eff_nvar;
971 for(i=0; i < noise_conv.size; i++) {
972 float x = noise_conv.Xval(i);
973 noise_conv[i] = expf(-((x * x) / var));
974 }
975
976 // normalize it
977 float sum = 0.0f;
978 for(i=0; i < noise_conv.size; i++)
979 sum += noise_conv[i];
980 for(i=0; i < noise_conv.size; i++)
981 noise_conv[i] /= sum;
982
983 // then create the initial function
984 FunLookup fun;
985 fun.x_range.min = nxx1_fun.x_range.min + noise_conv.x_range.min;
986 fun.x_range.max = nxx1_fun.x_range.max + noise_conv.x_range.max;
987 fun.res = nxx1_fun.res;
988 fun.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
989 fun.AllocForRange();
990
991 if(act_fun == LeabraUnitSpec::NOISY_LINEAR) {
992 for(i=0; i<fun.size; i++) {
993 float x = fun.Xval(i);
994 float val = 0.0f;
995 if(x > 0.0f)
996 val = act.gain * x;
997 fun[i] = val;
998 }
999 }
1000 else {
1001 for(i=0; i<fun.size; i++) {
1002 float x = fun.Xval(i);
1003 float val = 0.0f;
1004 if(x > 0.0f)
1005 val = (act.gain * x) / ((act.gain * x) + 1.0f);
1006 fun[i] = val;
1007 }
1008 }
1009
1010 nxx1_fun.Convolve(fun, noise_conv); // does alloc
1011}

1038void LeabraUnitSpec::Init_Netins(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork*) {
1039 // too drastic
1040 // u->net_scale = 0.0f;
1041 // u->bias_scale = 0.0f;
1042 u->act_sent = 0.0f;
1043 u->net_raw = 0.0f;
1044 u->net_delta = 0.0f;
1045 u->g_i_raw = 0.0f;
1046 u->g_i_delta = 0.0f;
1047
1048 u->net = 0.0f;
1049 u->gc.i = 0.0f;
1050
1051 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
1052 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
1053 recv_gp->net = 0.0f;
1054 recv_gp->net_raw = 0.0f;
1055 recv_gp->net_delta = 0.0f;
1056 }

1059void LeabraUnitSpec::Init_Acts(Unit* u, Network* net) {
1060 inherited::Init_Acts(u, net);
1061 LeabraUnit* lu = (LeabraUnit*)u;
1062
1063 Init_Netins(lu, (LeabraNetwork*)net);
1064
1065 lu->prv_net = 0.0f;
1066 lu->prv_g_i = 0.0f;
1067
1068 if(hyst.init) {
1069 lu->vcb.hyst = lu->vcb.g_h = 0.0f;
1070 lu->vcb.hyst_on = false;
1071 }
1072 if(acc.init) {
1073 lu->vcb.acc = lu->vcb.g_a = 0.0f;
1074 lu->vcb.acc_on = false;
1075 }
1076 lu->gc.l = 0.0f;
1077 lu->gc.i = 0.0f;
1078 lu->gc.h = 0.0f;
1079 lu->gc.a = 0.0f;
1080 lu->I_net = 0.0f;
1081 lu->v_m = v_m_init.Gen();
1082 lu->vm_dend = 0.0f;
1083 lu->adapt = 0.0f;
1084 lu->da = 0.0f;
1085 lu->act = 0.0f;
1086 lu->act_eq = 0.0f;
1087 lu->act_nd = 0.0f;
1088 lu->act_p = lu->act_m = lu->act_dif = 0.0f;
1089 lu->act_m2 = lu->act_p2 = lu->act_dif2 = 0.0f;
1090 lu->avg_ss = act.avg_init;
1091 lu->avg_s = act.avg_init;
1092 lu->avg_m = act.avg_init;
1093 lu->davg = 0.0f;
1094 lu->dav = 0.0f;
1095 lu->noise = 0.0f;
1096 lu->maint_h = 0.0f;
1097
1098 lu->i_thr = 0.0f;
1099 if(depress.on)
1100 lu->spk_amp = depress.max_amp;
1101 lu->spk_t = -1;
1102
1103 Init_SpikeBuff(lu);
1104 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
1105 lu->spike_e_buf->Reset();
1106 lu->spike_i_buf->Reset();
1107 }
1108
1109 Init_ActBuff(lu);
1110 if(syn_delay.on) {
1111 lu->act_buf->Reset();
1112 }
1113}
1114
1115
1116void LeabraUnitSpec::DecayState(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, float decay) {
1117 Init_Netins(u, net);
1118
1119 u->v_m -= decay * (u->v_m - v_m_init.mean);
1120 u->vm_dend -= decay * u->vm_dend;
1121 u->adapt -= decay * u->adapt;
1122 u->act -= decay * u->act;
1123 u->act_nd -= decay * u->act_nd;
1124 u->act_eq -= decay * u->act_eq;
1125 // note: this is causing a problem in learning with xcal:
1126// u->avg_ss -= decay * (u->avg_ss - act.avg_init);
1127// u->avg_s -= decay * (u->avg_s - act.avg_init);
1128// u->avg_m -= decay * (u->avg_m - act.avg_init);
1129 u->prv_net -= decay * u->prv_net;
1130 u->prv_g_i -= decay * u->prv_g_i;
1131 if(hyst.on && !hyst.trl)
1132 u->vcb.hyst -= decay * u->vcb.hyst;
1133 if(acc.on && !acc.trl)
1134 u->vcb.acc -= decay * u->vcb.acc;
1135 if(depress.on)
1136 u->spk_amp += (depress.max_amp - u->spk_amp) * decay;
1137
1138 u->da = u->I_net = 0.0f;
1139
1140 if(decay == 1.0f) {
1141 Init_SpikeBuff(u);
1142 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
1143 u->spike_e_buf->Reset();
1144 u->spike_i_buf->Reset();
1145 }
1146
1147 Init_ActBuff(u);
1148 if(syn_delay.on) {
1149 u->act_buf->Reset();
1150 }
1151 }
1152}
1153
1154void LeabraUnitSpec::Init_SpikeBuff(LeabraUnit* u) {
1155 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
1156 if(!u->spike_e_buf) {
1157 u->spike_e_buf = new float_CircBuffer;
1158 taBase::Own(u->spike_e_buf, u);
1159 }
1160 if(!u->spike_i_buf) {
1161 u->spike_i_buf = new float_CircBuffer;
1162 taBase::Own(u->spike_i_buf, u);
1163 }
1164 }
1165 else {
1166 if(u->spike_e_buf) {
1167 taBase::unRefDone(u->spike_e_buf);
1168 u->spike_e_buf = NULL__null;
1169 }
1170 if(u->spike_i_buf) {
1171 taBase::unRefDone(u->spike_i_buf);
1172 u->spike_i_buf = NULL__null;
1173 }
1174 }
1175}
1176
1177void LeabraUnitSpec::Init_ActBuff(LeabraUnit* u) {
1178 if(syn_delay.on) {
1179 if(!u->act_buf) {
1180 u->act_buf = new float_CircBuffer;
1181 taBase::Own(u->act_buf, u);
1182 }
1183 }
1184 else {
1185 if(u->act_buf) {
1186 taBase::unRefDone(u->act_buf);
1187 u->act_buf = NULL__null;
1188 }
1189 }
1190}

1212
1213void LeabraUnitSpec::Trial_NoiseInit(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1214 if(noise_type != NO_NOISE && noise_adapt.trial_fixed && !noise_adapt.k_pos_noise &&
1215 (noise.type != Random::NONE)) {
1216 u->noise = noise.Gen();
1217 }
1218}
1219
1220void LeabraUnitSpec::Trial_Init_SRAvg(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1221 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
1222
1223 if(net->learn_rule != LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_XCAL_C) {
1224 float lval = u->avg_m;
1225 if(lval > u->avg_l)
1226 u->avg_l += act_avg.l_up_dt * (lval - u->avg_l);
1227 else
1228 u->avg_l += act_avg.l_dn_dt * (lval - u->avg_l);
1229 }
1230
1231 if(net->learn_rule == LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_CAL || net->ct_sravg.force_con) {
1232 for(int g = 0; g < u->send.size; g++) {
1233 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)u->send.FastEl(g);
1234 if(send_gp->prjn->layer->lesioned() || !send_gp->size) continue;
1235 send_gp->Trial_Init_SRAvg(u);
1236 }
1237 }
1238}
1239
1240///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
1241// SettleInit functions
1242
1243void LeabraUnitSpec::Settle_Init_Unit(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
1244 Settle_Init_TargFlags(u, net);
1245 Settle_DecayState(u, net);
1246 Compute_NetinScale(u, net);
1247}
1248
1249void LeabraUnitSpec::Settle_Init_TargFlags(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1250 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
1251 if(!u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG))
1252 return;
1253
1254 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE) {
1255 if(!lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG)) { // layer isn't a target but unit is..
1256 u->targ = u->ext;
1257 }
1258 u->ext = 0.0f;
1259 u->UnSetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
1260 }
1261 else {
1262 u->ext = u->targ;
1263 u->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
1264 }
1265}
1266
1267void LeabraUnitSpec::Settle_DecayState(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1268 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
1269 LeabraLayerSpec* ls = (LeabraLayerSpec*)lay->GetLayerSpec();
1270 float dkval = 0.0f;
1271 if(net->phase_no == 1)
1272 dkval = ls->decay.phase;
1273 else
1274 dkval = ls->decay.phase2;
1275 DecayState(u, net, dkval);
1276}
1277
1278void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_NetinScale(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1279 // this is all receiver-based and done only at beginning of a trial
1280 u->net_scale = 0.0f; // total of scale values for this unit's inputs
1281
1282 float inhib_net_scale = 0.0f;
1283 int n_active_cons = 0; // track this for bias weight scaling!
1284 bool old_scaling = false;
1285 // possible dependence on recv_gp->size is why this cannot be computed in Projection
1286 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
1287 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
1288 LeabraLayer* from = (LeabraLayer*) recv_gp->prjn->from.ptr();
1289 if(from->lesioned() || !recv_gp->size) continue;
1290 // this is the normalization value: takes into account target activity of layer
1291 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
1292 cs->Compute_NetinScale(recv_gp, from);
1293 if(cs->wt_scale.old)
1294 old_scaling = true; // any old = old..
1295
1296 if(cs->inhib && !old_scaling) {
1297 inhib_net_scale += cs->wt_scale.rel;
1298 }
1299 else {
1300 n_active_cons++;
1301 u->net_scale += cs->wt_scale.rel;
1302 }
1303 }
1304 // add the bias weight into the netinput, scaled by 1/n
1305 if(u->bias.size) {
1306 LeabraConSpec* bspec = (LeabraConSpec*)bias_spec.SPtr();
1307 u->bias_scale = bspec->wt_scale.abs; // still have absolute scaling if wanted..
1308 if(u->n_recv_cons > 0)
1309 u->bias_scale /= (float)u->n_recv_cons; // one over n scaling for bias!
1310 }
1311 // now renormalize
1312 if(u->net_scale > 0.0f) {
1313 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
1314 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
1315 Projection* prjn = (Projection*) recv_gp->prjn;
1316 LeabraLayer* from = (LeabraLayer*) prjn->from.ptr();
1317 if(from->lesioned() || !recv_gp->size) continue;
1318 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
1319 if(cs->inhib && !old_scaling) continue; // norm separately
1320 recv_gp->scale_eff /= u->net_scale; // normalize by total connection scale
1321 }
1322 }
1323 // separately normalize inhibitory connections
1324 if(inhib_net_scale > 0.0f) {
1325 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
1326 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
1327 LeabraLayer* from = (LeabraLayer*) recv_gp->prjn->from.ptr();
1328 if(from->lesioned() || !recv_gp->size) continue;
1329 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
1330 if(!cs->inhib) continue; // norm separately
1331 recv_gp->scale_eff /= inhib_net_scale; // normalize by total connection scale
1332 }
1333 }
1334}
1335
1336void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_NetinScale_Senders(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork*) {
1337 for(int g=0; g<u->send.size; g++) {
1338 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)u->send.FastEl(g);
1339 if(send_gp->size > 0) {
1340 Unit* ru = send_gp->Un(0);
1341 send_gp->scale_eff = ((LeabraRecvCons*)ru->recv.FastEl(send_gp->recv_idx()))->scale_eff;
1342 }
1343 else {
1344 send_gp->scale_eff = 0.0f;
1345 }
1346 }
1347}
1348
1349void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_HardClamp(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork*) {
1350 u->net = u->prv_net = u->ext;
1351 u->act_eq = clamp_range.Clip(u->ext);
1352 u->act_nd = u->act_eq;
1353 u->act = u->act_eq;
1354 if(u->act_eq == 0.0f)
1355 u->v_m = e_rev.l;
1356 else
1357 u->v_m = act.thr + u->act_eq / act.gain;
1358 u->da = u->I_net = 0.0f;
1359
1360 if(syn_delay.on && !u->act_buf) Init_ActBuff(u);
1361 u->AddToActBuf(syn_delay);
1362}
1363
1364// NOTE: these two functions should always be the same modulo the clamp_range.Clip
1365
1366void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_HardClampNoClip(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork*) {
1367 u->net = u->prv_net = u->ext;
1368 // u->act_eq = clamp_range.Clip(u->ext);
1369 u->act_eq = u->ext;
1370 u->act_nd = u->act_eq;
1371 u->act = u->act_eq;
1372 if(u->act_eq == 0.0f)
1373 u->v_m = e_rev.l;
1374 else
1375 u->v_m = act.thr + u->act_eq / act.gain;
1376 u->da = u->I_net = 0.0f;
1377
1378 if(syn_delay.on && !u->act_buf) Init_ActBuff(u);
1379 u->AddToActBuf(syn_delay);
1380}
1381
1382void LeabraUnitSpec::ExtToComp(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork*) {
1383 if(!u->HasExtFlag(Unit::EXT))
1384 return;
1385 u->ext_flag = Unit::COMP;
1386 u->targ = u->ext;
1387 u->ext = 0.0f;
1388}
1389
1390void LeabraUnitSpec::TargExtToComp(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork*) {
1391 if(!u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG_EXT))
1392 return;
1393 if(u->HasExtFlag(Unit::EXT))
1394 u->targ = u->ext;
1395 u->ext = 0.0f;
1396 u->ext_flag = Unit::COMP;
1397}
1398
1399///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
1400// Cycle Step 1: netinput
1401
1402void LeabraUnitSpec::Send_NetinDelta(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
1403 int thno_arg = thread_no;
1404 if(thread_no < 0) {
1405 net->send_pct_tot++; // only safe for non-thread case
1406 if(net->NetinPerPrjn())
1407 thno_arg = 0; // pass 0 as arg -- need to store in tmp vec
1408 }
1409 float act_ts = u->act;
1410 if(syn_delay.on) {
1411 if(!u->act_buf)
1412 Init_ActBuff(u);
1413 act_ts = u->act_buf->CircSafeEl(0); // get first logical element..
1414 }
1415
1416 if(act_ts > opt_thresh.send) {
1417 float act_delta = act_ts - u->act_sent;
1418 if(fabsf(act_delta) > opt_thresh.delta) {
1419 if(thread_no < 0)
1420 net->send_pct_n++;
1421 for(int g=0; g<u->send.size; g++) {
1422 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)u->send.FastEl(g);
1423 LeabraLayer* tol = (LeabraLayer*) send_gp->prjn->layer;
1424 if(tol->lesioned() || tol->hard_clamped || !send_gp->size) continue;
1425 send_gp->Send_NetinDelta(net, thno_arg, act_delta);
1426 }
1427 u->act_sent = act_ts; // cache the last sent value
1428 }
1429 }
1430 else if(u->act_sent > opt_thresh.send) {
1431 if(thread_no < 0)
1432 net->send_pct_n++;
1433 float act_delta = - u->act_sent; // un-send the last above-threshold activation to get back to 0
1434 for(int g=0; g<u->send.size; g++) {
1435 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)u->send.FastEl(g);
1436 LeabraLayer* tol = (LeabraLayer*) send_gp->prjn->layer;
1437 if(tol->lesioned() || tol->hard_clamped || !send_gp->size) continue;
1438 send_gp->Send_NetinDelta(net, thno_arg, act_delta);
1439 }
1440 u->act_sent = 0.0f; // now it effectively sent a 0..
1441 }
1442}
1443
1444void LeabraUnitSpec::Send_NetinDelta_Post(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1445 int nt = net->threads.tasks.size;
1446 float nw_nt = 0.0f;
1447 if(net->NetinPerPrjn()) { // always uses netin_tmp -- this is where inhib goes
1448 float nw_inhb = 0.0f;
1449 if(!net->threads.using_threads)
1450 nt = 1;
1451 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
1452 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
1453 float g_nw_nt = 0.0f;
1454 for(int j=0;j<nt;j++) {
1455 g_nw_nt += net->send_netin_tmp.FastEl(u->flat_idx, g, j);
1456 }
1457 recv_gp->net_delta = g_nw_nt;
1458 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
1459 // todo: incorporate finer-grained inhib here..
1460 if(cs->inhib)
1461 nw_inhb += g_nw_nt;
1462 else
1463 nw_nt += g_nw_nt;
1464 }
1465 u->net_delta = nw_nt;
1466 u->g_i_delta = nw_inhb;
1467 }
1468 else {
1469 if(net->threads.using_threads) { // if not used, goes directly into unit vals
1470 for(int j=0;j<nt;j++) {
1471 nw_nt += net->send_netin_tmp.FastEl(u->flat_idx, j);
1472 }
1473 u->net_delta = nw_nt;
1474 }
1475 }
1476}
1477
1478void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_NetinInteg(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
1479 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
1480 if(lay->hard_clamped) return;
1481
1482 if(net->NetinPerPrjn()) {
1483 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
1484 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
1485 recv_gp->net_raw += recv_gp->net_delta;
1486 recv_gp->net_delta = 0.0f; // clear for next use
1487
1488 // todo: not clear if we need this at this point..
1489 // float dnet = dt.net * (tot_net - u->prv_net);
1490 // u->net = u->prv_net + dnet;
1491 // u->prv_net = u->net;
1492 // u->net = MAX(u->net, 0.0f); // negative netin doesn't make any sense
1493 }
1494 }
1495
1496 if(net->inhib_cons_used) {
1497 u->g_i_raw += u->g_i_delta;
1498 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
1499 u->gc.i = MAX(u->g_i_raw, 0.0f)(((u->g_i_raw) > (0.0f)) ? (u->g_i_raw) : (0.0f));
1500 Compute_NetinInteg_Spike_i(u, net);
1501 }
1502 else {
1503 u->gc.i = u->prv_g_i + dt.net * (u->g_i_raw - u->prv_g_i);
1504 u->prv_g_i = u->gc.i;
1505 }
1506 }
1507
1508 u->net_raw += u->net_delta;
1509 float tot_net = (u->bias_scale * u->bias.OwnCn(0)->wt) + u->net_raw;
1510 if(u->HasExtFlag(Unit::EXT)) {
1511 LeabraLayerSpec* ls = (LeabraLayerSpec*)lay->GetLayerSpec();
1512 tot_net += u->ext * ls->clamp.gain;
1513 }
1514
1515 u->net_delta = 0.0f; // clear for next use
1516 u->g_i_delta = 0.0f; // clear for next use
1517
1518 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
1519 // todo: need a mech for inhib spiking
1520 u->net = MAX(tot_net, 0.0f)(((tot_net) > (0.0f)) ? (tot_net) : (0.0f)); // store directly for integration
1521 Compute_NetinInteg_Spike_e(u, net);
1522 }
1523 else {
1524 float dnet = dt.net * (tot_net - u->prv_net);
1525 u->net = u->prv_net + dnet;
1526 u->prv_net = u->net;
1527 u->net = MAX(u->net, 0.0f)(((u->net) > (0.0f)) ? (u->net) : (0.0f)); // negative netin doesn't make any sense
1528 }
1529
1530 // add just before computing i_thr -- after all the other stuff is done..
1531 if((noise_type == NETIN_NOISE) && (noise.type != Random::NONE) && (net->cycle >= 0)) {
1532 u->net += Compute_Noise(u, net);
1533 }
1534 u->i_thr = Compute_IThresh(u, net);
1535}
1536
1537void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_NetinInteg_Spike_e(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1538 // netin gets added at the end of the spike_buf -- 0 time is the end
1539 Init_SpikeBuff(u);
1540 u->spike_e_buf->CircAddLimit(u->net, spike.window); // add current net to buffer
1541 int mx = MAX(spike.window, u->spike_e_buf->length)(((spike.window) > (u->spike_e_buf->length)) ? (spike
.window) : (u->spike_e_buf->length));
1542 float sum = 0.0f;
1543 if(spike.rise == 0.0f && spike.decay > 0.0f) {
1544 // optimized fast recursive exp decay: note: does NOT use dt.net
1545 for(int t=0;t<mx;t++) {
1546 sum += u->spike_e_buf->CircSafeEl(t);
1547 }
1548 sum /= (float)spike.window; // normalize over window
1549 float dnet = spike.gg_decay * sum - (u->prv_net * spike.oneo_decay);
1550 u->net = u->prv_net + dnet;
1551 u->prv_net = u->net;
1552 }
1553 else {
1554 for(int t=0;t<mx;t++) {
1555 float spkin = u->spike_e_buf->CircSafeEl(t);
1556 if(spkin > 0.0f) {
1557 sum += spkin * spike.ComputeAlpha(mx-t-1);
1558 }
1559 }
1560 u->net = sum;
1561 // from compute_netinavg
1562 float dnet = dt.net * (u->net - u->prv_net);
1563 u->net = u->prv_net + dnet;
1564 u->prv_net = u->net;
1565 }
1566}
1567
1568void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_NetinInteg_Spike_i(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1569 // netin gets added at the end of the spike_i_buf -- 0 time is the end
1570 Init_SpikeBuff(u);
1571 u->spike_i_buf->CircAddLimit(u->gc.i, spike.window); // add current net to buffer
1572 int mx = MAX(spike.window, u->spike_i_buf->length)(((spike.window) > (u->spike_i_buf->length)) ? (spike
.window) : (u->spike_i_buf->length));
1573 float sum = 0.0f;
1574 if(spike.rise == 0.0f && spike.decay > 0.0f) {
1575 // optimized fast recursive exp decay: note: does NOT use dt.net
1576 for(int t=0;t<mx;t++) {
1577 sum += u->spike_i_buf->CircSafeEl(t);
1578 }
1579 sum /= (float)spike.window; // normalize over window
1580 float dnet = spike.gg_decay * sum - (u->prv_g_i * spike.oneo_decay);
1581 u->gc.i = u->prv_g_i + dnet;
1582 u->prv_g_i = u->gc.i;
1583 }
1584 else {
1585 for(int t=0;t<mx;t++) {
1586 float spkin = u->spike_i_buf->CircSafeEl(t);
1587 if(spkin > 0.0f) {
1588 sum += spkin * spike.ComputeAlpha(mx-t-1);
1589 }
1590 }
1591 u->gc.i = sum;
1592 // from compute_netinavg
1593 float dnet = dt.net * (u->gc.i - u->prv_g_i);
1594 u->gc.i = u->prv_g_i + dnet;
1595 u->prv_g_i = u->gc.i;
1596 }
1597}
1598
1599float LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_IThresh(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1600 switch(act.i_thr) {
1601 case ActFunSpec::STD:
1602 return Compute_IThreshStd(u, net);
1603 case ActFunSpec::NO_A:
1604 return Compute_IThreshNoA(u, net);
1605 case ActFunSpec::NO_H:
1606 return Compute_IThreshNoH(u, net);
1607 case ActFunSpec::NO_AH:
1608 return Compute_IThreshNoAH(u, net);
1609 case ActFunSpec::ALL:
1610 return Compute_IThreshAll(u, net);
1611 }
1612 return 0.0f;
1613}
1614
1615///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
1616// Cycle Step 2: inhibition
1617
1618
1619///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
1620// Cycle Step 3: activation
1621
1622void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_Act(Unit* u, Network* net, int thread_no) {
1623 LeabraUnit* lu = (LeabraUnit*)u;
1624 LeabraNetwork* lnet = (LeabraNetwork*)net;
1625 LeabraLayer* lay = lu->own_lay();
1626
1627 if(syn_delay.on && !lu->act_buf) Init_ActBuff(lu);
1628
1629 if((lnet->cycle >= 0) && lay->hard_clamped) {
1630 if(lay->hard_clamped && act_fun == SPIKE) {
1631 Compute_ClampSpike(lu, lnet, u->ext * spike_misc.clamp_max_p);
1632 lu->AddToActBuf(syn_delay);
1633 }
1634 return; // don't re-compute
1635 }
1636
1637 Compute_Conduct(lu, lnet);
1638 Compute_Vm(lu, lnet);
1639 Compute_ActFmVm(lu, lnet);
1640 Compute_SelfReg_Cycle(lu, lnet);
1641
1642 lu->AddToActBuf(syn_delay);
1643}
1644
1645void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_ClampSpike(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, float spike_p) {
1646 bool fire_now = false;
1647 switch(spike_misc.clamp_type) {
1648 case SpikeMiscSpec::POISSON:
1649 if(Random::Poisson(spike_p) > 0.0f) fire_now = true;
1650 break;
1651 case SpikeMiscSpec::UNIFORM:
1652 fire_now = Random::BoolProb(spike_p);
1653 break;
1654 case SpikeMiscSpec::REGULAR: {
1655 if(spike_p > 0.0f) {
1656 int cyc_int = (int)((1.0f / spike_p) + 0.5f);
1657 fire_now = (net->ct_cycle % cyc_int == 0);
1658 }
1659 break;
1660 }
1661 case SpikeMiscSpec::CLAMPED:
1662 return; // do nothing further
1663 }
1664 if(fire_now) {
1665 u->v_m = spike_misc.spk_thr + 0.1f; // make it fire
1666 }
1667 else {
1668 u->v_m = e_rev.l; // make it not fire
1669 }
1670
1671 Compute_ActFmVm_spike(u, net); // then do normal spiking computation
1672}
1673
1674void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_Conduct(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1675 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
1676
1677 if(da_mod.on && (da_mod.mod == DaModSpec::PLUS_CONT)) {
1678 Compute_DaMod_PlusCont(u,net);
1679 }
1680
1681 // total conductances
1682 float g_bar_i_val = g_bar.i;
1683 float g_bar_e_val = g_bar.e;
1684 float g_bar_l_val = g_bar.l;
1685 LeabraLayerSpec* ls = (LeabraLayerSpec*)lay->spec.SPtr();
1686 if((ls->adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::G_BAR_I) || (ls->adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::G_BAR_IL))
1687 g_bar_i_val = lay->adapt_i.g_bar_i; // adapting value..
1688 if(ls->adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::G_BAR_IL)
1689 g_bar_l_val = lay->adapt_i.g_bar_l; // adapting value..
1690 u->gc.i *= g_bar_i_val;
1691 u->net *= g_bar_e_val;
1692 u->gc.l = g_bar_l_val;
1693 u->gc.h = g_bar.h * u->vcb.g_h;
1694 u->gc.a = g_bar.a * u->vcb.g_a;
1695}
1696
1697void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_DaMod_PlusCont(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1698 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::PLUS_PHASE) {
1699 if(u->dav > 0.0f) {
1700 u->vcb.g_a = 0.0f;
1701 u->vcb.g_h = u->maint_h + da_mod.gain * u->dav * u->act_m; // increase in proportion to participation in minus phase
1702 }
1703 else {
1704 u->vcb.g_h = u->maint_h;
1705 u->vcb.g_a = -da_mod.gain * u->dav * u->act_m; // decrease in proportion to participation in minus phase
1706 }
1707 }
1708 else {
1709 u->vcb.g_h = u->maint_h;
1710 u->vcb.g_a = 0.0f; // clear in minus phase!
1711 }
1712}
1713
1714void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_Vm(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1715 if(act_fun == SPIKE && spike_misc.t_r > 0 && u->spk_t > 0) {
1716 int spkdel = net->ct_cycle - u->spk_t;
1717 if(spkdel >= 0 && spkdel <= spike_misc.t_r)
1718 return; // just bail
1719 }
1720
1721 if(net->cycle < dt.vm_eq_cyc) {
1722 // directly go to equilibrium value
1723 float new_v_m = Compute_EqVm(u);
1724 u->I_net = new_v_m - u->v_m; // time integrate: not really I_net but hey
1725 u->v_m += dt.vm_eq_dt * u->I_net;
1726 }
1727 else {
1728 float v_m_eff = u->v_m;
1729 if(dt.midpoint) {
1730 float I_net_1 =
1731 (u->net * (e_rev.e - v_m_eff)) + (u->gc.l * (e_rev.l - v_m_eff)) +
1732 (u->gc.i * (e_rev.i - v_m_eff)) + (u->gc.h * (e_rev.h - v_m_eff)) +
1733 (u->gc.a * (e_rev.a - v_m_eff));
1734 v_m_eff += .5f * dt.vm * I_net_1; // go half way
1735 }
1736 u->I_net =
1737 (u->net * (e_rev.e - v_m_eff)) + (u->gc.l * (e_rev.l - v_m_eff)) +
1738 (u->gc.i * (e_rev.i - v_m_eff)) + (u->gc.h * (e_rev.h - v_m_eff)) +
1739 (u->gc.a * (e_rev.a - v_m_eff));
1740
1741 // add spike current if relevant
1742 if(act_fun == SPIKE && spike_misc.exp_slope > 0.0f) {
1743 u->I_net += g_bar.l * spike_misc.exp_slope *
1744 expf((v_m_eff - act.thr) / spike_misc.exp_slope);
1745 }
1746
1747 float dvm = dt.vm * (u->I_net - u->adapt);
1748 if(dvm > dt.d_vm_max) dvm = dt.d_vm_max;
1749 else if(dvm < -dt.d_vm_max) dvm = -dt.d_vm_max;
1750 u->v_m += dt.integ * dvm;
1751 }
1752
1753 if((noise_type == VM_NOISE) && (noise.type != Random::NONE) && (net->cycle >= 0)) {
1754 u->v_m += Compute_Noise(u, net);
1755 }
1756
1757 u->v_m = vm_range.Clip(u->v_m);
1758
1759 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
1760 // decay back to zero
1761 u->vm_dend -= spike_misc.vm_dend_dt * u->vm_dend;
1762 }
1763}
1764
1765void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_ActFmVm(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1766 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
1767 Compute_ActFmVm_spike(u, net);
1768 Compute_ActAdapt_spike(u, net);
1769 }
1770 else {
1771 Compute_ActFmVm_rate(u, net);
1772 Compute_ActAdapt_rate(u, net);
1773 }
1774}
1775
1776float LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_ActValFmVmVal_rate(float val_sub_thr) {
1777 float new_act = 0.0f;
1778 switch(act_fun) {
1779 case NOISY_XX1: {
1780 if(val_sub_thr <= nxx1_fun.x_range.min)
1781 new_act = 0.0f;
1782 else if(val_sub_thr >= nxx1_fun.x_range.max) {
1783 val_sub_thr *= act.gain;
1784 new_act = val_sub_thr / (val_sub_thr + 1.0f);
1785 }
1786 else {
1787 new_act = nxx1_fun.Eval(val_sub_thr);
1788 }
1789 break;
1790 }
1791 case SPIKE:
1792 break; // compiler food
1793 case NOISY_LINEAR: {
1794 if(val_sub_thr <= nxx1_fun.x_range.min)
1795 new_act = 0.0f;
1796 else if(val_sub_thr >= nxx1_fun.x_range.max) {
1797 new_act = val_sub_thr * act.gain;
1798 }
1799 else {
1800 new_act = nxx1_fun.Eval(val_sub_thr);
1801 }
1802 break;
1803 }
1804 case XX1: {
1805 if(val_sub_thr < 0.0f)
1806 new_act = 0.0f;
1807 else {
1808 val_sub_thr *= act.gain;
1809 new_act = val_sub_thr / (val_sub_thr + 1.0f);
1810 }
1811 break;
1812 }
1813 case LINEAR: {
1814 if(val_sub_thr < 0.0f)
1815 new_act = 0.0f;
1816 else
1817 new_act = val_sub_thr * act.gain;
1818 }
1819 break;
1820 }
1821 return new_act;
1822}
1823
1824void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_ActFmVm_rate(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1825 float new_act;
1826 if(act.gelin) {
1827 if(act.old_gelin) {
1828 float g_e_val = u->net;
1829 float vm_eq = act.vm_mod_max * (Compute_EqVm(u) - v_m_init.mean); // relative to starting!
1830 if(vm_eq > 0.0f) {
1831 float vmrat = (u->v_m - v_m_init.mean) / vm_eq;
1832 if(vmrat > 1.0f) vmrat = 1.0f;
1833 else if(vmrat < 0.0f) vmrat = 0.0f;
1834 g_e_val *= vmrat;
1835 }
1836 float g_e_thr = Compute_EThresh(u);
1837 new_act = Compute_ActValFmVmVal_rate(g_e_val - g_e_thr);
1838 }
1839 else { // new gelin
1840 if(u->v_m <= act.thr) {
1841 new_act = Compute_ActValFmVmVal_rate(u->v_m - act.thr);
1842 }
1843 else {
1844 float g_e_thr = Compute_EThresh(u);
1845 new_act = Compute_ActValFmVmVal_rate(u->net - g_e_thr);
1846 }
1847 if(net->cycle < dt.vm_eq_cyc) {
1848 new_act = u->act_nd + dt.vm_eq_dt * (new_act - u->act_nd); // eq dt
1849 }
1850 else {
1851 new_act = u->act_nd + dt.vm * (new_act - u->act_nd); // time integral with dt.vm -- use nd to avoid synd problems
1852 }
1853 }
1854 }
1855 else {
1856 new_act = Compute_ActValFmVmVal_rate(u->v_m - act.thr);
1857 }
1858 if(depress.on) { // synaptic depression
1859 u->act_nd = act_range.Clip(new_act); // nd is non-discounted activation!!! solves tons of probs
1860 new_act *= MIN(u->spk_amp, 1.0f)(((u->spk_amp) < (1.0f)) ? (u->spk_amp) : (1.0f));
1861 if((net->ct_cycle+1) % depress.interval == 0) {
1862 u->spk_amp += -new_act * depress.depl + (depress.max_amp - u->spk_amp) * depress.rec;
1863 }
1864 if(u->spk_amp < 0.0f) u->spk_amp = 0.0f;
1865 else if(u->spk_amp > depress.max_amp) u->spk_amp = depress.max_amp;
1866 }
1867
1868 u->da = new_act - u->act;
1869 if((noise_type == ACT_NOISE) && (noise.type != Random::NONE) && (net->cycle >= 0)) {
1870 new_act += Compute_Noise(u, net);
1871 }
1872 u->act = act_range.Clip(new_act);
1873 u->act_eq = u->act;
1874 if(!depress.on)
1875 u->act_nd = u->act_eq;
1876}
1877
1878void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_ActAdapt_rate(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1879 if(!adapt.on)
1880 u->adapt = 0.0f;
1881 else {
1882 float dad = dt.integ * adapt.Compute_dAdapt(u->v_m, e_rev.l, u->adapt); // rest relative
1883 if(net->ct_cycle % adapt.interval == 0) {
1884 dad += u->act * adapt.spike_gain; // rate code version of spiking
1885 }
1886 u->adapt += dad;
1887 }
1888}
1889
1890void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_ActFmVm_spike(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1891 if(u->v_m > spike_misc.spk_thr) {
1892 u->act = 1.0f;
1893 u->v_m = spike_misc.vm_r;
1894 u->vm_dend += spike_misc.vm_dend;
1895 u->spk_t = net->ct_cycle;
1896 }
1897 else {
1898 u->act = 0.0f;
1899 }
1900
1901 float old_nd = u->act_nd / spike.eq_gain;
1902 float new_nd;
1903 if(spike.eq_dt > 0.0f) {
1904 new_nd = act_range.Clip(spike.eq_gain * ((1.0f - spike.eq_dt) * old_nd + spike.eq_dt * u->act));
1905 }
1906 else { // increment by phase
1907 if(net->cycle > 0)
1908 old_nd *= (float)net->cycle;
1909 new_nd = act_range.Clip(spike.eq_gain * (old_nd + u->act) / (float)(net->cycle+1));
1910 }
1911 u->da = new_nd - u->act_nd; // da is on equilibrium activation
1912 u->act_nd = new_nd;
1913
1914 if(depress.on) {
1915 u->act *= MIN(u->spk_amp, 1.0f)(((u->spk_amp) < (1.0f)) ? (u->spk_amp) : (1.0f)); // after eq
1916 u->spk_amp += -u->act * depress.depl + (depress.max_amp - u->spk_amp) * depress.rec;
1917 if(u->spk_amp < 0.0f) u->spk_amp = 0.0f;
1918 else if(u->spk_amp > depress.max_amp) u->spk_amp = depress.max_amp;
1919 u->act_eq = u->spk_amp * u->act_nd; // act_eq is depressed rate code, nd is non-depressed!
1920 }
1921 else {
1922 u->act_eq = u->act_nd; // eq = nd
1923 }
1924}
1925
1926void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_ActAdapt_spike(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1927 if(!adapt.on)
1928 u->adapt = 0.0f;
1929 else {
1930 float dad = dt.integ * adapt.Compute_dAdapt(u->v_m, e_rev.l, u->adapt);
1931 if(u->act > 0.0f) { // spiked
1932 dad += adapt.spike_gain;
1933 }
1934 u->adapt += dad;
1935 }
1936}
1937
1938void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_SelfReg_Cycle(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork*) {
1939 // fast time scale updated every cycle
1940 if(hyst.on && !hyst.trl)
1941 hyst.UpdateBasis(u->vcb.hyst, u->vcb.hyst_on, u->vcb.g_h, u->act_eq);
1942 if(acc.on && !acc.trl)
1943 acc.UpdateBasis(u->vcb.acc, u->vcb.acc_on, u->vcb.g_a, u->act_eq);
1944}
1945
1946void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_SelfReg_Trial(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork*) {
1947 // slow time scale updated at end of trial
1948 if(hyst.on && hyst.trl)
1949 hyst.UpdateBasis(u->vcb.hyst, u->vcb.hyst_on, u->vcb.g_h, u->act_eq);
1950 if(acc.on && acc.trl)
1951 acc.UpdateBasis(u->vcb.acc, u->vcb.acc_on, u->vcb.g_a, u->act_eq);
1952}
1953
1954float LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_Noise(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1955 float rval = 0.0f;
1956 if(noise_adapt.trial_fixed) {
1957 rval = u->noise; // u->noise is trial-level generated value
1958 }
1959 else {
1960 rval = noise.Gen();
1961 u->noise = rval;
1962 }
1963
1964 if(noise_adapt.mode == NoiseAdaptSpec::SCHED_CYCLES) {
1965 rval *= noise_sched.GetVal(net->cycle);
1966 }
1967 else if(noise_adapt.mode == NoiseAdaptSpec::SCHED_EPOCHS) {
1968 rval *= noise_sched.GetVal(net->epoch);
1969 }
1970 else if(noise_adapt.mode == NoiseAdaptSpec::PVLV_PVI) {
1971 rval *= (1.0f - (noise_adapt.min_pct_c * net->pvlv_pvi));
1972 }
1973 else if(noise_adapt.mode == NoiseAdaptSpec::PVLV_LVE) {
1974 rval *= (1.0f - (noise_adapt.min_pct_c * net->pvlv_lve));
1975 }
1976 else if(noise_adapt.mode == NoiseAdaptSpec::PVLV_MIN) {
1977 float pvlv_val = MIN(net->pvlv_pvi, net->pvlv_lve)(((net->pvlv_pvi) < (net->pvlv_lve)) ? (net->pvlv_pvi
) : (net->pvlv_lve));
1978 rval *= (1.0f - (noise_adapt.min_pct_c * pvlv_val));
1979 }
1980
1981 return rval;
1982}
1983
1984///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
1985// Cycle Stats
1986
1987float LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_MaxDa(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1988 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
1989 float fda = 0.0f;
1990 switch(maxda.val) {
1991 case MaxDaSpec::NO_MAX_DA:
1992 break;
1993 case MaxDaSpec::DA_ONLY:
1994 fda = fabsf(u->da);
1995 break;
1996 case MaxDaSpec::INET_ONLY:
1997 fda = fabsf(maxda.inet_scale * u->I_net);
1998 break;
1999 case MaxDaSpec::INET_DA:
2000 if(lay->acts.avg <= maxda.lay_avg_thr)
2001 fda = fabsf(maxda.inet_scale * u->I_net);
2002 else
2003 fda = fabsf(u->da);
2004 break;
2005 }
2006 return fda;
2007}

2012void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_MidMinus(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
2013 u->act_m2 = u->act_eq;
2014}

2016void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_CycSynDep(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
2017 for(int g=0; g<u->send.size; g++) {
2018 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)u->send.FastEl(g);
2019 if(send_gp->prjn->layer->lesioned() || !send_gp->size) continue;
2020 send_gp->Compute_CycSynDep(u);
2021 }
2022}

2025///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
2026// Phase and Trial Activation Updating
2027
2028void LeabraUnitSpec::PostSettle(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
2029 bool no_plus_testing = false;
2030 if(net->no_plus_test && (net->train_mode == LeabraNetwork::TEST)) {
2031 no_plus_testing = true;
2032 }
2033
2034 switch(net->phase_order) {
2035 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS:
2036 if(no_plus_testing) {
2037 u->act_m = u->act_p = u->act_nd;
2038 u->act_dif = 0.0f;
2039 u->act_dif2 = 0.0f;
2040 Compute_ActTimeAvg(u, net);
2041 }
2042 else {
2043 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE)
2044 u->act_m = u->act_nd;
2045 else {
2046 u->act_p = u->act_nd;
2047 u->act_dif = u->act_p - u->act_m;
2048 u->act_dif2 = u->act_p - u->act_m2;
2049 Compute_DaMod_PlusPost(u, net);
2050 Compute_ActTimeAvg(u, net);
2051 }
2052 }
2053 break;
2054 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_MINUS:
2055 if(no_plus_testing) {
2056 u->act_m = u->act_p = u->act_nd;
2057 u->act_dif = 0.0f;
2058 u->act_dif2 = 0.0f;
2059 Compute_ActTimeAvg(u, net);
2060 }
2061 else {
2062 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE) {
2063 u->act_m = u->act_nd;
2064 u->act_dif = u->act_p - u->act_m;
2065 u->act_dif2 = u->act_p - u->act_m2;
2066 }
2067 else {
2068 u->act_p = u->act_nd;
2069 Compute_ActTimeAvg(u, net);
2070 }
2071 }
2072 break;
2073 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_ONLY:
2074 u->act_m = u->act_p = u->act_nd;
2075 u->act_dif = 0.0f;
2076 u->act_dif2 = 0.0f;
2077 Compute_ActTimeAvg(u, net);
2078 break;
2079 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
2080 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_MINUS:
2081 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
2082 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
2083 u->act_m = u->act_nd;
2084 }
2085 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
2086 u->act_p = u->act_nd;
2087 u->act_dif = u->act_p - u->act_m;
2088 if(no_plus_testing) {
2089 u->act_m = u->act_nd; // update act_m because it is actually another test case!
2090 }
2091 Compute_DaMod_PlusPost(u, net);
2092 Compute_ActTimeAvg(u, net);
2093 }
2094 else {
2095 u->act_m2 = u->act_nd;
2096 u->act_dif2 = u->act_p - u->act_m2;
2097 }
2098 break;
2099 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_NOTHING:
2100 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
2101 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
2102 u->act_p = u->act_nd;
2103 Compute_ActTimeAvg(u, net);
2104 }
2105 else {
2106 u->act_m = u->act_nd;
2107 u->act_dif = u->act_p - u->act_m;
2108 u->act_dif2 = u->act_p - u->act_m2;
2109 }
2110 break;
2111 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS:
2112 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
2113 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
2114 u->act_m = u->act_nd;
2115 }
2116 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
2117 u->act_p = u->act_nd;
2118 Compute_DaMod_PlusPost(u, net);
2119 Compute_ActTimeAvg(u, net);
2120 u->act_dif = u->act_p - u->act_m;
2121 }
2122 else {
2123 u->act_p2 = u->act_nd;
2124 u->act_dif2 = u->act_p2 - u->act_p;
2125 }
2126 break;
2127 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
2128 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_MINUS:
2129 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
2130 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
2131 u->act_m = u->act_nd;
2132 }
2133 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
2134 u->act_p = u->act_nd;
2135 u->act_dif = u->act_p - u->act_m;
2136 Compute_DaMod_PlusPost(u, net);
2137 Compute_ActTimeAvg(u, net);
2138 }
2139 else if(net->phase_no == 2) {
2140 u->act_p2 = u->act_nd;
2141 u->act_dif2 = u->act_p2 - u->act_p;
2142 }
2143 else {
2144 u->act_m2 = u->act_nd;
2145 u->act_dif2 = u->act_p2 - u->act_m2;
2146 }
2147 break;
2148 }
2149}
2150
2151void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_ActTimeAvg(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
2152 if(act.avg_dt <= 0.0f) return;
2153 u->act_avg += act.avg_dt * (u->act_eq - u->act_avg);
2154}
2155
2156void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_DaMod_PlusPost(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
2157 if(!da_mod.on || (da_mod.mod != DaModSpec::PLUS_POST)) return;
2158 float dact = da_mod.gain * u->dav * u->act_m; // delta activation
2159 if(dact > 0.0f) {
2160 dact *= 1.0f - u->act_p;
2161 }
2162 else {
2163 dact *= u->act_p;
2164 }
2165 u->act_p = act_range.Clip(u->act_p + dact);
2166}
2167
2168
2169//////////////////////////////////////////
2170// Stage 6: Learning //
2171//////////////////////////////////////////
2172
2173void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_SRAvg(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
2174 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
2175
2176 bool do_s = net->sravg_vals.do_s; // set on net at start of call..
2177
2178 float ru_act; // activation to use for updating averages
2179 if(net->learn_rule <= LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_CAL || act_avg.use_nd) {
2180 ru_act = u->act_nd;
2181 }
2182 else {
2183 ru_act = u->act;
2184 LeabraUnitSpec* rus = (LeabraUnitSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec();
2185 if(rus->act_fun == LeabraUnitSpec::SPIKE)
2186 ru_act *= rus->spike.eq_gain;
2187 }
2188
2189 if(net->learn_rule == LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_XCAL_C) {
2190 // note: this is cascade version -- each builds upon the other
2191 u->avg_ss += act_avg.ss_dt * (ru_act - u->avg_ss);
2192 float ds = act_avg.s_dt * (u->avg_ss - u->avg_s);
2193 u->avg_s += ds;
2194 u->davg += net->ct_lrn_trig.davg_dt * (ds - u->davg);
2195
2196 u->avg_m += act_avg.m_dt * (u->avg_s - u->avg_m);
2197
2198 float lval = u->avg_m; // note this is *avg_m* not act_m..
2199 if(lval > u->avg_l)
2200 u->avg_l += act_avg.l_up_dt * (lval - u->avg_l);
2201 else
2202 u->avg_l += act_avg.l_dn_dt * (lval - u->avg_l);
2203 }
2204 else {
2205 // use continuous updating so these are always current -- no need for post-average step
2206 LeabraLayerSpec* ls = (LeabraLayerSpec*)lay->GetLayerSpec();
2207 float eff_m_sum = net->sravg_vals.m_sum;
2208 if(ls->ct_inhib_mod.sravg_delay > 0) {
2209 eff_m_sum = net->sravg_vals.m_sum - (float)ls->ct_inhib_mod.sravg_delay;
2210 if(eff_m_sum < 0.0f)
2211 return; // not ready yet
2212 }
2213 if(eff_m_sum == 0.0f) {
2214 u->avg_m = ru_act;
2215 }
2216 else {
2217 u->avg_m = (ru_act + u->avg_m * eff_m_sum) / (eff_m_sum + 1.0f);
2218 }
2219 if(do_s) { // not subject to delay!
2220 if(net->sravg_vals.s_sum == 0.0f) {
2221 u->avg_s = ru_act;
2222 }
2223 else {
2224 u->avg_s = (ru_act + u->avg_s * net->sravg_vals.s_sum) / (net->sravg_vals.s_sum + 1.0f);
2225 }
2226 }
2227 }
2228
2229 if(net->learn_rule == LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_CAL || net->ct_sravg.force_con) {
2230 if(net->train_mode != LeabraNetwork::TEST) { // expensive con-level only for training
2231 for(int g=0; g<u->send.size; g++) {
2232 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)u->send.FastEl(g);
2233 LeabraLayer* rlay = (LeabraLayer*)send_gp->prjn->layer;
2234 if(rlay->lesioned() || !send_gp->size || !rlay->Compute_SRAvg_Test(net)) continue;
2235 send_gp->Compute_SRAvg(u, do_s);
2236 }
2237 }
2238 }
2239}
2240
2241void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_dWt_FirstPlus(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
2242 for(int g = 0; g < u->send.size; g++) {
2243 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)u->send.FastEl(g);
2244 LeabraLayer* rlay = (LeabraLayer*)send_gp->prjn->layer;
2245 if(rlay->lesioned() || !send_gp->size || !rlay->Compute_dWt_FirstPlus_Test(net)) continue;
2246 send_gp->Compute_Leabra_dWt(u);
2247 }
2248
2249 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
2250 if(!lay->Compute_dWt_FirstPlus_Test(net)) return; // applies to bias weights now
2251
2252 LeabraConSpec* bspc = ((LeabraConSpec*)bias_spec.SPtr());
2253 bspc->B_Compute_Leabra_dWt((LeabraCon*)u->bias.OwnCn(0), u, lay);
2254}
2255
2256void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_dWt_SecondPlus(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
2257 for(int g = 0; g < u->send.size; g++) {
2258 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)u->send.FastEl(g);
2259 LeabraLayer* rlay = (LeabraLayer*)send_gp->prjn->layer;
2260 if(rlay->lesioned() || !send_gp->size || !rlay->Compute_dWt_SecondPlus_Test(net)) continue;
2261 send_gp->Compute_Leabra_dWt(u);
2262 }
2263
2264 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
2265 if(!lay->Compute_dWt_SecondPlus_Test(net)) return; // applies to bias weights now
2266
2267 LeabraConSpec* bspc = ((LeabraConSpec*)bias_spec.SPtr());
2268 bspc->B_Compute_Leabra_dWt((LeabraCon*)u->bias.OwnCn(0), u, lay);
2269}
2270
2271void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_dWt_Nothing(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
2272 for(int g = 0; g < u->send.size; g++) {
2273 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)u->send.FastEl(g);
2274 LeabraLayer* rlay = (LeabraLayer*)send_gp->prjn->layer;
2275 if(rlay->lesioned() || !send_gp->size || !rlay->Compute_dWt_Nothing_Test(net)) continue;
2276 send_gp->Compute_Leabra_dWt(u);
2277 }
2278
2279 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
2280 if(!lay->Compute_dWt_Nothing_Test(net)) return; // applies to bias weights now
2281
2282 LeabraConSpec* bspc = ((LeabraConSpec*)bias_spec.SPtr());
2283 bspc->B_Compute_Leabra_dWt((LeabraCon*)u->bias.OwnCn(0), u, lay);
2284}
2285
2286void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_dWt_Norm(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
2287 LeabraLayer* rlay = u->own_lay();
2288 if(rlay->lesioned()) return;
2289 for(int g = 0; g < u->recv.size; g++) {
2290 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
2291 if(!recv_gp->size) continue;
2292 recv_gp->Compute_dWt_Norm(u);
2293 }
2294}
2295
2296void LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_Weights(Unit* u, Network* net, int thread_no) {
2297 LeabraUnit* lu = (LeabraUnit*)u;
2298 LeabraNetwork* lnet = (LeabraNetwork*)net;
2299
2300 if(lnet->learn_rule == LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_XCAL ||
2301 lnet->learn_rule == LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_XCAL_C) {
2302 if(lnet->epoch < lnet->ct_time.n_avg_only_epcs) { // no learning while gathering data!
2303 return;
2304 }
2305 }
2306
2307 for(int g = 0; g < lu->send.size; g++) {
2308 LeabraSendCons* send_gp = (LeabraSendCons*)lu->send.FastEl(g);
2309 LeabraLayer* rlay = (LeabraLayer*)send_gp->prjn->layer;
2310 if(rlay->lesioned() || !send_gp->size) continue;
2311 send_gp->Compute_Leabra_Weights(lu);
2312 }
2313 LeabraConSpec* bspc = ((LeabraConSpec*)bias_spec.SPtr());
2314 bspc->B_Compute_Weights((LeabraCon*)u->bias.OwnCn(0), lu);
2315}

2317///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
2318// Stats
2319
2320float LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_SSE(Unit* u, Network* net, bool& has_targ) {
2321 // just replaces act_m for act in original
2322 float sse = 0.0f;
2323 has_targ = false;
2324 LeabraUnit* lu = (LeabraUnit*)u;
2325 if(lu->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) {
2326 has_targ = true;
2327 float uerr = lu->targ - lu->act_m;
2328 if(fabsf(uerr) >= sse_tol)
2329 sse = uerr * uerr;
2330 }
2331 return sse;
2332}
2333
2334bool LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_PRerr(Unit* u, Network* net, float& true_pos, float& false_pos, float& false_neg) {
2335 // just replaces act_m for act in original
2336 true_pos = 0.0f; false_pos = 0.0f; false_neg = 0.0f;
2337 bool has_targ = false;
2338 LeabraUnit* lu = (LeabraUnit*)u;
2339 if(u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) {
2340 has_targ = true;
2341 float uerr = lu->targ - lu->act_m;
2342 if(fabsf(uerr) < sse_tol) {
2343 true_pos = lu->targ;
2344 }
2345 else {
2346 if(lu->targ > lu->act_m) {
2347 true_pos = lu->act_m;
2348 false_neg = lu->targ - lu->act_m;
2349 }
2350 else {
2351 true_pos = lu->targ;
2352 false_pos = lu->act_m - lu->targ;
2353 }
2354 }
2355 }
2356 return has_targ;
2357}
2358
2359float LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_NormErr(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
2360 if(!u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) return 0.0f;
2361
2362 if(net->on_errs) {
2363 if(u->act_m > 0.5f && u->targ < 0.5f) return 1.0f;
2364 }
2365 if(net->off_errs) {
2366 if(u->act_m < 0.5f && u->targ > 0.5f) return 1.0f;
2367 }
2368 return 0.0f;
2369}
2370
2371float LeabraUnitSpec::Compute_M2SSE(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, bool& has_targ) {
2372 float sse = 0.0f;
2373 has_targ = false;
2374 if(u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) {
2375 has_targ = true;
2376 float uerr = u->targ - u->act_m2;
2377 if(fabsf(uerr) >= sse_tol)
2378 sse = uerr * uerr;
2379 }
2380 return sse;
2381}

2386
2387void LeabraUnitSpec::BioParams(bool gelin, float norm_sec, float norm_volt, float volt_off, float norm_amp,
2388 float C_pF, float gbar_l_nS, float gbar_e_nS, float gbar_i_nS,
2389 float erev_l_mV, float erev_e_mV, float erev_i_mV,
2390 float act_thr_mV, float spk_thr_mV, float exp_slope_mV,
2391 float adapt_dt_time_ms, float adapt_vm_gain_nS, float adapt_spk_gain_nA)
2392{
2393 // derived units
2394 float norm_siemens = norm_amp / norm_volt;
2395 float norm_farad = (norm_sec * norm_amp) / norm_volt;
2396
2397 dt.vm = 1.0f / ((C_pF * 1.0e-12f) / norm_farad);
2398
2399 g_bar.l = (gbar_l_nS * 1.0e-9f) / norm_siemens;
2400 g_bar.e = (gbar_e_nS * 1.0e-9f) / norm_siemens;
2401 g_bar.i = (gbar_i_nS * 1.0e-9f) / norm_siemens;
2402
2403 e_rev.l = ((erev_l_mV * 1.0e-3f) - volt_off) / norm_volt;
2404 e_rev.e = ((erev_e_mV * 1.0e-3f) - volt_off) / norm_volt;
2405 e_rev.i = ((erev_i_mV * 1.0e-3f) - volt_off) / norm_volt;
2406
2407 act.thr = ((act_thr_mV* 1.0e-3f) - volt_off) / norm_volt;
2408 spike_misc.spk_thr = ((spk_thr_mV * 1.0e-3f) - volt_off) / norm_volt;
2409 spike_misc.exp_slope = ((exp_slope_mV * 1.0e-3f)) / norm_volt; // no off!
2410 spike_misc.vm_r = e_rev.l; // go back to leak
2411
2412 adapt.dt = 1.0f / ((adapt_dt_time_ms * 1.0e-3f) / norm_sec);
2413 adapt.vm_gain = (adapt_vm_gain_nS * 1.0e-9f) / norm_siemens;
2414 adapt.spike_gain = (adapt_spk_gain_nA * 1.0e-9f) / norm_amp;
2415
2416 v_m_init.mean = e_rev.l;
2417 vm_range.min = 0.0f;
2418 vm_range.max = 2.0f;
2419 dt.d_vm_max = 100.0f; // no max
2420
2421 if(gelin) {
2422 dt.vm = 0.3f;
2423 act.gain = 100;
2424 act.gelin = true;
2425 }
2426
2427 UpdateAfterEdit();
2428}
2429
2430void LeabraUnitSpec::GraphVmFun(DataTable* graph_data, float g_i, float min, float max, float incr) {
2431 taProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(taProject)(taProject *) GetOwner(&TA_taProject);
2432 if(!graph_data) {
2433 graph_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(name + "_VmFun", true);
2434 }
2435 int idx;
2436 graph_data->StructUpdate(true);
2437 graph_data->ResetData();
2438 DataCol* nt = graph_data->FindMakeColName("Net", idx, VT_FLOAT);
2439 DataCol* vm = graph_data->FindMakeColName("Vm", idx, VT_FLOAT);
2440
2441 incr = MAX(0.001f, incr)(((0.001f) > (incr)) ? (0.001f) : (incr)); // must be pos
2442
2443 for(float x = min; x <= max; x += incr) {
2444 float y = ((g_bar.e * x * e_rev.e) + (g_bar.i * g_i * e_rev.i) + (g_bar.l * e_rev.l)) /
2445 ((g_bar.e * x) + (g_bar.i * g_i) + g_bar.l);
2446 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
2447 nt->SetValAsFloat(x, -1);
2448 vm->SetValAsFloat(y, -1);
2449 }
2450 graph_data->StructUpdate(false);
2451 graph_data->FindMakeGraphView();
2452}
2453
2454void LeabraUnitSpec::GraphActFmVmFun(DataTable* graph_data, float min, float max, float incr) {
2455 if(TestError(act.gelin, "GraphActFmVmFun", "cannot graph act from vm when act.gelin = true, because act does not depend on vm in this case! Use GraphActFmNetFun instead."))
2456 return;
2457
2458 taProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(taProject)(taProject *) GetOwner(&TA_taProject);
2459 if(!graph_data) {
2460 graph_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(name + "_ActFmVmFun", true);
2461 }
2462 int idx;
2463 graph_data->StructUpdate(true);
2464 graph_data->ResetData();
2465 DataCol* nt = graph_data->FindMakeColName("Vm", idx, VT_FLOAT);
2466 DataCol* vm = graph_data->FindMakeColName("Act", idx, VT_FLOAT);
2467
2468 LeabraUnit un;
2469 LeabraNetwork* net = GET_MY_OWNER(LeabraNetwork)(LeabraNetwork *) GetOwner(&TA_LeabraNetwork);
2470
2471 incr = MAX(0.001f, incr)(((0.001f) > (incr)) ? (0.001f) : (incr)); // must be pos
2472 float x;
2473 for(x = min; x <= max; x += incr) {
2474 un.v_m = x;
2475 Compute_ActFmVm(&un, net);
2476 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
2477 nt->SetValAsFloat(x, -1);
2478 vm->SetValAsFloat(un.act, -1);
2479 }
2480 graph_data->StructUpdate(false);
2481 graph_data->FindMakeGraphView();
2482}
2483
2484void LeabraUnitSpec::GraphActFmNetFun(DataTable* graph_data, float g_i, float min, float max,
2485 float incr, float g_e_thr, float lin_gain) {
2486 taProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(taProject)(taProject *) GetOwner(&TA_taProject);
2487 if(!graph_data) {
2488 graph_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(name + "_ActFmNetFun", true);
2489 }
2490 int idx;
2491 graph_data->StructUpdate(true);
2492 graph_data->ResetData();
2493 DataCol* nt = graph_data->FindMakeColName("Net", idx, VT_FLOAT);
2494 DataCol* av = graph_data->FindMakeColName("Act", idx, VT_FLOAT);
2495 DataCol* lin = graph_data->FindMakeColName("Linear", idx, VT_FLOAT);
2496
2497 av->SetUserData("PLOT_1", true);
2498 av->SetUserData("MIN", 0.0f);
2499 av->SetUserData("MAX", 1.0f);
2500
2501 lin->SetUserData("PLOT_2", true);
2502
2503 LeabraNetwork* net = GET_MY_OWNER(LeabraNetwork)(LeabraNetwork *) GetOwner(&TA_LeabraNetwork);
2504
2505 incr = MAX(0.001f, incr)(((0.001f) > (incr)) ? (0.001f) : (incr)); // must be pos
2506 float x;
2507 for(x = min; x <= max; x += incr) {
2508 float aval;
2509 if(act.gelin) {
2510 aval = Compute_ActValFmVmVal_rate(x - g_e_thr);
2511 }
2512 else {
2513 float v_m = ((g_bar.e * x * e_rev.e) + (g_bar.i * g_i * e_rev.i) + (g_bar.l * e_rev.l)) /
2514 ((g_bar.e * x) + (g_bar.i * g_i) + g_bar.l);
2515 aval = Compute_ActValFmVmVal_rate(v_m - act.thr);
2516 }
2517 float ln = x - g_e_thr;
2518 if(ln < 0.0f) ln = 0.0f;
2519 ln *= lin_gain;
2520 if(ln > 1.0f) ln = 1.0f;
2521 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
2522 nt->SetValAsFloat(x, -1);
2523 av->SetValAsFloat(aval, -1);
2524 lin->SetValAsFloat(ln, -1);
2525 }
2526 graph_data->StructUpdate(false);
2527 graph_data->FindMakeGraphView();
2528}
2529
2530void LeabraUnitSpec::TimeExp(int mode, int nreps) {
2531
2532 const char* modes[6] = {"double sum", "double exp", "double exp_fast",
2533 "float sum", "float exp", "float exp_fast"};
2534
2535 TimeUsedHR tu;
2536 tu.StartTimer(true); // start, w/reset
2537 double dsum = 0.0;
2538 float fsum = 0.0f;
2539 switch (mode) {
2540 case 0: {
2541 for(int i=0;i<nreps; i++) {
2542 dsum += Random::UniformMinMax(-50.0, 50.0) - 0.99 * dsum;
2543 }
2544 break;
2545 }
2546 case 1: {
2547 for(int i=0;i<nreps; i++) {
2548 dsum += taMath_double::exp(Random::UniformMinMax(-50.0, 50.0)) - 0.99 * dsum;
2549 }
2550 break;
2551 }
2552 case 2: {
2553 for(int i=0;i<nreps; i++) {
2554 dsum += taMath_double::exp_fast(Random::UniformMinMax(-50.0, 50.0)) - 0.99 * dsum;
2555 }
2556 break;
2557 }
2558 case 3: {
2559 for(int i=0;i<nreps; i++) {
2560 fsum += Random::UniformMinMax(-50.0, 50.0) - 0.99f * fsum;
2561 }
2562 break;
2563 }
2564 case 4: {
2565 for(int i=0;i<nreps; i++) {
2566 fsum += taMath_float::exp(Random::UniformMinMax(-50.0, 50.0)) - 0.99f * fsum;
2567 }
2568 break;
2569 }
2570 case 5: {
2571 for(int i=0;i<nreps; i++) {
2572 fsum += taMath_float::exp_fast(Random::UniformMinMax(-50.0, 50.0)) - 0.99f * fsum;
2573 }
2574 break;
2575 }
2576 }
2577 tu.EndTimer();
2578 StringtaString msg;
2579 msg << "mode: " << mode << " " << modes[mode] << " seconds used: " << tu.s_used
2580 << " dsum: " << dsum << " fsum: " << fsum;
2581 taMisc::Info(msg);
2582}
2583
2584void LeabraUnitSpec::GraphSpikeAlphaFun(DataTable* graph_data, bool force_alpha) {
2585 taProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(taProject)(taProject *) GetOwner(&TA_taProject);
2586 if(!graph_data) {
2587 graph_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(name + "_SpikeAlphFun", true);
2588 }
2589 int idx;
2590 graph_data->StructUpdate(true);
2591 graph_data->ResetData();
2592 DataCol* t = graph_data->FindMakeColName("time_fm_spike", idx, VT_FLOAT);
2593 DataCol* g = graph_data->FindMakeColName("conductance", idx, VT_FLOAT);
2594
2595 float tmax = MAX(spike.window, 2.0f)(((spike.window) > (2.0f)) ? (spike.window) : (2.0f));
2596
2597 float sumg = 0.0f;
2598 float x;
2599 if(!force_alpha && spike.rise == 0.0f && spike.decay > 0.0f) {
2600 float net = 0.0f;
2601 float input;
2602 tmax = 20.0f;
2603 for(x = 0.0f; x <= tmax; x += 1.0f) {
2604 if(x < spike.window)
2605 input = spike.gg_decay / (float)spike.window;
2606 else
2607 input = 0.0f;
2608 net = net + input - net / spike.decay;
2609 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
2610 t->SetValAsFloat(x, -1);
2611 g->SetValAsFloat(net, -1);
2612 sumg += net;
2613 }
2614 }
2615 else {
2616 for(x = 0.0f; x <= tmax; x += 1.0f) {
2617 float y = spike.ComputeAlpha(x);
2618 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
2619 t->SetValAsFloat(x, -1);
2620 g->SetValAsFloat(y, -1);
2621 sumg += y;
2622 }
2623 }
2624 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
2625 t->SetValAsFloat(x, -1);
2626 g->SetValAsFloat(0.0f, -1);
2627 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
2628 t->SetValAsFloat(x+1.0f, -1);
2629 g->SetValAsFloat(sumg, -1);
2630 graph_data->StructUpdate(false);
2631 graph_data->FindMakeGraphView();
2632}

2742 spike_i_buf = NULL__null;

2752bool LeabraUnit::BuildUnits() {
2753 bool rval = inherited::BuildUnits();
2754 if(!rval) return false;
2755 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)GetUnitSpec();
2756 if(us) {
2757 us->Init_SpikeBuff(this);
2758 us->Init_ActBuff(this);
2759 }
2760 return rval;
2761}
2762
2763void LeabraUnit::GetInSubGp() {
2764 Unit_Group* ownr = (Unit_Group*)owner;
2765 if((ownr != NULL__null) && (ownr->owner != NULL__null) && ownr->owner->InheritsFrom(TA_taSubGroup))
2766 in_subgp = true;
2767 else
2768 in_subgp = false;
2769}
2770
2771void LeabraUnit::Copy_(const LeabraUnit& cp) {
2772 act_eq = cp.act_eq;
2773 act_nd = cp.act_nd;
2774 act_avg = cp.act_avg;

3069
3070bool LeabraLayerSpec::CheckConfig_Layer(Layer* ly, bool quiet) {
3071 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)ly;
3072 bool rval = true;
3073
3074 LeabraNetwork* net = (LeabraNetwork*)lay->own_net;
3075 if(net && net->learn_rule >= LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_CAL) {
3076 if(TestWarning(decay.phase == 1.0f,
3077 "LeabraLayerSpec decay.phase should be 0 or small for for CTLEABRA_X/CAL -- I just set it to 0 for you in spec:", name)) {
3078 SetUnique("decay", true);
3079 decay.phase = 0.0f;
3080 }
3081 }
3082
3083 if(lay->CheckError(!lay->projections.el_base->InheritsFrom(&TA_LeabraPrjn), quiet, rval,
3084 "does not have LeabraPrjn projection base type!",
3085 "project must be updated and projections remade"))
3086 return false;
3087 bool has_rel_net_conspec = false;
3088 for(int i=0;i<lay->projections.size;i++) {
3089 Projection* prjn = (Projection*)lay->projections[i];
3090 lay->CheckError(!prjn->InheritsFrom(&TA_LeabraPrjn), quiet, rval,
3091 "does not have LeabraPrjn projection base type!",
3092 "Projection must be re-made");
3093 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)prjn->con_spec.GetSpec();
3094 if(cs && cs->rel_net_adapt.on) has_rel_net_conspec = true;
3095 }
3096 if(has_rel_net_conspec) {
3097 // check for total trg_netin_rel
3098 float sum_trg_netin_rel = 0.0f;
3099 for(int i=0;i<lay->projections.size;i++) {
3100 LeabraPrjn* prjn = (LeabraPrjn*)lay->projections[i];
3101 sum_trg_netin_rel += prjn->trg_netin_rel;
3102 }
3103 lay->CheckError((fabsf(sum_trg_netin_rel - 1.0f) > .001f), quiet, rval,
3104 "sum of trg_netin_rel values for layer:",StringtaString(sum_trg_netin_rel),
3105 "!= 1.0 -- must fix!");
3106 }
3107
3108 lay->CheckError((inhib_group == UNIT_GROUPS && !lay->unit_groups), quiet, rval,
3109 "inhib_group is UNIT_GROUPS but layer is not set to use unit_groups! will not work.");
3110
3111 return rval;
3112}
3113
3114void LeabraLayerSpec::HelpConfig() {
3115 StringtaString help = "LeabraLayerSpec Configuration:\n\
3116The layer spec sets the target level of activity, k, for each layer. \
3117Therefore, you must have a different layer spec with an appropriate activity \
3118level for layers that have different activity levels. Note that if you set \
3119the activity level by percent this will work for different sized layers that \
3120have the same percent activity level.";
3121 taMisc::Confirm(help);
3122}

3124LeabraLayer* LeabraLayerSpec::FindLayerFmSpec(LeabraLayer* lay, int& prjn_idx, TypeDef* layer_spec) {
3125 LeabraLayer* rval = NULL__null;
3126 prjn_idx = -1;
3127 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(Projection, p, lay->projections)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (Projection *p = (Projection
*) (lay->projections).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); p; p = (Projection
*) (lay->projections).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
3128 LeabraLayer* fmlay = (LeabraLayer*)p->from.ptr();
3129 if(fmlay->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(layer_spec)) { // inherits - not excact match!
3130 prjn_idx = p->recv_idx;
3131 rval = fmlay;
3132 break;
3133 }
3134 }
3135 return rval;
3136}
3137
3138LeabraLayer* LeabraLayerSpec::FindLayerFmSpecExact(LeabraLayer* lay, int& prjn_idx, TypeDef* layer_spec) {
3139 LeabraLayer* rval = NULL__null;
3140 prjn_idx = -1;
3141 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(Projection, p, lay->projections)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (Projection *p = (Projection
*) (lay->projections).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); p; p = (Projection
*) (lay->projections).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
3142 LeabraLayer* fmlay = (LeabraLayer*)p->from.ptr();
3143 if(fmlay->spec.SPtr()->GetTypeDef() == layer_spec) { // not inherits - excact match!
3144 prjn_idx = p->recv_idx;
3145 rval = fmlay;
3146 break;
3147 }
3148 }
3149 return rval;
3150}

3152LeabraLayer* LeabraLayerSpec::FindLayerFmSpecNet(Network* net, TypeDef* layer_spec) {
3153 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, net->layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (net->layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay
= (LeabraLayer*) (net->layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
3154 if(lay->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(layer_spec)) { // inherits - not excact match!

3195void LeabraLayerSpec::Init_Weights(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3196 lay->BuildKwtaBuffs(); // make sure kwta buffs are rebuilt!
3197 Compute_Active_K(lay, net); // need kwta.pct for init
3198 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
3199 u->Init_Weights(net);
3200 }
3201 if(lay->unit_groups) {
3202 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
3203 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
3204 gpd->Init_State();
3205 }
3206 }
3207 Init_Inhib(lay, net); // initialize inhibition at start..
3208 Init_Stats(lay, net);
3209}
3210
3211void LeabraLayerSpec::Init_Inhib(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3212 lay->adapt_i.avg_avg = lay->kwta.pct;
3213 lay->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt = inhib.kwta_pt;
3214 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
3215 lay->adapt_i.g_bar_i = us->g_bar.i;
3216 lay->adapt_i.g_bar_l = us->g_bar.l;
3217 if(lay->unit_groups) {
3218 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
3219 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
3220 gpd->adapt_i.avg_avg = gpd->kwta.pct;
3221 if(((inhib.type == LeabraInhibSpec::AVG_MAX_PT_INHIB)
3222 || (inhib.type == LeabraInhibSpec::MAX_INHIB))
3223 && (inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER))
3224 gpd->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt = inhib.gp_pt;
3225 else
3226 gpd->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt = inhib.kwta_pt;
3227 gpd->adapt_i.g_bar_i = us->g_bar.i;
3228 gpd->adapt_i.g_bar_l = us->g_bar.l;
3229 }
3230 }
3231}

3261void LeabraLayerSpec::Init_Acts(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3262 lay->ext_flag = Unit::NO_EXTERNAL;
3263 lay->hard_clamped = false;
3264 lay->ResetSortBuf();
3265 if(lay->units.leaves == 0) return; // may not be built yet!
3266

3268 lay->Inhib_Init_Acts(this);
3269 if(lay->unit_groups) {
3270 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
3271 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
3272 gpd->Inhib_Init_Acts(this);
