3274 }
3275 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
3276 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
3277 u->Init_Acts(net);
3278 }
3279}

3330 u->noise = 0.0f;

3367///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
3368// SettleInit -- at start of settling
3369
3370void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Active_K(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3371 if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && lay->unit_groups) {
3372 int totk = 0;
3373 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
3374 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
3375 Compute_Active_K_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, gp_kwta);
3376 totk += gpd->kwta.k;
3377 }
3378 if(inhib_group == UNIT_GROUPS) {
3379 if(lay->kwta.k != totk) {
3380 lay->lay_kbuffs.ResetAllBuffs();
3381 lay->Inhib_ResetSortBuf();
3382 }
3383 lay->kwta.k = totk;
3384 lay->kwta.Compute_Pct(lay->units.leaves);
3385 if(gp_kwta.diff_act_pct)
3386 lay->kwta.pct = gp_kwta.act_pct; // override!!
3387 if(unit_gp_inhib.on && unit_gp_inhib.diff_act_pct)
3388 lay->kwta.pct *= unit_gp_inhib.act_pct_mult;
3389 }
3390 }
3391 if(inhib_group != UNIT_GROUPS) {
3392 Compute_Active_K_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, kwta);
3393 if(kwta.diff_act_pct)
3394 lay->kwta.pct = kwta.act_pct; // override!!
3395 }
3396 if(lay_gp_inhib.on && lay_gp_inhib.diff_act_pct)
3397 lay->kwta.pct *= lay_gp_inhib.act_pct_mult;
3398}
3399
3400void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Active_K_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
3401 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
3402 LeabraInhib* thr, KWTASpec& kwtspec)
3403{
3404 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
3405 int new_k = 0;
3406 if(kwtspec.k_from == KWTASpec::USE_PCT)
3407 new_k = (int)(kwtspec.pct * (float)nunits);
3408 else if((kwtspec.k_from == KWTASpec::USE_PAT_K) &&
3409 (lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP | Unit::EXT)))
3410 new_k = Compute_Pat_K(lay, acc_md, gpidx, thr);
3411 else
3412 new_k = kwtspec.k;
3413
3414 if(inhib.type == LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_INHIB)
3415 new_k = MIN(nunits - 1, new_k)(((nunits - 1) < (new_k)) ? (nunits - 1) : (new_k));
3416 else
3417 new_k = MIN(nunits, new_k)(((nunits) < (new_k)) ? (nunits) : (new_k));
3418 new_k = MAX(1, new_k)(((1) > (new_k)) ? (1) : (new_k));
3419
3420 if(thr->kwta.k != new_k) {
3421 KwtaSortBuff_List* srtbuff = lay->SortBuffList(acc_md);
3422 srtbuff->ResetAllBuffs();
3423 thr->Inhib_ResetSortBuf();
3424 }
3425
3426 thr->kwta.k = new_k;
3427 thr->kwta.Compute_Pct(nunits);
3428}
3429
3430int LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Pat_K(LeabraLayer* lay,
3431 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
3432 LeabraInhib* thr) {
3433 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
3434 bool use_comp = false;
3435 if(lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::COMP)) // only use comparison vals if entire lay is COMP!
3436 use_comp = true;
3437 int pat_k = 0;
3438 for(int i=0; i<nunits; i++) {
3439 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
3440 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
3441 // use either EXT or TARG information...
3442 if(u->HasExtFlag(Unit::EXT)) {
3443 if(u->ext >= kwta.pat_q)
3444 pat_k++;
3445 }
3446 else if(u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG)) {
3447 if(u->targ >= kwta.pat_q)
3448 pat_k++;
3449 }
3450 else if(use_comp && u->HasExtFlag(Unit::COMP)) {
3451 if(u->targ >= kwta.pat_q)
3452 pat_k++;
3453 }
3454 }
3455 return pat_k;
3456}

3478void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_HardClampPhase2(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3479 // special case to speed up processing by clamping 2nd plus phase to prior + phase
3480 lay->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
3481 lay->hard_clamped = true;
3482 lay->Inhib_SetVals(inhib.kwta_pt); // assume 0 - 1 clamped inputs
3483
3484 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
3485 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
3486 u->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
3487 u->ext = u->act_p;
3488 u->Compute_HardClampNoClip(net); // important: uses no clip here: not really external values!
3489 }
3490 Compute_CycleStats(lay, net); // compute once only now
3491}
3492
3493void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_HardClamp(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3494 if(decay.clamp_phase2 && (net->phase != LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE) && (net->phase_no >= 2)) {
3495 Compute_HardClampPhase2(lay, net);
3496 return;
3497 }
3498 if(!(clamp.hard && lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::EXT))) {
3499 lay->hard_clamped = false;
3500 return;
3501 }
3502 lay->hard_clamped = true; // cache this flag
3503 lay->Inhib_SetVals(inhib.kwta_pt); // assume 0 - 1 clamped inputs
3504
3505 if(clamp.max_plus && net->phase == LeabraNetwork::PLUS_PHASE && net->phase_no > 0 &&
3506 lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG)) {
3507 float min_max = lay->acts_m.max;
3508 float clmp = min_max + clamp.plus;
3509 clmp = MAX(clmp, clamp.min_clamp)(((clmp) > (clamp.min_clamp)) ? (clmp) : (clamp.min_clamp)
);
3510
3511 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
3512 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
3513 u->ext *= clmp; // modify!
3514 }
3515 }
3516
3517 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
3518 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
3519 u->Compute_HardClamp(net);
3520 }
3521 Compute_CycleStats(lay, net); // compute once only
3522}

*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)

3546///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
3547// Cycle Step 1: Netinput
3548
3549void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_NetinStats_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
3550 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
3551 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3552 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
3553 thr->netin.InitVals(); thr->i_thrs.InitVals();
3554 for(int i=0; i<nunits; i++) {
3555 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
3556 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
3557 thr->netin.UpdtVals(u->net, i); thr->i_thrs.UpdtVals(u->i_thr, i);
3558 }
3559 thr->netin.CalcAvg(nunits); thr->i_thrs.CalcAvg(nunits);
3560
3561 if(thr->netin_top_k.cmpt) {
3562 thr->netin_top_k.InitVals();
3563 int k_eff = thr->kwta.k; // keep cutoff at k
3564 KwtaSortBuff* act_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::ACTIVE);
3565 if(k_eff <= 0 || act_buff->Size(gpidx) != k_eff)
3566 return; // no can do
3567
3568 for(int j=0; j < k_eff; j++) {
3569 thr->netin_top_k.UpdtVals(act_buff->Un(j, gpidx)->net, j);
3570 }
3571 thr->netin_top_k.CalcAvg(k_eff);
3572 }
3573}
3574
3575void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_NetinStats(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3576 if(lay->hard_clamped) return;
3577
3578 if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && lay->unit_groups) {
3579 lay->netin.InitVals(); lay->i_thrs.InitVals();
3580 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(Layer::ACC_GP);
3581 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
3582 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
3583 Compute_NetinStats_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net);
3584 lay->netin.UpdtFmAvgMax(gpd->netin, nunits, g);
3585 lay->i_thrs.UpdtFmAvgMax(gpd->i_thrs, nunits, g);
3586 lay->netin_top_k.UpdtFmAvgMax(gpd->netin_top_k, 1, g); // only compute gp-wise avg for avg top k (n=1 per group)
3587 }
3588 lay->netin.CalcAvg(lay->units.leaves);
3589 lay->i_thrs.CalcAvg(lay->units.leaves);
3590 lay->netin_top_k.CalcAvg(lay->gp_geom.n);
3591 }
3592 else {
3593 Compute_NetinStats_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
3594 }
3595}

3597///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
3598// Cycle Step 2: Inhibition, Basic computation
3599
3600void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3601 if(lay->hard_clamped) return; // say no more..
3602
3603 if(inhib_group != UNIT_GROUPS) {
3604 Compute_Inhib_impl(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net, inhib);
3605 }
3606 if(lay->unit_groups) {
3607 if(inhib_group == UNIT_GROUPS) {
3608 lay->Inhib_SetVals(0.0f);
3609 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
3610 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
3611 Compute_Inhib_impl(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net, inhib);
3612 float gp_g_i = gpd->i_val.g_i;
3613 if(unit_gp_inhib.on)
3614 gp_g_i *= unit_gp_inhib.gp_g;
3615 lay->i_val.g_i = MAX(lay->i_val.g_i, gp_g_i)(((lay->i_val.g_i) > (gp_g_i)) ? (lay->i_val.g_i) : (
gp_g_i));
3616 }
3617 }
3618 else if(inhib_group == LAY_AND_GPS) {
3619 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
3620 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
3621 Compute_Inhib_impl(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net, inhib);
3622 }
3623 }
3624 Compute_LayInhibToGps(lay, net);
3625 }
3626
3627 Compute_CtDynamicInhib(lay, net);
3628}
3629
3630void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_impl(LeabraLayer* lay,
3631 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
3632 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net, LeabraInhibSpec& ispec) {
3633 if(ispec.type == LeabraInhibSpec::UNIT_INHIB) {
3634 thr->i_val.g_i = 0.0f; // make sure it's zero, cuz this gets added to units..
3635 }
3636 else {
3637 switch(ispec.type) {
3638 case LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_INHIB:
3639 Compute_Inhib_kWTA(lay, acc_md, gpidx, thr, net, ispec);
3640 break;
3641 case LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_AVG_INHIB:
3642 Compute_Inhib_kWTA_Avg(lay, acc_md, gpidx, thr, net, ispec);
3643 break;
3644 case LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_KV2K:
3645 Compute_Inhib_kWTA_kv2k(lay, acc_md, gpidx, thr, net, ispec);
3646 break;
3647 case LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_COMP_COST:
3648 Compute_Inhib_kWTA_CompCost(lay, acc_md, gpidx, thr, net, ispec);
3649 break;
3650 case LeabraInhibSpec::AVG_MAX_PT_INHIB:
3651 Compute_Inhib_AvgMaxPt(lay, acc_md, gpidx, thr, net, ispec);
3652 break;
3653 case LeabraInhibSpec::MAX_INHIB:
3654 Compute_Inhib_Max(lay, acc_md, gpidx, thr, net, ispec);
3655 break;
3656 case LeabraInhibSpec::AVG_NET_ACT:
3657 Compute_Inhib_AvgNetAct(lay, acc_md, gpidx, thr, net, ispec);
3658 break;
3659 case LeabraInhibSpec::UNIT_INHIB:
3660 break;
3661 }
3662 thr->i_val.g_i = thr->i_val.kwta;
3663 }
3664
3665 thr->i_val.g_i_orig = thr->i_val.g_i; // retain original values..
3666}
3667
3668// basic sorting function:
3669
3670void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_kWTA_Sort(LeabraLayer* lay, Layer::AccessMode acc_md,
3671 int gpidx, int nunits, LeabraInhib* thr,
3672 KwtaSortBuff& act_buff, KwtaSortBuff& inact_buff,
3673 int& k_eff, float& k_net, int& k_idx) {
3674 LeabraUnit* u;
3675 int j;
3676 if(act_buff.Size(gpidx) != k_eff) { // need to fill the sort buf..
3677 act_buff.ResetGp(gpidx);
3678 int end_j = k_eff;
3679 for(j=0; j < end_j; j++) {
3680 u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, j, gpidx);
3681 if(u->lesioned()) {
3682 end_j++;
3683 if(end_j >= nunits) {
3684 k_eff = act_buff.Size(gpidx); // this may not end well really..
3685 break;
3686 }
3687 continue;
3688 }
3689 act_buff.Add(u, gpidx); // add to list
3690 if(u->i_thr < k_net) {
3691 k_net = u->i_thr; k_idx = act_buff.Size(gpidx)-1;
3692 }
3693 }
3694 inact_buff.ResetGp(gpidx);
3695 // now, use the "replace-the-lowest" sorting technique
3696 for(; j < nunits; j++) {
3697 u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, j, gpidx);
3698 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
3699 if(u->i_thr <= k_net) { // not bigger than smallest one in sort buffer
3700 inact_buff.Add(u, gpidx);
3701 continue;
3702 }
3703 inact_buff.Add(act_buff.Un(k_idx, gpidx), gpidx); // now inactive
3704 act_buff.Set(u, k_idx, gpidx); // replace the smallest with it
3705 k_net = u->i_thr; // assume its the smallest
3706 for(int b=0; b < k_eff; b++) { // and recompute the actual smallest
3707 float tmp = act_buff.Un(b, gpidx)->i_thr;
3708 if(tmp < k_net) {
3709 k_net = tmp; k_idx = b;
3710 }
3711 }
3712 }
3713 }
3714 else { // keep the ones around from last time, find k_net
3715 for(j=0; j < k_eff; j++) { // these should be the top ones, very fast!!
3716 float tmp = act_buff.Un(j, gpidx)->i_thr;
3717 if(tmp < k_net) {
3718 k_net = tmp; k_idx = j;
3719 }
3720 }
3721 // now, use the "replace-the-lowest" sorting technique (on the inact_list)
3722 int iabsz = inact_buff.Size(gpidx);
3723 for(j=0; j < iabsz; j++) {
3724 u = inact_buff.Un(j, gpidx);
3725 if(u->i_thr <= k_net) // not bigger than smallest one in sort buffer
3726 continue;
3727 inact_buff.Set(act_buff.Un(k_idx, gpidx), j, gpidx); // now inactive
3728 act_buff.Set(u, k_idx, gpidx); // replace the smallest with it
3729 k_net = u->i_thr; // assume its the smallest
3730 for(int b=0; b < k_eff; b++) { // and recompute the actual smallest
3731 float tmp = act_buff.Un(b, gpidx)->i_thr;
3732 if(tmp < k_net) {
3733 k_net = tmp; k_idx = b;
3734 }
3735 }
3736 }
3737 }
3738}
3739
3740void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_BreakTie(LeabraInhib* thr) {
3741 if(thr->kwta.k_ithr > 0.0f)
3742 thr->kwta.ithr_diff = (thr->kwta.k_ithr - thr->kwta.k1_ithr) / thr->kwta.k_ithr;
3743 else
3744 thr->kwta.ithr_diff = 0.0f;
3745 thr->kwta.tie_brk = 0;
3746 if(tie_brk.on && (thr->kwta.k_ithr > tie_brk.k_thr)) {
3747 if(thr->kwta.ithr_diff < tie_brk.diff_thr) {
3748 // we now have an official tie: break it by reducing firing of "others"
3749 thr->kwta.tie_brk = 1;
3750 thr->kwta.tie_brk_gain = (tie_brk.diff_thr - thr->kwta.ithr_diff) / tie_brk.diff_thr;
3751 thr->kwta.k1_ithr *= (1.0f - thr->kwta.tie_brk_gain * tie_brk.thr_gain);
3752 thr->kwta.eff_loser_gain = 1.0f + (tie_brk.loser_gain * thr->kwta.tie_brk_gain);
3753 }
3754 }
3755}
3756
3757// actual kwta impls:
3758
3759void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_kWTA(LeabraLayer* lay,
3760 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
3761 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net, LeabraInhibSpec& ispec) {
3762 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
3763 if(nunits <= 1) { // this is undefined
3764 thr->Inhib_SetVals(ispec.kwta_pt);
3765 return;
3766 }
3767
3768 int k_plus_1 = thr->kwta.k + 1; // expand cutoff to include N+1th one
3769 k_plus_1 = MIN(nunits, k_plus_1)(((nunits) < (k_plus_1)) ? (nunits) : (k_plus_1));
3770 float k1_net = FLT_MAX3.40282347e+38F;
3771 int k1_idx = 0;
3772
3773 KwtaSortBuff* act_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::ACTIVE);
3774 KwtaSortBuff* inact_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::INACT);
3775
3776 Compute_Inhib_kWTA_Sort(lay, acc_md, gpidx, nunits, thr,
3777 *act_buff, *inact_buff, k_plus_1, k1_net, k1_idx);
3778
3779 if(k_plus_1 <= 1) { // something bad happened
3780 thr->Inhib_SetVals(ispec.kwta_pt);
3781 return;
3782 }
3783
3784 // active_buf now has k+1 most active units, get the next-highest one
3785 int k_idx = -1;
3786 float net_k = FLT_MAX3.40282347e+38F;
3787 for(int j=0; j < k_plus_1; j++) {
3788 float tmp = act_buff->Un(j, gpidx)->i_thr;
3789 if((tmp < net_k) && (j != k1_idx)) {
3790 net_k = tmp; k_idx = j;
3791 }
3792 }
3793 if(k_idx == -1) { // we didn't find the next one
3794 k_idx = k1_idx;
3795 net_k = k1_net;
Value stored to 'net_k' is never read
3796 }
3797
3798 LeabraUnit* k1_u = act_buff->Un(k1_idx, gpidx);
3799 LeabraUnit* k_u = act_buff->Un(k_idx, gpidx);
3800
3801 float k1_i = k1_u->i_thr;
3802 float k_i = k_u->i_thr;
3803 thr->kwta.k_ithr = k_i;
3804 thr->kwta.k1_ithr = k1_i;
3805
3806 Compute_Inhib_BreakTie(thr);
3807
3808 // place kwta inhibition between k and k+1
3809 float nw_gi;
3810 if(inhib.low0)
3811 nw_gi = ispec.kwta_pt * thr->kwta.k_ithr;
3812 else
3813 nw_gi = thr->kwta.k1_ithr + ispec.kwta_pt * (thr->kwta.k_ithr - thr->kwta.k1_ithr);
3814 nw_gi = MAX(nw_gi, ispec.min_i)(((nw_gi) > (ispec.min_i)) ? (nw_gi) : (ispec.min_i));
3815 thr->i_val.kwta = nw_gi;
3816 thr->kwta.Compute_IThrR();
3817}
3818
3819void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_kWTA_Avg(LeabraLayer* lay,
3820 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
3821 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net, LeabraInhibSpec& ispec) {
3822 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
3823 if(nunits <= 1) { // this is undefined
3824 thr->Inhib_SetVals(ispec.kwta_pt);
3825 return;
3826 }
3827
3828 int k_eff = thr->kwta.k; // keep cutoff at k
3829 float k_net = FLT_MAX3.40282347e+38F;
3830 int k_idx = 0;
3831
3832 KwtaSortBuff* act_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::ACTIVE);
3833 KwtaSortBuff* inact_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::INACT);
3834
3835 Compute_Inhib_kWTA_Sort(lay, acc_md, gpidx, nunits, thr,
3836 *act_buff, *inact_buff, k_eff, k_net, k_idx);
3837
3838 if(k_eff <= 0) { // something bad happened
3839 thr->Inhib_SetVals(ispec.kwta_pt);
3840 return;
3841 }
3842
3843 // active_buf now has k most active units, get averages of both groups
3844 int j;
3845 float k_avg = 0.0f;
3846 for(j=0; j < k_eff; j++)
3847 k_avg += act_buff->Un(j, gpidx)->i_thr;
3848 k_avg /= (float)k_eff;
3849
3850 float oth_avg = 0.0f;
3851 int iabsz = inact_buff->Size(gpidx);
3852 for(j=0; j < iabsz; j++)
3853 oth_avg += inact_buff->Un(j, gpidx)->i_thr;
3854 if(iabsz > 0)
3855 oth_avg /= (float)iabsz;
3856
3857 // place kwta inhibition between two averages
3858 // this uses the adapting point!
3859 float pt = ispec.kwta_pt;
3860 if(adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::KWTA_PT)
3861 pt = thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt;
3862 thr->kwta.k_ithr = k_avg;
3863 thr->kwta.k1_ithr = oth_avg;
3864
3865 Compute_Inhib_BreakTie(thr);
3866
3867 float nw_gi;
3868 if(inhib.low0)
3869 nw_gi = pt * thr->kwta.k_ithr;
3870 else
3871 nw_gi = thr->kwta.k1_ithr + pt * (thr->kwta.k_ithr - thr->kwta.k1_ithr);
3872
3873 nw_gi = MAX(nw_gi, ispec.min_i)(((nw_gi) > (ispec.min_i)) ? (nw_gi) : (ispec.min_i));
3874 thr->i_val.kwta = nw_gi;
3875 thr->kwta.Compute_IThrR();
3876}
3877
3878void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_kWTA_kv2k(LeabraLayer* lay,
3879 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
3880 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net, LeabraInhibSpec& ispec) {
3881 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
3882 if(nunits <= 1) { // this is undefined
3883 thr->Inhib_SetVals(ispec.kwta_pt);
3884 return;
3885 }
3886
3887 int k_eff = thr->kwta.k;
3888 float k_net = FLT_MAX3.40282347e+38F;
3889 int k_idx = 0;
3890
3891 KwtaSortBuff* act_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::ACTIVE);
3892 KwtaSortBuff* inact_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::INACT);
3893
3894 Compute_Inhib_kWTA_Sort(lay, acc_md, gpidx, nunits, thr,
3895 *act_buff, *inact_buff, k_eff, k_net, k_idx);
3896
3897 if(k_eff <= 0) { // something bad happened
3898 thr->Inhib_SetVals(ispec.kwta_pt);
3899 return;
3900 }
3901
3902 // active_buf now has k most active units, get average from act buf
3903 int j;
3904 float oth_avg = 0.0f;
3905 float k_avg = 0.0f;
3906 for(j=0; j < k_eff; j++)
3907 k_avg += act_buff->Un(j, gpidx)->i_thr;
3908 k_avg /= (float)k_eff;
3909
3910 int k2_eff = 2 * thr->kwta.k;
3911 if(k2_eff >= nunits) {
3912 // just use inact buf: same as kwta_avg in this case..
3913 int iabsz = inact_buff->Size(gpidx);
3914 for(j=0; j < iabsz; j++)
3915 oth_avg += inact_buff->Un(j, gpidx)->i_thr;
3916 if(iabsz > 0)
3917 oth_avg /= (float)iabsz;
3918 }
3919 else {
3920 // find 2k guys
3921 float k2_net = FLT_MAX3.40282347e+38F;
3922 int k2_idx = 0;
3923
3924 KwtaSortBuff* act_buff2k = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::ACTIVE_2K);
3925 KwtaSortBuff* inact_buff2k = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::INACT_2K);
3926
3927 Compute_Inhib_kWTA_Sort(lay, acc_md, gpidx, nunits, thr,
3928 *act_buff2k, *inact_buff2k, k2_eff, k2_net, k2_idx);
3929
3930 if(k2_eff <= 0) { // something bad happened
3931 thr->Inhib_SetVals(ispec.kwta_pt);
3932 return;
3933 }
3934
3935 for(j=0; j < k2_eff; j++)
3936 oth_avg += act_buff2k->Un(j, gpidx)->i_thr;
3937 oth_avg /= (float)k2_eff;
3938 }
3939
3940 // place kwta inhibition between two averages
3941 // this uses the adapting point!
3942 float pt = ispec.kwta_pt;
3943 if(adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::KWTA_PT)
3944 pt = thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt;
3945 thr->kwta.k_ithr = k_avg;
3946 thr->kwta.k1_ithr = oth_avg;
3947
3948 Compute_Inhib_BreakTie(thr);
3949
3950 float nw_gi = thr->kwta.k1_ithr + pt * (thr->kwta.k_ithr - thr->kwta.k1_ithr);
3951 nw_gi = MAX(nw_gi, ispec.min_i)(((nw_gi) > (ispec.min_i)) ? (nw_gi) : (ispec.min_i));
3952 thr->i_val.kwta = nw_gi;
3953 thr->kwta.Compute_IThrR();
3954}
3955
3956void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_kWTA_CompCost(LeabraLayer* lay,
3957 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
3958 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net, LeabraInhibSpec& ispec) {
3959 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
3960 if(nunits <= 1) { // this is undefined
3961 thr->Inhib_SetVals(ispec.kwta_pt);
3962 return;
3963 }
3964
3965 int k_eff = thr->kwta.k; // keep cutoff at k
3966 float k_net = FLT_MAX3.40282347e+38F;
3967 int k_idx = 0;
3968
3969 KwtaSortBuff* act_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::ACTIVE);
3970 KwtaSortBuff* inact_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::INACT);
3971
3972 Compute_Inhib_kWTA_Sort(lay, acc_md, gpidx, nunits, thr,
3973 *act_buff, *inact_buff, k_eff, k_net, k_idx);
3974
3975 if(k_eff <= 0) { // something bad happened
3976 thr->Inhib_SetVals(ispec.kwta_pt);
3977 return;
3978 }
3979
3980 LeabraUnit* k_u = act_buff->Un(k_idx, gpidx);
3981 float k_ithr = k_u->i_thr;
3982
3983 float oth_sum = 0.0f;
3984 int iabsz = inact_buff->Size(gpidx);
3985 for(int j=0; j < iabsz; j++) {
3986 float oth_nrm = inact_buff->Un(j,gpidx)->i_thr / k_ithr;
3987 if(oth_nrm >= ispec.comp_thr)
3988 oth_sum += oth_nrm;
3989 }
3990 if(iabsz > 0)
3991 oth_sum /= (float)iabsz;
3992
3993 float pt = ispec.kwta_pt;
3994// if(adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::KWTA_PT) // this is not correct: adapt goes the wrong way!
3995// pt = thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt;
3996
3997 float nw_gi = k_ithr - pt * (1.0f - ispec.comp_gain * oth_sum);
3998
3999 thr->kwta.k_ithr = k_ithr;
4000 thr->kwta.k1_ithr = nw_gi;
4001
4002// Compute_Inhib_BreakTie(thr); // not applicable!
4003
4004 nw_gi = MAX(nw_gi, ispec.min_i)(((nw_gi) > (ispec.min_i)) ? (nw_gi) : (ispec.min_i));
4005 thr->i_val.kwta = nw_gi;
4006 thr->kwta.Compute_IThrR();
4007}
4008
4009void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_AvgMaxPt(LeabraLayer* lay,
4010 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4011 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net, LeabraInhibSpec& ispec) {
4012 float pt = ispec.kwta_pt;
4013 if(adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::KWTA_PT)
4014 pt = thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt;
4015 else if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && ((LeabraInhib*)lay != thr))
4016 pt = ispec.gp_pt; // use sub-group version for sub-groups..
4017
4018 float oth_avg = thr->i_thrs.avg; // put between the avg
4019 float k_avg = thr->i_thrs.max; // and the max..
4020
4021 float nw_gi = oth_avg + pt * (k_avg - oth_avg);
4022 nw_gi = MAX(nw_gi, ispec.min_i)(((nw_gi) > (ispec.min_i)) ? (nw_gi) : (ispec.min_i));
4023 thr->i_val.kwta = nw_gi;
4024 thr->kwta.k_ithr = k_avg;
4025 thr->kwta.k1_ithr = oth_avg;
4026 thr->kwta.Compute_IThrR();
4027}
4028
4029void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_Max(LeabraLayer* lay,
4030 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4031 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net, LeabraInhibSpec& ispec) {
4032 float pt = ispec.kwta_pt;
4033 if(adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::KWTA_PT)
4034 pt = thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt;
4035 else if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && ((LeabraInhib*)lay != thr))
4036 pt = ispec.gp_pt; // use sub-group version for sub-groups..
4037
4038 float k_avg = thr->i_thrs.max; // and the max..
4039 float nw_gi = k_avg - pt;
4040 nw_gi = MAX(nw_gi, ispec.min_i)(((nw_gi) > (ispec.min_i)) ? (nw_gi) : (ispec.min_i));
4041 thr->i_val.kwta = nw_gi;
4042 thr->kwta.k_ithr = k_avg;
4043 thr->kwta.k1_ithr = nw_gi;
4044 thr->kwta.Compute_IThrR();
4045}
4046
4047void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Inhib_AvgNetAct(LeabraLayer* lay,
4048 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4049 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net, LeabraInhibSpec& ispec) {
4050 float pt = ispec.kwta_pt;
4051 if(adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::KWTA_PT)
4052 pt = thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt;
4053 else if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && ((LeabraInhib*)lay != thr))
4054 pt = ispec.gp_pt; // use sub-group version for sub-groups..
4055
4056 float eff_act_gain = ispec.act_gain;
4057 if(thr->acts_iavg.avg > thr->kwta.pct)
4058 eff_act_gain *= ispec.kink_gain;
4059
4060 float nw_gi = thr->netin.avg * ispec.net_gain + thr->acts_iavg.avg * eff_act_gain;
4061 nw_gi *= pt; // pt is basic overall multiplier
4062
4063 thr->i_val.kwta = nw_gi;
4064 thr->kwta.k_ithr = nw_gi;
4065 thr->kwta.k1_ithr = nw_gi;
4066 thr->kwta.Compute_IThrR();
4067}
4068
4069void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_CtDynamicInhib(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4070 if(net->learn_rule == LeabraNetwork::LEABRA_CHL) return;
4071
4072 float bi = net->ct_sin_i.burst_i;
4073 float ti = net->ct_sin_i.trough_i;
4074 if(ct_inhib_mod.use_sin) {
4075 bi = ct_inhib_mod.burst_i;
4076 ti = ct_inhib_mod.trough_i;
4077 }
4078 float ii = net->ct_fin_i.inhib_i;
4079 if(ct_inhib_mod.use_fin) {
4080 ii = ct_inhib_mod.inhib_i;
4081 }
4082 float imod = net->ct_sin_i.GetInhibMod(net->ct_cycle, bi, ti) +
4083 net->ct_fin_i.GetInhibMod(net->ct_cycle - net->ct_time.inhib_start, ii);
4084
4085 // only one is going to be in effect at a time..
4086 lay->i_val.g_i += imod * lay->i_val.g_i;
4087
4088 if(inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) {
4089 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4090 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4091 gpd->i_val.g_i += imod * gpd->i_val.g_i;
4092 }
4093 }
4094}
4095
4096////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4097// Inhibition Stage 2.2: LayInhibToGps
4098
4099void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_LayInhibToGps(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork*) {
4100 if(!lay->unit_groups) return;
4101
4102 if(inhib_group == ENTIRE_LAYER) {
4103 // propagate g_i to all subgroups even if doing ENTIRE_LAYER
4104 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4105 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4106 gpd->i_val.g_i = lay->i_val.g_i;
4107 }
4108 }
4109 else if(inhib_group == UNIT_GROUPS) {
4110 if(unit_gp_inhib.on) { // linking groups: get max from layer
4111 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4112 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4113 gpd->i_val.gp_g_i = lay->i_val.g_i;
4114 gpd->i_val.g_i = MAX(gpd->i_val.g_i, lay->i_val.g_i)(((gpd->i_val.g_i) > (lay->i_val.g_i)) ? (gpd->i_val
.g_i) : (lay->i_val.g_i));
4115 }
4116 }
4117 }
4118 else if(inhib_group == LAY_AND_GPS) {
4119 // actual inhibition is max of layer and group
4120 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4121 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4122 gpd->i_val.g_i = MAX(gpd->i_val.g_i, lay->i_val.g_i)(((gpd->i_val.g_i) > (lay->i_val.g_i)) ? (gpd->i_val
.g_i) : (lay->i_val.g_i));
4123 }
4124 }
4125}
4126
4127////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4128// Inhibition Stage 2.3: Apply Inhib
4129
4130void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_ApplyInhib(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4131 if((net->cycle >= 0) && lay->hard_clamped)
4132 return; // don't do this during normal processing
4133
4134 if(inhib.type == LeabraInhibSpec::UNIT_INHIB) return; // otherwise overwrites!
4135
4136 if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && lay->unit_groups) {
4137 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4138 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4139 Compute_ApplyInhib_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net);
4140 }
4141 }
4142 else {
4143 Compute_ApplyInhib_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
4144 }
4145}
4146
4147void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_ApplyInhib_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
4148 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4149 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net)
4150{
4151 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
4152 float inhib_val = thr->i_val.g_i;
4153 if(thr->kwta.tie_brk == 1) {
4154 float inhib_thr = thr->kwta.k_ithr;
4155 float inhib_loser = thr->kwta.eff_loser_gain * thr->i_val.g_i;
4156 for(int i=0; i<nunits; i++) {
4157 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
4158 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4159 u->Compute_ApplyInhib_LoserGain(net, inhib_thr, inhib_val, inhib_loser);
4160 }
4161 }
4162 else {
4163 for(int i=0; i<nunits; i++) {
4164 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
4165 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4166 u->Compute_ApplyInhib(net, inhib_val);
4167 }
4168 }
4169}

4171///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4172// Cycle Step 3: Activation
4173
4174///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4175// Cycle Stats
4176
4177void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_CycleStats(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4178 if((net->cycle >= 0) && lay->hard_clamped) {
4179 Compute_OutputName(lay, net); // need to keep doing this because network clears it
4180 return;
4181 }
4182
4183 Compute_Acts_AvgMax(lay, net);
4184 if(inhib.type == LeabraInhibSpec::AVG_NET_ACT)
4185 Compute_ActsIAvg_AvgMax(lay, net);
4186 Compute_MaxDa(lay, net);
4187 Compute_OutputName(lay, net);
4188
4189 if(lay->un_g_i.cmpt)
4190 Compute_UnitInhib_AvgMax(lay, net);
4191
4192 if(lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG)) {
4193 net->trg_max_act = MAX(net->trg_max_act, lay->acts.max)(((net->trg_max_act) > (lay->acts.max)) ? (net->trg_max_act
) : (lay->acts.max));
4194 }
4195
4196 if(lay->Iconified()) {
4197 lay->icon_value = lay->acts.avg;
4198 }
4199}
4200
4201void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_AvgMaxVals_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
4202 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4203 AvgMaxVals& vals, ta_memb_ptr mb_off) {
4204 vals.InitVals();
4205 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
4206 for(int i=0; i<nunits; i++) {
4207 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
4208 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4209 float val = *((float*)MemberDef::GetOff_static((void*)u, 0, mb_off));
4210 vals.UpdtVals(val, i);
4211 }
4212 vals.CalcAvg(nunits);
4213}
4214
4215void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_AvgMaxActs_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
4216 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4217 LeabraInhib* thr) {
4218 thr->acts.InitVals();
4219 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
4220 for(int i=0; i<nunits; i++) {
4221 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
4222 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4223 thr->acts.UpdtVals(u->act_eq, i);
4224 }
4225 thr->acts.CalcAvg(nunits);
4226
4227 if(thr->acts_top_k.cmpt) {
4228 thr->acts_top_k.InitVals();
4229 int k_eff = thr->kwta.k; // keep cutoff at k
4230 KwtaSortBuff* act_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::ACTIVE);
4231 if(k_eff <= 0 || act_buff->Size(gpidx) != k_eff)
4232 return; // no can do
4233
4234 for(int j=0; j < k_eff; j++) {
4235 thr->acts_top_k.UpdtVals(act_buff->Un(j, gpidx)->act_eq, j);
4236 }
4237 thr->acts_top_k.CalcAvg(k_eff);
4238 }
4239}
4240
4241void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_Acts_AvgMax(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4242 AvgMaxVals& vals = lay->acts;
4243// static ta_memb_ptr mb_off = 0;
4244// if(mb_off == 0) {
4245// TypeDef* td = &TA_LeabraUnit; int net_base_off = 0;
4246// TypeDef::FindMemberPathStatic(td, net_base_off, mb_off, "act_eq");
4247// }
4248 if(lay->unit_groups) {
4249 vals.InitVals();
4250 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(Layer::ACC_GP);
4251 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4252 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4253 Compute_AvgMaxActs_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd);
4254 vals.UpdtFmAvgMax(gpd->acts, nunits, g);
4255 lay->acts_top_k.UpdtFmAvgMax(gpd->acts_top_k, 1, g); // only compute gp-wise avg for avg top k (n=1 per group)
4256 }
4257 vals.CalcAvg(lay->units.leaves);
4258 lay->acts_top_k.CalcAvg(lay->gp_geom.n);
4259 }
4260 else {
4261 Compute_AvgMaxActs_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay);
4262 }
4263}
4264
4265void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_ActsIAvg_AvgMax(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4266 AvgMaxVals& vals = lay->acts_iavg;
4267 AvgMaxVals vals_prv;
4268 vals_prv.CopyFrom(&lay->acts_iavg); // copy
4269 static ta_memb_ptr mb_off = 0;
4270 if(mb_off == 0) {
4271 TypeDef* td = &TA_LeabraUnit; int net_base_off = 0;
4272 TypeDef::FindMemberPathStatic(td, net_base_off, mb_off, "act");
4273 }
4274 if(lay->unit_groups) {
4275 vals.InitVals();
4276 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(Layer::ACC_GP);
4277 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4278 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4279 AvgMaxVals gp_vals_prv;
4280 gp_vals_prv.CopyFrom(&gpd->acts_iavg); // copy
4281 Compute_AvgMaxVals_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, gpd->acts_iavg, mb_off);
4282
4283 if(gpd->acts_iavg.avg > gp_vals_prv.avg) {
4284 gpd->acts_iavg.avg = gp_vals_prv.avg + inhib.avg_up_dt * (gpd->acts_iavg.avg - gp_vals_prv.avg);
4285 }
4286 else {
4287 gpd->acts_iavg.avg = gp_vals_prv.avg + inhib.avg_dn_dt * (gpd->acts_iavg.avg - gp_vals_prv.avg);
4288 }
4289
4290 vals.UpdtFmAvgMax(gpd->acts_iavg, nunits, g);
4291 }
4292 vals.CalcAvg(lay->units.leaves);
4293 }
4294 else {
4295 Compute_AvgMaxVals_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, vals, mb_off);
4296 }
4297
4298 if(vals.avg > vals_prv.avg) {
4299 vals.avg = vals_prv.avg + inhib.avg_up_dt * (vals.avg - vals_prv.avg);
4300 }
4301 else {
4302 vals.avg = vals_prv.avg + inhib.avg_dn_dt * (vals.avg - vals_prv.avg);
4303 }
4304}

4306
4307void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_MaxDa_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
4308 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4309 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4310 thr->maxda = 0.0f;
4311 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
4312 for(int i=0; i<nunits; i++) {
4313 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
4314 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4315 float fda = u->Compute_MaxDa(net);
4316 lay->maxda = MAX(fda, lay->maxda)(((fda) > (lay->maxda)) ? (fda) : (lay->maxda));
4317 thr->maxda = MAX(fda, thr->maxda)(((fda) > (thr->maxda)) ? (fda) : (thr->maxda));
4318 net->maxda = MAX(fda, net->maxda)(((fda) > (net->maxda)) ? (fda) : (net->maxda));
4319 }
4320}
4321
4322void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_MaxDa(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4323 lay->maxda = 0.0f;

4325 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4326 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4327 Compute_MaxDa_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net);
4328 }
4329 }
4330 else {
4331 Compute_MaxDa_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
4332 }
4333}
4334
4335void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_OutputName_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
4336 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4337 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4338 StringtaString* onm;
4339 if(lay->unit_groups)
4340 onm = &(lay->gp_output_names.FastEl_Flat(gpidx));
4341 else
4342 onm = &(lay->output_name);
4343
4344 if(thr->acts.max_i < 0) {
4345 *onm = "n/a";
4346 return;
4347 }
4348 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, thr->acts.max_i, gpidx);
4349 if(!u || u->lesioned()) {
4350 *onm = "n/a";
4351 return;
4352 }
4353 // for target/output layers, if we set something, set network name!
4354 if(u->name.empty()) return;
4355 *onm = u->name; // if it is something..
4356
4357 if(lay->unit_groups) { // also aggregate the layer name
4358 if(lay->output_name.nonempty())
4359 lay->output_name += "_";
4360 lay->output_name += u->name;
4361 }
4362
4363 if((lay->layer_type != Layer::OUTPUT) && (lay->layer_type != Layer::TARGET)) return;
4364 if(net->output_name.nonempty())
4365 net->output_name += "_";
4366 net->output_name += u->name;
4367}

4373 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4374 Compute_OutputName_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net);
4375 }
4376 }
4377 else {
4378 Compute_OutputName_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
4379 }
4380}

4404///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4405// Cycle Stats -- optional non-default guys
4406
4407float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_TopKAvgAct_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
4408 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4409 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork*) {
4410 int k_eff = thr->kwta.k; // keep cutoff at k
4411 KwtaSortBuff* act_buff = lay->SortBuff(acc_md, KwtaSortBuff_List::ACTIVE);
4412 if(TestError(k_eff <= 0 || act_buff->Size(gpidx) != k_eff, "Compute_TopKAvgAct_ugp",
4413 "Only usable when using a kwta function -- kwta sort buff was not set properly!")) {
4414 return -1;
4415 }
4416
4417 float k_avg = 0.0f;
4418 for(int j=0; j < k_eff; j++)
4419 k_avg += act_buff->Un(j, gpidx)->act_eq;
4420 k_avg /= (float)k_eff;
4421
4422 return k_avg;
4423}
4424
4425float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_TopKAvgAct(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4426 float k_avg = 0.0f;
4427 if(lay->unit_groups) {
4428 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4429 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4430 k_avg += Compute_TopKAvgAct_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net);
4431 }
4432 if(lay->unit_groups)
4433 k_avg /= (float)lay->gp_geom.n;
4434 }
4435 else {
4436 k_avg = Compute_TopKAvgAct_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
4437 }
4438 return k_avg;
4439}

4447 "Only usable when using a kwta function -- kwta sort buff was not set properly!")) {
4448 return -1;

4450
4451 float k_avg = 0.0f;
4452 for(int j=0; j < k_eff; j++)
4453 k_avg += act_buff->Un(j, gpidx)->net;

4478void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_MidMinus(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4479 // just snapshot the activation state
4480 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
4481 if(u->lesioned()) continue;

4485
4486///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4487// SettleFinal
4488
4489void LeabraLayerSpec::PostSettle(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4490 bool no_plus_testing = false;
4491 if(net->no_plus_test && (net->train_mode == LeabraNetwork::TEST)) {
4492 no_plus_testing = true;
4493 }
4494
4495 switch(net->phase_order) {
4496 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS:
4497 if(no_plus_testing) {
4498 PostSettle_GetMinus(lay, net);
4499 PostSettle_GetPlus(lay, net);
4500 lay->phase_dif_ratio = 1.0f;
4501 }
4502 else {
4503 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE)
4504 PostSettle_GetMinus(lay, net);
4505 else {
4506 PostSettle_GetPlus(lay, net);
4507 PostSettle_GetPhaseDifRatio(lay, net);
4508 }
4509 }
4510 break;
4511 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_MINUS:
4512 if(no_plus_testing) {
4513 PostSettle_GetMinus(lay, net);
4514 PostSettle_GetPlus(lay, net);
4515 lay->phase_dif_ratio = 1.0f;
4516 }
4517 else {
4518 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE) {
4519 PostSettle_GetMinus(lay, net);
4520 PostSettle_GetPhaseDifRatio(lay, net);
4521 }
4522 else {
4523 PostSettle_GetPlus(lay, net);
4524 }
4525 }
4526 break;
4527 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_ONLY:
4528 PostSettle_GetMinus(lay, net);
4529 PostSettle_GetPlus(lay, net);
4530 lay->phase_dif_ratio = 1.0f;
4531 break;
4532 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
4533 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_MINUS:
4534 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
4535 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
4536 PostSettle_GetMinus(lay, net);
4537 }
4538 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
4539 PostSettle_GetPlus(lay, net);
4540 PostSettle_GetPhaseDifRatio(lay, net);
4541 }
4542 else {
4543 PostSettle_GetPlus2(lay, net);
4544 }
4545 break;
4546 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_NOTHING:
4547 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
4548 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
4549 PostSettle_GetPlus(lay, net);
4550 }
4551 else {
4552 PostSettle_GetMinus(lay, net);
4553 PostSettle_GetPhaseDifRatio(lay, net);
4554 }
4555 break;
4556 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS:
4557 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
4558 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
4559 PostSettle_GetMinus(lay, net);
4560 }
4561 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
4562 PostSettle_GetPlus(lay, net);
4563 PostSettle_GetPhaseDifRatio(lay, net);
4564 }
4565 else {
4566 PostSettle_GetPlus2(lay, net);
4567 }
4568 break;
4569 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
4570 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_MINUS:
4571 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
4572 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
4573 PostSettle_GetMinus(lay, net);
4574 }
4575 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
4576 PostSettle_GetPlus(lay, net);
4577 PostSettle_GetPhaseDifRatio(lay, net);
4578 }
4579 else if(net->phase_no == 2) {
4580 PostSettle_GetPlus2(lay, net);
4581 }
4582 else {
4583 PostSettle_GetMinus2(lay, net);
4584 }
4585 break;
4586 }
4587
4588 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
4589 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4590 u->PostSettle(net);
4591 }
4592
4593 if((adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::G_BAR_I) || (adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::G_BAR_IL)) {
4594 AdaptGBarI(lay, net);
4595 }
4596}
4597
4598void LeabraLayerSpec::PostSettle_GetMinus(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4599 lay->acts_m = lay->acts;
4600 if(lay->unit_groups) {
4601 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4602 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4603 gpd->acts_m = gpd->acts;
4604 }
4605 }
4606}
4607void LeabraLayerSpec::PostSettle_GetPlus(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4608 lay->acts_p = lay->acts;
4609 if(lay->unit_groups) {
4610 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4611 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4612 gpd->acts_p = gpd->acts;
4613 }
4614 }
4615}
4616void LeabraLayerSpec::PostSettle_GetMinus2(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4617 lay->acts_m2 = lay->acts;
4618 if(lay->unit_groups) {
4619 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4620 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4621 gpd->acts_m2 = gpd->acts;
4622 }
4623 }
4624}
4625void LeabraLayerSpec::PostSettle_GetPlus2(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4626 lay->acts_p2 = lay->acts;
4627 if(lay->unit_groups) {
4628 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4629 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4630 gpd->acts_p2 = gpd->acts;
4631 }
4632 }
4633}
4634void LeabraLayerSpec::PostSettle_GetPhaseDifRatio(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4635 if(lay->acts_p.avg > 0.0f)
4636 lay->phase_dif_ratio = lay->acts_m.avg / lay->acts_p.avg;
4637 else
4638 lay->phase_dif_ratio = 1.0f;
4639 if(lay->unit_groups) {
4640 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4641 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4642 if(gpd->acts_p.avg > 0.0f)
4643 gpd->phase_dif_ratio = gpd->acts_m.avg / gpd->acts_p.avg;
4644 else
4645 gpd->phase_dif_ratio = 1.0f;
4646 }
4647 }
4648}
4649
4650void LeabraLayerSpec::AdaptGBarI(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork*) {
4651 float diff = lay->kwta.pct - lay->acts.avg;
4652 if(fabsf(diff) > adapt_i.tol) {
4653 float p_i = 1.0f;
4654 if(adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::G_BAR_IL) {
4655 p_i = 1.0f - adapt_i.l;
4656 }
4657 lay->adapt_i.g_bar_i -= p_i * adapt_i.p_dt * diff;
4658 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
4659 float minv = us->g_bar.i * (1.0 - adapt_i.mx_d);
4660 float maxv = us->g_bar.i * (1.0 + adapt_i.mx_d);
4661 if(lay->adapt_i.g_bar_i < minv) lay->adapt_i.g_bar_i = minv;
4662 if(lay->adapt_i.g_bar_i > maxv) lay->adapt_i.g_bar_i = maxv;
4663 if(adapt_i.type == AdaptISpec::G_BAR_IL) {
4664 lay->adapt_i.g_bar_l -= adapt_i.l * adapt_i.p_dt * diff;
4665 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
4666 float minv = us->g_bar.l * (1.0 - adapt_i.mx_d);
4667 float maxv = us->g_bar.l * (1.0 + adapt_i.mx_d);
4668 if(lay->adapt_i.g_bar_l < minv) lay->adapt_i.g_bar_l = minv;
4669 if(lay->adapt_i.g_bar_l > maxv) lay->adapt_i.g_bar_l = maxv;
4670 }
4671 }
4672}

4698
4699void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_ActP_AvgMax(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4700 AvgMaxVals& vals = lay->acts_p;
4701 static ta_memb_ptr mb_off = 0;
4702 if(mb_off == 0) {
4703 TypeDef* td = &TA_LeabraUnit; int net_base_off = 0;
4704 TypeDef::FindMemberPathStatic(td, net_base_off, mb_off, "act_p");
4705 }
4706 if(lay->unit_groups) {
4707 vals.InitVals();
4708 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(Layer::ACC_GP);
4709 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4710 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4711 Compute_AvgMaxVals_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, gpd->acts_p, mb_off);
4712 vals.UpdtFmAvgMax(gpd->acts_p, nunits, g);
4713 }
4714 vals.CalcAvg(lay->units.leaves);
4715 }
4716 else {
4717 Compute_AvgMaxVals_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, vals, mb_off);
4718 }
4719}

*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)

4741///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4742// Learning
4743
4744bool LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_SRAvg_Test(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4745 return true;
4746}
4747
4748bool LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_dWt_FirstPlus_Test(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4749 if((net->phase_order == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING ||
4750 net->phase_order == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_MINUS) &&
4751 (net->learn_rule != LeabraNetwork::LEABRA_CHL &&
4752 net->learn_rule != LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_XCAL_C)) { // xcal_c learns on 1st plus!
4753 return false;
4754 }
4755 return true;
4756}
4757
4758bool LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_dWt_SecondPlus_Test(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4759 return false; // standard layers never learn here
4760}
4761
4762bool LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_dWt_Nothing_Test(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4763 // shouldn't happen, but just in case..
4764 if(net->learn_rule == LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_XCAL_C) return false; // only 1st plus
4765 return true; // all types learn here..
4766}

4771float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_SSE(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net,
4772 int& n_vals, bool unit_avg, bool sqrt) {
4773 return lay->Layer::Compute_SSE(net, n_vals, unit_avg, sqrt);
4774}
4775
4776float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_NormErr_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
4777 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4778 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4779 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
4780 float nerr = 0.0f;
4781 for(int i=0; i<nunits; i++) {
4782 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
4783 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4784 nerr += u->Compute_NormErr(net);
4785 }
4786 return nerr;
4787}
4788
4789float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_NormErr(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4790 lay->norm_err = -1.0f; // assume not contributing
4791 if(!lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) return -1.0f; // indicates not applicable
4792
4793 float nerr = 0.0f;
4794 int ntot = 0;
4795 if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && lay->unit_groups) {
4796 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4797 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4798 nerr += Compute_NormErr_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net);
4799 if(net->on_errs && net->off_errs)
4800 ntot += 2 * gpd->kwta.k;
4801 else
4802 ntot += gpd->kwta.k;
4803 }
4804 }
4805 else {
4806 nerr += Compute_NormErr_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
4807 if(net->on_errs && net->off_errs)
4808 ntot += 2 * lay->kwta.k;
4809 else
4810 ntot += lay->kwta.k;
4811 }
4812 if(ntot == 0) return -1.0f;
4813
4814 lay->norm_err = nerr / (float)ntot;
4815 if(lay->norm_err > 1.0f) lay->norm_err = 1.0f;
4816
4817 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) ||
4818 (lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::COMP) && lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE)))
4819 return -1.0f; // no contributarse
4820
4821 return lay->norm_err;
4822}
4823
4824float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_M2SSE(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net,
4825 int& n_vals) {
4826 n_vals = 0;
4827 float sse = 0.0f;
4828 if(!lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) return 0.0f;
4829 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) || (lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::COMP) &&
4830 lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE))) {
4831 return 0.0f;
4832 }
4833 bool has_targ = false;
4834 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
4835 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4836 sse += u->Compute_M2SSE(net, has_targ);
4837 if(has_targ) n_vals++;
4838 }
4839 return sse;
4840}
4841
4842float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_CosErr(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net,
4843 int& n_vals) {
4844 n_vals = 0;
4845 float cosv = 0.0f;
4846 if(!lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) return 0.0f;
4847 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) || (lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::COMP) &&
4848 lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE))) {
4849 return 0.0f;
4850 }
4851 float ssm = 0.0f;
4852 float sst = 0.0f;
4853 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
4854 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4855 if(!u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) continue;
4856 n_vals++;
4857 cosv += u->targ * u->act_m;
4858 ssm += u->act_m * u->act_m;
4859 sst += u->targ * u->targ;
4860 }
4861 if(n_vals == 0) return 0.0f;
4862 float dist = sqrtf(ssm * sst);
4863 if(dist != 0.0f)
4864 cosv /= dist;
4865 return cosv;
4866}
4867
4868float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_M2CosErr(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net,
4869 int& n_vals) {
4870 n_vals = 0;
4871 float cosv = 0.0f;
4872 if(!lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) return 0.0f;
4873 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) || (lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::COMP) &&
4874 lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE))) {
4875 return 0.0f;
4876 }
4877 float ssm = 0.0f;
4878 float sst = 0.0f;
4879 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
4880 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4881 if(!u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) continue;
4882 n_vals++;
4883 cosv += u->targ * u->act_m2;
4884 ssm += u->act_m2 * u->act_m2;
4885 sst += u->targ * u->targ;
4886 }
4887 if(n_vals == 0) return 0.0f;
4888 float dist = sqrtf(ssm * sst);
4889 if(dist != 0.0f)
4890 cosv /= dist;
4891 return cosv;
4892}
4893
4894float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_CosDiff(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4895 float cosv = 0.0f;
4896 float ssm = 0.0f;
4897 float sst = 0.0f;
4898 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
4899 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4900 cosv += u->act_p * u->act_m;
4901 ssm += u->act_m * u->act_m;
4902 sst += u->act_p * u->act_p;
4903 }
4904 float dist = sqrtf(ssm * sst);
4905 if(dist != 0.0f)
4906 cosv /= dist;
4907 return cosv;
4908}
4909
4910float LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_CosDiff2(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4911 float cosv = 0.0f;
4912 float ssm = 0.0f;
4913 float sst = 0.0f;
4914 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
4915 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4916 cosv += u->act_p * u->act_m2;
4917 ssm += u->act_m2 * u->act_m2;
4918 sst += u->act_p * u->act_p;
4919 }
4920 float dist = sqrtf(ssm * sst);
4921 if(dist != 0.0f)
4922 cosv /= dist;
4923 return cosv;
4924}

4926////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4927// Parameter Adaptation over longer timesales
4928
4929void LeabraLayerSpec::AdaptKWTAPt_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
4930 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
4931 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4932 thr->adapt_i.avg_avg += adapt_i.a_dt * (thr->acts_m.avg - thr->adapt_i.avg_avg);
4933 float dif = thr->adapt_i.avg_avg - thr->kwta.pct;
4934 if(dif < -adapt_i.tol) { // average is less than target
4935 // so reduce the point towards lower value
4936 thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt += adapt_i.p_dt *
4937 ((inhib.kwta_pt - adapt_i.mx_d) - thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt);
4938 }
4939 else if(dif > adapt_i.tol) { // average is more than target
4940 // so increase point towards higher value
4941 thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt += adapt_i.p_dt *
4942 ((inhib.kwta_pt + adapt_i.mx_d) - thr->adapt_i.i_kwta_pt);
4943 }
4944}
4945
4946void LeabraLayerSpec::AdaptKWTAPt(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4947 if(lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::EXT) && !lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG))
4948 return; // don't adapt points for input-only layers
4949 if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && lay->unit_groups) {
4950 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
4951 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
4952 AdaptKWTAPt_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net);
4953 }
4954 }
4955 AdaptKWTAPt_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
4956}
4957
4958void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_AbsRelNetin(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4959 if(lay->netin.max < 0.01f) return; // not getting enough activation to count!
4960
4961 lay->avg_netin_sum.avg += lay->netin.avg;
4962 lay->avg_netin_sum.max += lay->netin.max;
4963 lay->avg_netin_n++;
4964
4965 float sum_net = 0.0f;
4966 for(int i=0;i<lay->projections.size;i++) {
4967 LeabraPrjn* prjn = (LeabraPrjn*)lay->projections[i];
4968 if(prjn->off || !prjn->from || prjn->from->lesioned()) continue;
4969 prjn->netin_avg = 0.0f;
4970 int netin_avg_n = 0;
4971 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
4972 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
4973 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec();
4974 if(u->act_eq < us->opt_thresh.send) continue; // ignore if not above sending thr
4975 LeabraRecvCons* cg = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.SafeEl(prjn->recv_idx);
4976 if(!cg) continue;
4977 float netin = cg->Compute_Netin(u);
4978 cg->net = netin;
4979 prjn->netin_avg += netin;
4980 netin_avg_n++;
4981 }
4982 if(netin_avg_n > 0)
4983 prjn->netin_avg /= (float)netin_avg_n;
4984 sum_net += prjn->netin_avg;
4985 }
4986
4987 for(int i=0;i<lay->projections.size;i++) {
4988 LeabraPrjn* prjn = (LeabraPrjn*)lay->projections[i];
4989 if(sum_net > 0.0f)
4990 prjn->netin_rel = prjn->netin_avg / sum_net;
4991 // increment epoch-level
4992 prjn->avg_netin_avg_sum += prjn->netin_avg;
4993 prjn->avg_netin_rel_sum += prjn->netin_rel;
4994 prjn->avg_netin_n++;
4995 }
4996}
4997
4998void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_AvgAbsRelNetin(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
4999#ifdef DMEM_COMPILE
5000 lay->DMem_ComputeAggs(net->dmem_trl_comm.comm);
5001#endif
5002 if(lay->avg_netin_n > 0) {
5003 lay->avg_netin.avg = lay->avg_netin_sum.avg / (float)lay->avg_netin_n;
5004 lay->avg_netin.max = lay->avg_netin_sum.max / (float)lay->avg_netin_n;
5005 }
5006 lay->avg_netin_sum.avg = 0.0f;
5007 lay->avg_netin_sum.max = 0.0f;
5008 lay->avg_netin_n = 0;
5009 for(int i=0;i<lay->projections.size;i++) {
5010 LeabraPrjn* prjn = (LeabraPrjn*)lay->projections[i];
5011 if(prjn->off || !prjn->from || prjn->from->lesioned()) continue;
5012#ifdef DMEM_COMPILE
5013 prjn->DMem_ComputeAggs(net->dmem_trl_comm.comm);
5014#endif
5015 if(prjn->avg_netin_n > 0) {
5016 prjn->avg_netin_avg = prjn->avg_netin_avg_sum / (float)prjn->avg_netin_n;
5017 prjn->avg_netin_rel = prjn->avg_netin_rel_sum / (float)prjn->avg_netin_n;
5018 }
5019 prjn->avg_netin_n = 0;
5020 prjn->avg_netin_avg_sum = 0.0f;
5021 prjn->avg_netin_rel_sum = 0.0f;
5022 }
5023}
5024
5025void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_TrgRelNetin(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork*) {
5026 int n_in = 0;
5027 int n_out = 0;
5028 int n_lat = 0;
5029 for(int i=0;i<lay->projections.size;i++) {
5030 LeabraPrjn* prjn = (LeabraPrjn*)lay->projections[i];
5031 if(prjn->off || !prjn->from || prjn->from->lesioned()) {
5032 prjn->trg_netin_rel = 0.0f;
5033 continue;
5034 }
5035 if(prjn->con_spec->InheritsFrom(&TA_MarkerConSpec)) { // fix these guys
5036 prjn->trg_netin_rel = 0.0f;
5037 prjn->direction = Projection::DIR_UNKNOWN;
5038 continue;
5039 }
5040 if(prjn->direction == Projection::FM_INPUT) n_in++;
5041 else if(prjn->direction == Projection::FM_OUTPUT) n_out++;
5042 else if(prjn->direction == Projection::LATERAL) n_lat++;
5043 }
5044 for(int i=0;i<lay->projections.size;i++) {
5045 LeabraPrjn* prjn = (LeabraPrjn*)lay->projections[i];
5046 if(prjn->off || !prjn->from || prjn->from->lesioned()) continue;
5047 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)prjn->con_spec.SPtr();
5048 float in_trg = cs->rel_net_adapt.trg_fm_input;
5049 float out_trg = cs->rel_net_adapt.trg_fm_output;
5050 float lat_trg = cs->rel_net_adapt.trg_lateral;
5051 if(prjn->direction == Projection::FM_INPUT) {
5052 if(n_out == 0 && n_lat == 0) in_trg = 1.0;
5053 else if(n_out == 0) in_trg = in_trg / (in_trg + lat_trg);
5054 else if(n_lat == 0) in_trg = in_trg / (in_trg + out_trg);
5055 prjn->trg_netin_rel = in_trg / (float)n_in;
5056 }
5057 else if(prjn->direction == Projection::FM_OUTPUT) {
5058 if(n_in == 0 && n_lat == 0) out_trg = 1.0;
5059 else if(n_in == 0) out_trg = out_trg / (out_trg + lat_trg);
5060 else if(n_lat == 0) out_trg = out_trg / (out_trg + in_trg);
5061 prjn->trg_netin_rel = out_trg / (float)n_out;
5062 }
5063 else if(prjn->direction == Projection::LATERAL) {
5064 if(n_in == 0 && n_out == 0) lat_trg = 1.0;
5065 else if(n_in == 0) lat_trg = lat_trg / (lat_trg + out_trg);
5066 else if(n_out == 0) lat_trg = lat_trg / (lat_trg + in_trg);
5067 prjn->trg_netin_rel = lat_trg / (float)n_lat;
5068 }
5069 }
5070}
5071
5072void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_AdaptRelNetin(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork*) {
5073 for(int i=0;i<lay->projections.size;i++) {
5074 LeabraPrjn* prjn = (LeabraPrjn*)lay->projections[i];
5075 if(prjn->off || !prjn->from || prjn->from->lesioned()) continue;
5076 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)prjn->con_spec.SPtr();
5077 if(prjn->trg_netin_rel <= 0.0f) continue; // not set
5078 if(!cs->rel_net_adapt.on) continue;
5079 if(cs->rel_net_adapt.CheckInTolerance(prjn->trg_netin_rel, prjn->avg_netin_rel))
5080 continue;
5081 cs->SetUnique("wt_scale", true);
5082 cs->wt_scale.rel += cs->rel_net_adapt.rel_lrate *
5083 (prjn->trg_netin_rel - prjn->avg_netin_rel);
5084 if(cs->wt_scale.rel <= 0.0f) cs->wt_scale.rel = 0.0f;
5085 }
5086}
5087
5088void LeabraLayerSpec::Compute_AdaptAbsNetin(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork*) {
5089 if(!abs_net_adapt.on) return;
5090 float dst = abs_net_adapt.trg_net - lay->avg_netin.max;
5091 if(fabsf(dst) < abs_net_adapt.tol) return;
5092 for(int i=0;i<lay->projections.size;i++) {
5093 LeabraPrjn* prjn = (LeabraPrjn*)lay->projections[i];
5094 if(prjn->off || !prjn->from || prjn->from->lesioned()) continue;
5095 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)prjn->con_spec.SPtr();
5096 cs->SetUnique("wt_scale", true);
5097 cs->wt_scale.abs += abs_net_adapt.abs_lrate * dst;
5098 }
5099}

5166
5167void KWTAVals::Initialize() {
5168 k = 12;
5169 pct = .25f;
5170 pct_c = .75f;
5171 adth_k = 1;
5172 k_ithr = 0.0f;
5173 k1_ithr = 0.0f;
5174 ithr_r = 0.0f;
5175 ithr_diff = 0.0f;
5176 tie_brk_gain = 0.0f;
5177 eff_loser_gain = 1.0f;
5178 tie_brk = 0;
5179}
5180
5181void KWTAVals::Copy_(const KWTAVals& cp) {
5182 k = cp.k;
5183 pct = cp.pct;
5184 pct_c = cp.pct_c;
5185 adth_k = cp.adth_k;
5186 k_ithr = cp.k_ithr;
5187 k1_ithr = cp.k1_ithr;
5188 ithr_r = cp.ithr_r;
5189 ithr_diff = cp.ithr_diff;
5190 tie_brk_gain = cp.tie_brk_gain;
5191 eff_loser_gain = cp.eff_loser_gain;
5192 tie_brk = cp.tie_brk;
5193}
5194
5195void KWTAVals::Compute_Pct(int n_units) {
5196 if(n_units > 0)
5197 pct = (float)k / (float)n_units;
5198 else
5199 pct = 0.0f;
5200 pct_c = 1.0f - pct;
5201}
5202
5203void KWTAVals::Compute_IThrR() {
5204 if(k1_ithr <= 0.0f)
5205 ithr_r = 0.0f;
5206 else
5207 ithr_r = logf(k_ithr / k1_ithr);
5208}

5409bool LeabraLayer::SetLayerSpec(LayerSpec* sp) {
5410 if(sp == NULL__null) return false;
5411 if(sp->CheckObjectType(this))
5412 spec.SetSpec((LeabraLayerSpec*)sp);
5413 else
5414 return false;
5415 return true;
5416}

5421 gp_kbuffs.AllocAllBuffs(un_geom.n, gp_geom.n);
5422
5423 ungp_data.Reset();
5424 ungp_data.SetBaseType(((LeabraLayerSpec*)GetLayerSpec())->UnGpDataType());
5425 ungp_data.SetSize(gp_geom.n);
5426}

5586
5587void LeabraNetwork::GraphInhibMod(bool flip_sign, DataTable* graph_data) {
5588 taProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(taProject)(taProject *) GetOwner(&TA_taProject);
5589 if(!graph_data) {
5590 graph_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(name + "_InhibMod", true);
5591 }
5592 graph_data->StructUpdate(true);
5593 graph_data->ResetData();
5594 int idx;
5595 DataCol* cyc_col = graph_data->FindMakeColName("ct_cycle", idx, VT_INT);
5596 DataCol* imod_col = graph_data->FindMakeColName("inhib_mod", idx, VT_FLOAT);
5597// imod->SetUserData("MIN", 0.0f);
5598// imod->SetUserData("MAX", 1.0f);
5599
5600 float bi = ct_sin_i.burst_i;
5601 float ti = ct_sin_i.trough_i;
5602 float ii = ct_fin_i.inhib_i;
5603
5604 for(int cyc = 0; cyc < ct_time.total_cycles; cyc++) {
5605 float imod = ct_sin_i.GetInhibMod(cyc, bi, ti) +
5606 ct_fin_i.GetInhibMod(cyc - ct_time.inhib_start, ii);
5607 if(flip_sign) imod *= -1.0f;
5608 graph_data->AddBlankRow();
5609 cyc_col->SetValAsInt(cyc, -1);
5610 imod_col->SetValAsFloat(imod, -1);
5611 }
5612 graph_data->StructUpdate(false);
5613 graph_data->FindMakeGraphView();
5614}

5692
5693void LeabraNetwork::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
5694 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
5695 ct_time.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
5696 ct_lrn_trig.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
5697
5698 if(TestWarning(ct_sravg.plus_s_st >= ct_time.plus, "UAE",
5699 "ct_sravg.plus_s_st is higher than ct_time.plus (# of cycles in plus phase)"
5700 "just set it to plus-2")) {
5701 ct_sravg.plus_s_st = ct_time.plus -2;
5702 }
5703
5704// if(TestWarning(learn_rule != CTLEABRA_CAL && ct_sravg.interval == 5, "UAE",
5705// "ct_sravg.interval should be 1 for all algorithms *EXCEPT* CTLEABRA_CAL -- I just set it to 1 for you. Also, while I'm at it, I set n_avg_only_epcs = 0 as well, because that is the new default")) {
5706// ct_sravg.interval = 1;
5707// ct_time.n_avg_only_epcs = 0;
5708// }
5709// if(TestWarning(learn_rule == CTLEABRA_CAL && ct_sravg.interval == 1, "UAE",
5710// "ct_sravg.interval should be > 1 for CTLEABRA_CAL -- I just set it to 5 for you")) {
5711// ct_sravg.interval = 5;
5712// }
5713
5714 if(TestWarning(!off_errs && !on_errs, "UAE", "can't have both off_errs and on_errs be off (no err would be computed at all) -- turned both back on")) {
5715 on_errs = true;
5716 off_errs = true;
5717 }
5718
5719 if(prv_learn_rule == -1) {
5720 prv_learn_rule = learn_rule;
5721 }
5722 else if(prv_learn_rule != learn_rule) {
5723 SetLearnRule();
5724 prv_learn_rule = learn_rule;
5725 }
5726}

5836void LeabraNetwork::SetLearnRule() {
5837 if(learn_rule == LEABRA_CHL) {
5838 if(phase_order == MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING) {
5839 phase_order = MINUS_PLUS;
5840 }
5841 maxda_stopcrit = 0.005f;
5842 min_cycles = 15;
5843 min_cycles_phase2 = 35;
5844 cycle_max = 60;
5845 }
5846 else {
5847// if(phase_order == MINUS_PLUS) {
5848// phase_order = MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING;
5849// }
5850
5851 if(learn_rule == CTLEABRA_CAL) {
5852 ct_sravg.interval = 5;
5853 }
5854 else {
5855 ct_sravg.interval = 1;
5856 }
5857
5858 maxda_stopcrit = -1;
5859 min_cycles = 0;
5860 min_cycles_phase2 = 0;
5861 }
5862
5863 SetLearnRule_ConSpecs(&specs);
5864 // set all my specs -- otherwise it looks weird in hierarchy for unused parent specs
5865
5866 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
5867 lay->SetLearnRule(this);
5868 }
5869}

5887///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
5888// TrialInit -- at start of trial
5889
5890void LeabraNetwork::Trial_Init() {
5891 cycle = -1;
5892 Trial_Init_Phases();
5893 SetCurLrate();
5894
5895 Trial_Init_Unit(); // performs following at unit-level
5896// Trial_DecayState();
5897 Trial_NoiseInit(); // run for kpos case
5898// Trial_Init_SRAvg();
5899 Trial_Init_Layer();
5900}
5901
5902void LeabraNetwork::Trial_Init_Phases() {
5903 phase = MINUS_PHASE;
5904 nothing_phase = false;
5905 phase_no = 0;
5906
5907 bool no_plus_testing = false;
5908 if(no_plus_test && (train_mode == TEST)) {
5909 no_plus_testing = true;
5910 }
5911
5912 switch(phase_order) {
5913 case MINUS_PLUS:
5914 if(no_plus_testing)
5915 phase_max=1;
5916 else
5917 phase_max=2;
5918 break;
5919 case PLUS_MINUS:
5920 if(no_plus_testing)
5921 phase_max=1; // just do minus
5922 else {
5923 phase_max=2;
5924 phase = PLUS_PHASE;
5925 }
5926 break;
5927 case PLUS_ONLY:
5928 phase_max=1;
5929 phase = PLUS_PHASE;
5930 break;
5931 case MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
5932 case MINUS_PLUS_MINUS:
5933 phase_max=3; // ignore no_plus_test here -- just turn PLUS into extra MINUS
5934 break;
5935 case PLUS_NOTHING:
5936 phase_max=2; // ignore no_plus_test here -- just turn PLUS into MINUS
5937 break;
5938 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS:
5939 phase_max=3; // ignore no_plus_test here -- just turn PLUS into extra MINUS
5940 break;
5941 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
5942 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_MINUS:
5943 phase_max=4; // ignore no_plus_test here -- just turn PLUS into extra MINUS
5944 break;
5945 }
5946}
5947

; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
5950 if(!lay->lesioned())
5951 lay->SetCurLrate(this, epoch);
5952 }
5953}

5995///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
5996// SettleInit -- at start of settling
5997
5998void LeabraNetwork::Settle_Init() {
5999 int tmp_cycle = cycle;
6000 cycle = -2; // special signal for settle init
6001
6002 Settle_Init_CtTimes();
6003 Compute_Active_K(); // compute here because could depend on pat_n
6004
6005 Settle_Init_Unit(); // do chunk of following unit-level functions:
6006
6007// Settle_Init_TargFlags();
6008// Settle_DecayState();
6009// Compute_NetinScale(); // compute net scaling
6010
6011 Compute_HardClamp(); // clamp all hard-clamped input acts: not easily threadable
6012 cycle = tmp_cycle;
6013}
6014
6015void LeabraNetwork::Settle_Init_CtTimes() {
6016 if(learn_rule == LEABRA_CHL) return;
6017
6018 if(phase_order >= MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_NOTHING) {
6019 switch(phase_no) {
6020 case 0:
6021 cycle_max = ct_time.minus;
6022 break;
6023 case 1:
6024 cycle_max = ct_time.plus;
6025 break;
6026 case 2:
6027 cycle_max = ct_time.plus;
6028 break;
6029 case 3:
6030 cycle_max = ct_time.inhib;
6031 break;
6032 }
6033 }
6034 else { // for all other cases
6035 switch(phase_no) {
6036 case 0:
6037 cycle_max = ct_time.minus;
6038 break;
6039 case 1:
6040 cycle_max = ct_time.plus;
6041 break;
6042 case 2:
6043 cycle_max = ct_time.inhib;
6044 break;
6045 }
6046 }
6047}
6048
6049void LeabraNetwork::Compute_Active_K() {
6050 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6051 if(lay->lesioned()) continue;
6052 lay->Compute_Active_K(this); // this gets done at the outset..
6053 }
6054}
6055
6056void LeabraNetwork::Settle_Init_Unit() {
6057 if(nothing_phase) {
6058 if(phase_order != MINUS_PLUS_MINUS && phase_order != MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_MINUS) {
6059 TargExtToComp(); // all external input is now 'comparison' = nothing!
6060 }
6061 }
6062
6063 ThreadUnitCall un_call((ThreadUnitMethod)(LeabraUnitMethod)&LeabraUnit::Settle_Init_Unit);
6064 if(thread_flags & SETTLE_INIT)
6065 threads.Run(&un_call, .1f);
6066 else
6067 threads.Run(&un_call, -1.0f); // -1 = always run localized
6068
6069 Settle_Init_Layer();
6070
6071 Compute_NetinScale_Senders(); // second phase after recv-based NetinScale
6072 // put it after Settle_Init_Layer to allow for mods to netin scale in that guy..
6073}

6076 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6077 if(!lay->lesioned())
6078 lay->Settle_Init_Layer(this);
6079 }
6080}

6140
6141////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
6142// Cycle_Run
6143
6144void LeabraNetwork::Cycle_Run() {
6145 // ct_cycle is pretty useful anyway
6146 if(phase_no == 0 && cycle == 0) // detect start of trial
6147 ct_cycle = 0;
6148
6149 Send_Netin();
6150 Compute_ExtraNetin(); // layer level extra netinput for special algorithms
6151 Compute_NetinInteg();
6152 Compute_NetinStats();
6153
6154 Compute_Inhib();
6155 Compute_ApplyInhib();
6156
6157 Compute_Act();
6158 Compute_CycleStats();
6159
6160 Compute_CycSynDep();
6161
6162 Compute_SRAvg(); // note: only ctleabra variants do con-level compute here
6163 Compute_XCalC_dWt();
6164 Compute_MidMinus(); // check for mid-minus and run if so (PBWM)
6165
6166 ct_cycle++;
6167 time += time_inc; // always increment time..
6168}
6169
6170///////////////////////////////////////////////////////
6171// Cycle Stage 1: netinput
6172
6173void LeabraNetwork::Send_Netin() {
6174 // always use delta mode!
6175 send_pct_n = send_pct_tot = 0;
6176 ThreadUnitCall un_call((ThreadUnitMethod)(LeabraUnitMethod)&LeabraUnit::Send_NetinDelta);
6177 if(thread_flags & NETIN)
6178 threads.Run(&un_call, 1.0f);
6179 else
6180 threads.Run(&un_call, -1.0f); // -1 = always run localized
6181
6182 // now need to roll up the netinput into unit vals
6183 const int nu = units_flat.size;
6184 for(int i=1;i<nu;i++) { // 0 = dummy idx
6185 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)units_flat[i];
6186 u->Send_NetinDelta_Post(this);
6187 }
6188
6189 if(NetinPerPrjn() || threads.using_threads) {
6190 send_netin_tmp.InitVals(0.0f); // reset for next time around
6191 }
6192
6193#ifdef DMEM_COMPILE
6194 dmem_share_units.Sync(3);
6195#endif
6196 if(send_pct_tot > 0) { // only avail for non-threaded calls
6197 send_pct = (float)send_pct_n / (float)send_pct_tot;
6198 avg_send_pct_sum += send_pct;
6199 avg_send_pct_n++;
6200 }
6201}
6202
6203void LeabraNetwork::Compute_ExtraNetin() {
6204 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6205 if(lay->lesioned()) continue;
6206 lay->Compute_ExtraNetin(this);
6207 }
6208}

6210void LeabraNetwork::Compute_NetinInteg() {

6216}

6224
6225///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
6226// Cycle Step 2: Inhibition
6227
6228void LeabraNetwork::Compute_Inhib() {
6229 bool do_lay_gp = false;
6230 if(layers.gp.size == 0) do_lay_gp = true; // falsely set to true to prevent further checking
6231 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6232 if(lay->lesioned()) continue;
6233 lay->Compute_Inhib(this);
6234 if(!do_lay_gp) {
6235 LeabraLayerSpec* laysp = (LeabraLayerSpec*)lay->spec.SPtr();
6236 if(laysp->lay_gp_inhib.on) do_lay_gp = true;
6237 }
6238 }
6239 if(layers.gp.size == 0) do_lay_gp = false; // now override anything
6240 if(do_lay_gp) {
6241 for(int lgi = 0; lgi < layers.gp.size; lgi++) {
6242 Layer_Group* lg = (Layer_Group*)layers.gp[lgi];
6243 float lay_gp_g_i = 0.0f;
6244 for(int li = 0; li < lg->size; li++) {
6245 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)lg->FastEl(li);
6246 LeabraLayerSpec* laysp = (LeabraLayerSpec*)lay->spec.SPtr();
6247 if(lay->lesioned() || !laysp->lay_gp_inhib.on) continue;
6248 float lay_val = laysp->lay_gp_inhib.gp_g * lay->i_val.g_i;
6249 lay_gp_g_i = MAX(lay_val, lay_gp_g_i)(((lay_val) > (lay_gp_g_i)) ? (lay_val) : (lay_gp_g_i));
6250 }
6251 if(lay_gp_g_i > 0.0f) { // actually got something
6252 for(int li = 0; li < lg->size; li++) {
6253 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)lg->FastEl(li);
6254 LeabraLayerSpec* laysp = (LeabraLayerSpec*)lay->spec.SPtr();
6255 if(lay->lesioned() || !laysp->lay_gp_inhib.on) continue;
6256 lay->i_val.gp_g_i = lay_gp_g_i;
6257 lay->i_val.g_i = MAX(lay->i_val.gp_g_i, lay->i_val.g_i)(((lay->i_val.gp_g_i) > (lay->i_val.g_i)) ? (lay->
i_val.gp_g_i) : (lay->i_val.g_i));
6258
6259 if(lay->unit_groups) {
6260 lay->Compute_LayInhibToGps(this);
6261 }
6262 }
6263 }
6264 }
6265 }
6266}
6267
6268void LeabraNetwork::Compute_ApplyInhib() {
6269 // this is not threadable due to interactions with inhib vals at layer level
6270 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6271 if(lay->lesioned()) continue;
6272 lay->Compute_ApplyInhib(this);
6273 }
6274}

6287///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
6288// Cycle Stats
6289
6290void LeabraNetwork::Compute_CycleStats() {
6291 // stats are never threadable due to updating at higher levels
6292 output_name = ""; // this will be updated by layer
6293 maxda = 0.0f; // initialize
6294 trg_max_act = 0.0f;
6295 init_netins_cycle_stat = false;
6296
6297 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6298 if(lay->lesioned()) continue;
6299 lay->Compute_CycleStats(this);
6300 }
6301 if(init_netins_cycle_stat) {
6302 Init_Netins();
6303 }
6304}

6315}

6335}

; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =

; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =

6350
6351void LeabraNetwork::Settle_Compute_dWt() {
6352 if(train_mode == TEST)
6353 return;
6354
6355 switch(phase_order) {
6356 case MINUS_PLUS:
6357 case PLUS_MINUS:
6358 case PLUS_NOTHING:
6359 if(phase_no == 1) {
6360 Compute_dWt_FirstPlus();
6361 AdaptKWTAPt();
6362 }
6363 break;
6364 case PLUS_ONLY:
6365 Compute_dWt_FirstPlus();
6366 AdaptKWTAPt();
6367 break;
6368 case MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
6369 case MINUS_PLUS_MINUS:
6370 if(phase_no == 1)
6371 Compute_dWt_FirstPlus();
6372 else if(phase_no == 2) {
6373 Compute_dWt_Nothing();
6374 AdaptKWTAPt();
6375 }
6376 break;
6377 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS:
6378 if(phase_no == 1)
6379 Compute_dWt_FirstPlus();
6380 else if(phase_no == 2) {
6381 Compute_dWt_SecondPlus();
6382 AdaptKWTAPt();
6383 }
6384 break;
6385 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
6386 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_MINUS:
6387 if(phase_no == 1)
6388 Compute_dWt_FirstPlus();
6389 else if(phase_no == 2)
6390 Compute_dWt_SecondPlus();
6391 else if(phase_no == 3) {
6392 Compute_dWt_Nothing();
6393 AdaptKWTAPt();
6394 }
6395 break;
6396 }
6397}
6398
6399void LeabraNetwork::AdaptKWTAPt() {
6400 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6401 if(!lay->lesioned())
6402 lay->AdaptKWTAPt(this);
6403 }
6404}
6405
6406
6407///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
6408// Trial Update and Final
6409
6410void LeabraNetwork::Trial_UpdatePhase() {
6411 if(phase_no == phase_max) return; // done!
6412
6413 // this assumes that phase_no > 0 -- called after updating phase_no
6414 nothing_phase = false;
6415 bool no_plus_testing = false;
6416 if(no_plus_test && (train_mode == TEST)) {
6417 no_plus_testing = true;
6418 }
6419
6420 switch(phase_order) {
6421 case MINUS_PLUS:
6422 phase = PLUS_PHASE;
6423 break;
6424 case PLUS_MINUS:
6425 phase = MINUS_PHASE;
6426 break;
6427 case PLUS_ONLY:
6428 // nop
6429 break;
6430 case MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
6431 case MINUS_PLUS_MINUS:
6432 // diff between these two is in Settle_Init_Decay: TargExtToComp()
6433 if(phase_no == 1) {
6434 if(no_plus_testing)
6435 phase = MINUS_PHASE; // another minus
6436 else
6437 phase = PLUS_PHASE;
6438 }
6439 else {
6440 phase = MINUS_PHASE;
6441 nothing_phase = true;
6442 }
6443 break;
6444 case PLUS_NOTHING:
6445 phase = MINUS_PHASE;
6446 nothing_phase = true;
6447 break;
6448 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS:
6449 if(no_plus_testing)
6450 phase = MINUS_PHASE; // another minus
6451 else
6452 phase = PLUS_PHASE;
6453 break;
6454 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
6455 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_MINUS:
6456 // diff between these two is in Settle_Init_Decay: TargExtToComp()
6457 if(phase_no <= 2) {
6458 if(no_plus_testing)
6459 phase = MINUS_PHASE; // another minus
6460 else
6461 phase = PLUS_PHASE;
6462 }
6463 else {
6464 phase = MINUS_PHASE;
6465 nothing_phase = true;
6466 }
6467 break;
6468 }
6469}
6470
6471void LeabraNetwork::Trial_Final() {
6472 EncodeState();
6473 Compute_SelfReg_Trial();
6474}
6475
6476void LeabraNetwork::EncodeState() {
6477 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6478 if(!lay->lesioned())
6479 lay->EncodeState(this);
6480 }
6481}
6482
6483void LeabraNetwork::Compute_SelfReg_Trial() {
6484 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6485 if(!lay->lesioned())
6486 lay->Compute_SelfReg_Trial(this);
6487 }
6488}
