6490///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
6491// Learning
6492
6493bool LeabraNetwork::Compute_SRAvg_Now() {
6494 int eff_int = ct_sravg.interval;
6495 if(phase == LeabraNetwork::PLUS_PHASE && cycle >= ct_sravg.plus_s_st) {
6496 if((ct_time.plus - ct_sravg.plus_s_st) < eff_int) {
6497 eff_int = 1; // make sure you get short-time/plus phase info!
6498 }
6499 }
6500 if((ct_cycle >= ct_sravg.start) &&
6501 (ct_cycle < (ct_time.inhib_start + ct_sravg.end)) &&
6502 ((ct_cycle - ct_sravg.start) % eff_int == 0)) {
6503 return true;
6504 }
6505 return false;
6506}
6507
6508void LeabraNetwork::Compute_SRAvg() {
6509 if(!Compute_SRAvg_Now()) return;
6510
6511 if(phase == LeabraNetwork::PLUS_PHASE && cycle >= ct_sravg.plus_s_st)
6512 sravg_vals.do_s = true;
6513 else
6514 sravg_vals.do_s = false;
6515
6516 ThreadUnitCall un_call((ThreadUnitMethod)(LeabraUnitMethod)&LeabraUnit::Compute_SRAvg);
6517 if(thread_flags & SRAVG)
6518 threads.Run(&un_call, 0.9f);
6519 else
6520 threads.Run(&un_call, -1.0f); // -1 = always run localized
6521
6522 sravg_vals.m_sum += 1.0f; // normal weighting
6523 if(sravg_vals.do_s)
6524 sravg_vals.s_sum += 1.0f;
6525}
6526
6527void LeabraNetwork::Compute_dWt_SRAvg() {
6528 if(sravg_vals.m_sum > 0.0f)
6529 sravg_vals.m_nrm = 1.0f / sravg_vals.m_sum;
6530 else
6531 sravg_vals.m_nrm = 1.0f;
6532 if(sravg_vals.s_sum > 0.0f)
6533 sravg_vals.s_nrm = 1.0f / sravg_vals.s_sum;
6534 else
6535 sravg_vals.s_nrm = 1.0f;
6536}
6537
6538void LeabraNetwork::Compute_XCalC_dWt() {
6539 if(learn_rule != CTLEABRA_XCAL_C) return;
6540
6541 bool do_lrn = false;
6542
6543 float tmp_davg = 0.0f;
6544 for(int i=1; i<units_flat.size; i++) {
6545 LeabraUnit* un = (LeabraUnit*)units_flat[i];
6546 tmp_davg += fabsf(un->davg);
6547 }
6548 lrn_trig.davg = tmp_davg / (float)units_flat.size;
6549 lrn_trig.davg_s += ct_lrn_trig.davg_s_dt * (lrn_trig.davg - lrn_trig.davg_s);
6550 lrn_trig.davg_m += ct_lrn_trig.davg_m_dt * (lrn_trig.davg_s - lrn_trig.davg_m);
6551 float nw_smd = lrn_trig.davg_s - lrn_trig.davg_m;
6552 float d_smd = nw_smd - lrn_trig.davg_smd;
6553 lrn_trig.davg_smd = nw_smd;
6554
6555 lrn_trig.davg_l += ct_lrn_trig.davg_l_dt * (lrn_trig.davg_smd - lrn_trig.davg_l);
6556 if(lrn_trig.davg_smd >= lrn_trig.davg_max) {
6557 lrn_trig.davg_max = lrn_trig.davg_smd;
6558 }
6559 else {
6560 lrn_trig.davg_max += ct_lrn_trig.davg_l_dt * (lrn_trig.davg_l - lrn_trig.davg_max);
6561 }
6562
6563 if(d_smd > 0.0f) {
6564 lrn_trig.loc_max = lrn_trig.davg_smd; // indicate local max
6565 lrn_trig.cyc_fm_inc = 0;
6566 lrn_trig.cyc_fm_dec++;
6567 }
6568 else {
6569 lrn_trig.cyc_fm_dec = 0;
6570 lrn_trig.cyc_fm_inc++;
6571 }
6572
6573 float maxldif = lrn_trig.davg_max - lrn_trig.davg_l;
6574 float thr_min_eff = lrn_trig.davg_l + ct_lrn_trig.thr_min * maxldif;
6575 float thr_max_eff = lrn_trig.davg_l + ct_lrn_trig.thr_max * maxldif;
6576
6577 float loc_dec_norm = (lrn_trig.loc_max - lrn_trig.davg_smd) / maxldif;
6578
6579 if(lrn_trig.lrn_trig > 0.0f) { // already met thresh, counting up to learn time
6580 lrn_trig.lrn_trig += ct_lrn_trig.lrn_delay_inc;
6581 if(lrn_trig.lrn_trig >= 1.0f) {
6582 do_lrn = true;
6583 lrn_trig.lrn_trig = -1.0f; // begin refractory period
6584 }
6585 }
6586 else if(lrn_trig.lrn_trig < 0.0f) { // already learned, counting down to refract
6587 lrn_trig.lrn_trig += ct_lrn_trig.lrn_refract_inc;
6588 if(lrn_trig.lrn_trig >= 0.0f) {
6589 lrn_trig.lrn_trig = 0.0f; // reset -- eligible for learning again
6590 }
6591 }
6592 else if((lrn_trig.cyc_fm_dec == 0) && // going down
6593 (lrn_trig.cyc_fm_inc == ct_lrn_trig.loc_max_cyc) && // x amount from inc
6594 (loc_dec_norm >= ct_lrn_trig.loc_max_dec) && // x inc
6595 (lrn_trig.loc_max >= thr_min_eff && lrn_trig.loc_max <= thr_max_eff)) { // max in range
6596 lrn_trig.lrn_max = lrn_trig.loc_max;
6597 lrn_trig.lrn_trig = ct_lrn_trig.lrn_delay_inc; // start counting
6598 }
6599
6600 if(ct_lrn_trig.plus_lrn_cyc > 0) {
6601 // fake it override!
6602 do_lrn = (ct_cycle == (ct_time.minus + ct_lrn_trig.plus_lrn_cyc));
6603 }
6604
6605 if(do_lrn) {
6606 // this is all the std code from Compute_dWt_FirstPlus
6607 Compute_dWt_SRAvg();
6608 Compute_dWt_Layer_pre();
6609 lrn_trig.lrn = 1;
6610 ThreadUnitCall un_call((ThreadUnitMethod)(LeabraUnitMethod)&LeabraUnit::Compute_dWt_FirstPlus);
6611 if(thread_flags & DWT)
6612 threads.Run(&un_call, 0.6f);
6613 else
6614 threads.Run(&un_call, -1.0f); // -1 = always run localized
6615
6616 Compute_dWt_Norm();
6617
6618 lrn_trig.lrn_stats_n++;
6619 if(phase_no == 0) {
6620 lrn_trig.lrn_min_sum += 1.0f;
6621 lrn_trig.lrn_min_cyc_sum += cycle;
6622 lrn_trig.lrn_min_thr_sum += lrn_trig.lrn_max;
6623 }
6624 else if(phase_no == 1) {
6625 lrn_trig.lrn_plus_sum += 1.0f;
6626 lrn_trig.lrn_plus_cyc_sum += cycle;
6627 lrn_trig.lrn_plus_thr_sum += lrn_trig.lrn_max;
6628 }
6629 else {
6630 lrn_trig.lrn_noth_sum += 1.0f;
6631 lrn_trig.lrn_noth_cyc_sum += cycle;
6632 lrn_trig.lrn_noth_thr_sum += lrn_trig.lrn_max;
6633 }
6634 }
6635 else {
6636 lrn_trig.lrn = 0;
6637 }
6638}
6639
6640void LeabraNetwork::Compute_dWt_Layer_pre() {
6641 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6642 if(lay->lesioned()) continue;
6643 lay->Compute_dWt_Layer_pre(this);
6644 }
6645}
6646
6647void LeabraNetwork::Compute_dWt_FirstPlus() {
6648 if(learn_rule == CTLEABRA_XCAL_C) return; // done separately
6649 if(learn_rule == LeabraNetwork::CTLEABRA_XCAL && epoch < ct_time.n_avg_only_epcs) {
6650 return; // no learning while gathering data!
6651 }
6652 Compute_dWt_SRAvg();
6653 Compute_dWt_Layer_pre();
6654 ThreadUnitCall un_call((ThreadUnitMethod)(LeabraUnitMethod)&LeabraUnit::Compute_dWt_FirstPlus);
6655 if(thread_flags & DWT)
6656 threads.Run(&un_call, 0.6f);
6657 else
6658 threads.Run(&un_call, -1.0f); // -1 = always run localized
6659 Compute_dWt_Norm();
6660}

6668 Compute_dWt_Layer_pre();

6672 else

6677void LeabraNetwork::Compute_dWt_Nothing() {

6685 if(thread_flags & DWT)

6687 else

6698 if(thread_flags & DWT)
6699 threads.Run(&un_call, 0.6f);
6700 else
6701 threads.Run(&un_call, -1.0f); // -1 = always run localized
6702}

6710}

6716void LeabraNetwork::Compute_ExtRew() {
6717 // assumes any ext rew computation has happened before this point, and set the
6718 // network ext_rew and ext_rew_avail flags appropriately
6719 if(ext_rew_avail) {
6720 avg_ext_rew_sum += ext_rew;
6721 avg_ext_rew_n++;
6722 }
6723}
6724
6725void LeabraNetwork::Compute_NormErr() {
6726 float nerr_sum = 0.0f;
6727 float nerr_avail = 0.0f;
6728 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6729 if(lay->lesioned()) continue;
6730 float nerr = lay->Compute_NormErr(this);
6731 if(nerr >= 0.0f) {
6732 nerr_avail += 1.0f;
6733 nerr_sum += nerr;
6734 }
6735 }
6736 if(nerr_avail > 0.0f) {
6737 norm_err = nerr_sum / nerr_avail; // normalize contribution across layers
6738
6739 avg_norm_err_sum += norm_err;
6740 avg_norm_err_n++;
6741 }
6742 else {
6743 norm_err = 0.0f;
6744 }
6745}
6746
6747float LeabraNetwork::Compute_M2SSE(bool unit_avg, bool sqrt) {
6748 float sse = 0.0f;
6749 int n_vals = 0;
6750 int lay_vals = 0;
6751 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, l, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *l = (
LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); l; l = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6752 if(l->lesioned()) continue;
6753 sse += l->Compute_M2SSE(this, lay_vals);
6754 n_vals += lay_vals;
6755 }
6756 if(unit_avg && n_vals > 0)
6757 sse /= (float)n_vals;
6758 if(sqrt)
6759 sse = sqrtf(sse);
6760 return sse;
6761}
6762
6763float LeabraNetwork::Compute_M2SSE_Recon(bool unit_avg, bool sqrt) {
6764 float sse = 0.0f;
6765 int n_vals = 0;
6766 int lay_vals = 0;
6767 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, l, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *l = (
LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); l; l = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6768 if(l->lesioned() || l->layer_type != Layer::INPUT) continue;
6769 sse += l->Compute_M2SSE(this, lay_vals);
6770 n_vals += lay_vals;
6771 }
6772 if(unit_avg && n_vals > 0)
6773 sse /= (float)n_vals;
6774 if(sqrt)
6775 sse = sqrtf(sse);
6776 return sse;
6777}
6778
6779float LeabraNetwork::Compute_CosErr() {
6780 float cosv = 0.0f;
6781 int n_lays = 0;
6782 int lay_vals = 0;
6783 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, l, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *l = (
LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); l; l = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6784 if(l->lesioned()) continue;
6785 cosv += l->Compute_CosErr(this, lay_vals);
6786 if(lay_vals > 0)
6787 n_lays++;
6788 }
6789 if(n_lays > 0)
6790 cosv /= (float)n_lays;
6791 return cosv;
6792}
6793
6794float LeabraNetwork::Compute_M2CosErr() {
6795 float cosv = 0.0f;
6796 int n_lays = 0;
6797 int lay_vals = 0;
6798 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, l, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *l = (
LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); l; l = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6799 if(l->lesioned()) continue;
6800 cosv += l->Compute_M2CosErr(this, lay_vals);
6801 if(lay_vals > 0)
6802 n_lays++;
6803 }
6804 if(n_lays > 0)
6805 cosv /= (float)n_lays;
6806 return cosv;
6807}
6808
6809float LeabraNetwork::Compute_M2CosErr_Recon() {
6810 float cosv = 0.0f;
6811 int n_lays = 0;
6812 int lay_vals = 0;
6813 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, l, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *l = (
LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); l; l = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6814 if(l->lesioned() || l->layer_type != Layer::INPUT) continue;
6815 cosv += l->Compute_M2CosErr(this, lay_vals);
6816 if(lay_vals > 0)
6817 n_lays++;
6818 }
6819 if(n_lays > 0)
6820 cosv /= (float)n_lays;
6821 return cosv;
6822}
6823
6824float LeabraNetwork::Compute_CosDiff() {
6825 float cosv = 0.0f;
6826 int n_lays = 0;
6827 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, l, layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *l = (
LeabraLayer*) (layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); l; l = (LeabraLayer
*) (layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6828 if(l->lesioned()) continue;
6829 cosv += l->Compute_CosDiff(this);
6830 n_lays++;
6831 }
6832 if(n_lays > 0)
6833 cosv /= (float)n_lays;
6834 return cosv;
6835}

6849
6850void LeabraNetwork::Compute_MinusCycles() {
6851 minus_cycles = cycle;
6852 avg_cycles_sum += minus_cycles;
6853 avg_cycles_n++;
6854}
6855
6856bool LeabraNetwork::Compute_TrialStats_Test() {
6857 bool is_time = false;
6858
6859 bool no_plus_testing = false;
6860 if(no_plus_test && (train_mode == TEST)) {
6861 no_plus_testing = true;
6862 }
6863
6864 switch(phase_order) {
6865 case MINUS_PLUS:
6866 if(phase_no == 0) is_time = true;
6867 break;
6868 case PLUS_MINUS:
6869 if(no_plus_testing)
6870 is_time = true;
6871 else {
6872 if(phase_no == 1) is_time = true;
6873 }
6874 break;
6875 case PLUS_ONLY:
6876 is_time = true;
6877 break;
6878 case MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
6879 case MINUS_PLUS_MINUS:
6880 if(no_plus_testing) {
6881 if(phase_no == 1) is_time = true;
6882 }
6883 else {
6884 if(phase_no == 0) is_time = true;
6885 }
6886 break;
6887 case PLUS_NOTHING:
6888 if(phase_no == 1) is_time = true;
6889 break;
6890 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS:
6891 if(phase_no == 0) is_time = true;
6892 break;
6893 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
6894 case MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_MINUS:
6895 if(phase_no == 0) is_time = true;
6896 break;
6897 }
6898
6899 return is_time;
6900}

6904 Compute_NormErr();
6905 Compute_MinusCycles();
6906 minus_output_name = output_name; // grab and hold..
6907}

6944void LeabraNetwork::Compute_AvgCycles() {
6945 if(avg_cycles_n > 0) {
6946 avg_cycles = avg_cycles_sum / (float)avg_cycles_n;
6947 }
6948 avg_cycles_sum = 0.0f;
6949 avg_cycles_n = 0;
6950}

6952void LeabraNetwork::Compute_AvgSendPct() {
6953 if(avg_send_pct_n > 0) {
6954 avg_send_pct = avg_send_pct_sum / (float)avg_send_pct_n;
6955 }
6956 avg_send_pct_sum = 0.0f;
6957 avg_send_pct_n = 0;
6958}
6959
6960void LeabraNetwork::Compute_AvgExtRew() {
6961 if(avg_ext_rew_n > 0) {
6962 avg_ext_rew = avg_ext_rew_sum / (float)avg_ext_rew_n;
6963 }
6964 avg_ext_rew_sum = 0.0f;
6965 avg_ext_rew_n = 0;
6966}
6967
6968void LeabraNetwork::Compute_AvgNormErr() {
6969 if(avg_norm_err_n > 0) {
6970 avg_norm_err = avg_norm_err_sum / (float)avg_norm_err_n;
6971 }
6972 avg_norm_err_sum = 0.0f;
6973 avg_norm_err_n = 0;
6974}
6975
6976void LeabraNetwork::Compute_CtLrnTrigAvgs() {
6977 if(lrn_trig.lrn_stats_n > 0) {
6978 float ltrign = (float)lrn_trig.lrn_stats_n;
6979 if(lrn_trig.lrn_min_sum > 0.0f) {
6980 lrn_trig.lrn_min_cyc = lrn_trig.lrn_min_cyc_sum / lrn_trig.lrn_min_sum;
6981 lrn_trig.lrn_min_thr = lrn_trig.lrn_min_thr_sum / lrn_trig.lrn_min_sum;
6982 }
6983 else {
6984 lrn_trig.lrn_min_cyc = 0.0f;
6985 lrn_trig.lrn_min_thr = 0.0f;
6986 }
6987 lrn_trig.lrn_min = lrn_trig.lrn_min_sum / ltrign;
6988
6989 if(lrn_trig.lrn_plus_sum > 0.0f) {
6990 lrn_trig.lrn_plus_cyc = lrn_trig.lrn_plus_cyc_sum / lrn_trig.lrn_plus_sum;
6991 lrn_trig.lrn_plus_thr = lrn_trig.lrn_plus_thr_sum / lrn_trig.lrn_plus_sum;
6992 }
6993 else {
6994 lrn_trig.lrn_plus_cyc = 0.0f;
6995 lrn_trig.lrn_plus_thr = 0.0f;
6996 }
6997 lrn_trig.lrn_plus = lrn_trig.lrn_plus_sum / ltrign;
6998
6999 if(lrn_trig.lrn_noth_sum > 0.0f) {
7000 lrn_trig.lrn_noth_cyc = lrn_trig.lrn_noth_cyc_sum / lrn_trig.lrn_noth_sum;
7001 lrn_trig.lrn_noth_thr = lrn_trig.lrn_noth_thr_sum / lrn_trig.lrn_noth_sum;
7002 }
7003 else {
7004 lrn_trig.lrn_noth_cyc = 0.0f;
7005 lrn_trig.lrn_noth_thr = 0.0f;
7006 }
7007 lrn_trig.lrn_noth = lrn_trig.lrn_noth_sum / ltrign;
7008 }
7009 lrn_trig.Init_Stats_Sums();
7010}
7011
7012void LeabraNetwork::Compute_EpochStats() {
7013 inherited::Compute_EpochStats();
7014 Compute_AvgCycles();
7015 Compute_AvgNormErr();
7016 Compute_AvgExtRew();
7017 Compute_AvgSendPct();
7018 Compute_CtLrnTrigAvgs();
7019}

7038
7039StringtaString LeabraWizard::RenderWizDoc_network() {
7040 StringtaString rval = inherited::RenderWizDoc_network();
7041 rval += StringtaString("\
7042* [[<this>.SRNContext()|SRN Context]] -- configure a network with a simple-recurrent-network (SRN) context layer\n\
7043* [[<this>.UnitInhib()|Unit Inhib]] -- configure unit-based inhibition for all layers in selected network (as compared with standard kWTA inhibition) ('''NOTE: parameters are out of date''').\n\
7044* [[<this>.Hippo()|Hippo]] -- configure a Hippocampus using quad-phase specs -- high functioning hippocampal episodic memory system.\n\
7045* [[<this>.TD()|Temporal Differences (TD)]] -- configure temporal-differences (TD) reinforcement learning layers.\n\
7046* [[<this>.PVLV()|PVLV]] -- configure PVLV (Primary Value, Learned Value) biologically-motivated reinforcement learning layers -- provides a simulated dopamine signal that reflects unexpected primary rewards (PV = primary value system) and unexpected learned reward assocations (conditioned stimuli; LV = learned value = system).\n\
7047:* [[<this>.PVLV_ConnectLayer()|PVLV Connect Layer]] -- connect or disconnect a layer as an input to the PVLV system -- multiple PVLV layers should be connected together so this automates that process and is strongly recommended.\n\
7048:* [[<this>.PVLV_OutToPVe()|PVLV Connect Output to PVe]] -- connect or disconnect an Output layer to the PVe (primary value, excitatory) layer, which then computes reward based on network success in producing target outputs.\n\
7049* [[<this>.PBWM()|PBWM]] -- create and configure prefrontal cortex basal ganglia working memory (PBWM) layers in the network -- also does a PVLV configuration, which does the reinforcement learning for PBWM.\n\
7050:* [[<this>.PBWM_Defaults()|PBWM Defaults]] -- set the parameters in the specs of the network to the latest default values for the PBWM model, and also ensures that the standard select edits are built and contain relevant parameters -- this is only for a model that already has PBWM configured and in a standard current format (i.e., everything in groups).\n\
7051:* [[<this>.PBWM_SetNStripes()|PBWM Set N Stripes]] -- set the number of stripes (unit groups) throughout the set of PFC and BG layers that have stripes -- easier than doing it manually for each layer.\n\
7052:* [[<this>.PBWM_Remove()|PBWM Remove]] -- Remove PBWM layers and specs from a network -- can be useful for converting between PBWM versions -- ONLY works when layers are organized into groups.\n\
7053");
7054 return rval;
7055}

7057bool LeabraWizard::StdNetwork() {
7058 ProjectBase* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(ProjectBase)(ProjectBase *) GetOwner(&TA_ProjectBase);
7059 if(proj->networks.size == 0) { // make a new one for starters always
7060 LeabraNetwork* net = (LeabraNetwork*)proj->networks.New(1);
7061 if(net)
7062 StdLayerSpecs(net);
7063 }
7064 bool rval = std_net_dlg.DoDialog();
7065 return rval;
7066}
7067
7068bool LeabraWizard::StdLayerSpecs(LeabraNetwork* net) {
7069 if(!net) {
7070 LeabraProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(LeabraProject)(LeabraProject *) GetOwner(&TA_LeabraProject);
7071 net = (LeabraNetwork*)proj->GetNewNetwork();
7072 if(TestError(!net, "StdLayerSpecs", "network is NULL and could not make a new one -- aborting!")) return false;
7073 }
7074 LeabraLayerSpec* hid;
7075 hid = (LeabraLayerSpec*)net->FindMakeSpec("", &TA_LeabraLayerSpec);
7076 hid->name = "HiddenLayer";
7077 LeabraLayerSpec* inout;
7078 inout = (LeabraLayerSpec*)hid->children.FindMakeSpec("Input_Output", &TA_LeabraLayerSpec);
7079 hid->inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_AVG_INHIB;
7080 hid->inhib.kwta_pt = .6f;
7081 inout->SetUnique("inhib", true);
7082 inout->SetUnique("kwta", true);
7083 inout->inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_INHIB;
7084 inout->inhib.kwta_pt = .25f;
7085 inout->kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_PAT_K;
7086
7087 // move the bias spec under the con spec
7088 LeabraBiasSpec* bs;
7089 bs = (LeabraBiasSpec*)net->specs.FindType(&TA_LeabraBiasSpec);
7090 if(bs != NULL__null) {
7091 LeabraConSpec* ps = (LeabraConSpec*)bs->FindParent();
7092 if(ps != NULL__null) return false;
7093 ps = (LeabraConSpec*)net->specs.FindSpecTypeNotMe(&TA_LeabraConSpec, bs);
7094 if(ps != NULL__null) {
7095 ps->children.Transfer(bs);
7096 }
7097 }
7098 return true;
7099}
7100
7101///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
7102// Unit Inhib
7103///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
7104
7105bool LeabraWizard::UnitInhib(LeabraNetwork* net, int n_inhib_units) {
7106 LeabraProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(LeabraProject)(LeabraProject *) GetOwner(&TA_LeabraProject);
7107 if(!net) {
7108 net = (LeabraNetwork*)proj->GetNewNetwork();
7109 if(TestError(!net, "UnitInhib", "network is NULL and could not make a new one -- aborting!")) return false;
7110 }
7111
7112 net->RemoveUnits();
7113
7114 LeabraUnitSpec* basic_us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)net->FindSpecType(&TA_LeabraUnitSpec);
7115 if(TestError(!basic_us, "UnitInhib", "basic LeabraUnitSpec not found, bailing!")) {
7116 return false;
7117 }
7118 LeabraUnitSpec* inhib_us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)basic_us->children.FindMakeSpec("InhibUnits", &TA_LeabraUnitSpec);
7119
7120 LeabraConSpec* basic_cs = (LeabraConSpec*)net->FindSpecType(&TA_LeabraConSpec);
7121 if(TestError(!basic_cs, "UnitInhib", "basic LeabraConSpec not found, bailing!")) {
7122 return false;
7123 }
7124 LeabraConSpec* inhib_cs = (LeabraConSpec*)basic_cs->children.FindMakeSpec("InhibCons", &TA_LeabraConSpec);
7125
7126 LeabraConSpec* fb_inhib_cs = (LeabraConSpec*)basic_cs->children.FindMakeSpec("FBtoInhib", &TA_LeabraConSpec);
7127 LeabraConSpec* ff_inhib_cs = (LeabraConSpec*)fb_inhib_cs->children.FindMakeSpec("FFtoInhib", &TA_LeabraConSpec);
7128
7129 LeabraLayerSpec* basic_ls = (LeabraLayerSpec*)net->FindSpecType(&TA_LeabraLayerSpec);
7130 if(TestError(!basic_ls, "UnitInhib", "basic LeabraLayerSpec not found, bailing!")) {
7131 return false;
7132 }
7133 LeabraLayerSpec* inhib_ls = (LeabraLayerSpec*)basic_ls->children.FindMakeSpec("InhibLayers", &TA_LeabraLayerSpec);
7134
7135 FullPrjnSpec* fullprjn = (FullPrjnSpec*)net->FindSpecType(&TA_FullPrjnSpec);
7136 if(TestError(!fullprjn, "UnitInhib", "basic FullPrjnSpec not found, bailing!")) {
7137 return false;
7138 }
7139
7140 // todo: optimize these params..
7141 basic_us->dt.vm = .04f;
7142 basic_us->g_bar.i = 10.0f;
7143 inhib_us->SetUnique("dt", true);
7144 inhib_us->dt.vm = .07f;
7145
7146 inhib_cs->SetUnique("rnd", true);
7147 inhib_cs->rnd.mean = 1.0f; inhib_cs->rnd.var = 0.0f;
7148 inhib_cs->SetUnique("wt_limits", true);
7149 inhib_cs->wt_limits.sym = false;
7150 inhib_cs->SetUnique("inhib", true);
7151 inhib_cs->inhib = true;
7152
7153 fb_inhib_cs->SetUnique("wt_limits", true);
7154 fb_inhib_cs->wt_limits.sym = false;
7155 fb_inhib_cs->SetUnique("rnd", true);
7156 fb_inhib_cs->rnd.mean = .5f; fb_inhib_cs->rnd.var = 0.05f;
7157 fb_inhib_cs->SetUnique("lrate", true);
7158 fb_inhib_cs->lrate = 0.0f;
7159
7160 // todo: optimize
7161 ff_inhib_cs->SetUnique("wt_scale", true);
7162 ff_inhib_cs->wt_scale.abs = .4f;
7163
7164 basic_ls->inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::UNIT_INHIB;
7165 basic_ls->adapt_i.type = AdaptISpec::G_BAR_I;
7166 basic_ls->adapt_i.tol = .02f; // these params sometimes get off..
7167 basic_ls->adapt_i.p_dt = .1f;
7168
7169 inhib_ls->SetUnique("kwta", true);
7170 inhib_ls->kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_PCT;
7171 inhib_ls->kwta.pct = .34f;
7172
7173 basic_us->UpdateAfterEdit();
7174 basic_cs->UpdateAfterEdit();
7175 basic_ls->UpdateAfterEdit();
7176
7177 int i;
7178 for(i=0;i<net->layers.size;i++) {
7179 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)net->layers[i];
7180 if(lay->layer_type == Layer::INPUT) continue;
7181 StringtaString nm = lay->name;
7182 nm.downcase();
7183 if(nm.contains("_inhib")) continue;
7184
7185 StringtaString inm = lay->name + "_Inhib";
7186 LeabraLayer* ilay = (LeabraLayer*)net->layers.FindName(inm);
7187 if(ilay == NULL__null) {
7188 ilay = (LeabraLayer*)net->layers.NewEl(1);
7189 ilay->name = inm;
7190 ilay->pos.z = lay->pos.z;
7191 ilay->pos.x = lay->pos.x + lay->disp_geom.x + 1;
7192 ilay->un_geom.n = n_inhib_units;
7193 if(n_inhib_units <= 20) {
7194 ilay->un_geom.x = 2; ilay->un_geom.y = n_inhib_units / 2;
7195 while(ilay->un_geom.x * ilay->un_geom.y < n_inhib_units) ilay->un_geom.y++;
7196 }
7197 else if(n_inhib_units <= 40) {
7198 ilay->un_geom.x = 4; ilay->un_geom.y = n_inhib_units / 4;
7199 while(ilay->un_geom.x * ilay->un_geom.y < n_inhib_units) ilay->un_geom.y++;
7200 }
7201 }
7202 ilay->SetLayerSpec(inhib_ls);
7203 ilay->SetUnitSpec(inhib_us);
7204
7205 int j;
7206 for(j=0;j<lay->projections.size;j++) {
7207 LeabraLayer* fmlay = (LeabraLayer*)((Projection*)lay->projections[j])->from.ptr();
7208 if(fmlay->name.contains("_Inhib")) continue;
7209 if(fmlay == lay) continue;
7210 net->FindMakePrjn(ilay, fmlay, fullprjn, ff_inhib_cs);
7211 }
7212 net->FindMakePrjn(ilay, lay, fullprjn, fb_inhib_cs);
7213 net->FindMakePrjn(lay, ilay, fullprjn, inhib_cs);
7214 net->FindMakePrjn(ilay, ilay, fullprjn, inhib_cs);
7215 }
7216
7217 net->UpdateAfterEdit();
7218 // todo:
7219// net->InitAllViews();
7220
7221 // todo: !!!
7222// winbMisc::DelayedMenuUpdate(net);
7223
7224 // set settle cycles to 300
7225 net->cycle_max = 300;
7226 net->min_cycles = 150;
7227
7228 SelectEdit* edit = proj->FindMakeSelectEdit("UnitInhib");
7229 if(edit != NULL__null) {
7230 basic_us->SelectForEditNm("dt", edit, "excite");
7231 inhib_us->SelectForEditNm("dt", edit, "inhib");
7232 basic_us->SelectForEditNm("g_bar", edit, "excite");
7233 ff_inhib_cs->SelectForEditNm("wt_scale", edit, "ff_inhib");
7234 fb_inhib_cs->SelectForEditNm("rnd", edit, "to_inhib");
7235 inhib_cs->SelectForEditNm("rnd", edit, "fm_inhib");
7236 basic_ls->SelectForEditNm("adapt_i", edit, "layers");
7237
7238 net->SelectForEditNm("cycle_max", edit, net->name);
7239 net->SelectForEditNm("min_cycles", edit, net->name);
7240 }
7241
7242 if(proj) {
7243 proj->undo_mgr.SaveUndo(net, "Wizard::UnitInhib -- actually saves network specifically");
7244 }
7245 return true;
7246}

7261
